Welsh AMwo le nu xam ɖe “ale si woadze abe abunekeviwo ene la ŋu”
Dzimaɖitsitsi aɖe le AM aɖewo me ɖe susu si wodo ɖa be woƒe ɖoƒewo natrɔ azu MWPwo (Welsh Sewɔtakpekpemenɔla) la ŋu.
Esia do mo ɖa ɖe ɖoɖo si wowɔ be woatrɔ ƒuƒoƒea wòazu Welsh Sewɔtakpeƒea la ŋu.
AM siwo katã le dunyahehe ƒe ɖoƒewo la le nu xam be esia ahe vlodoame vɛ.
AM ɖeka si nye Dɔwɔwɔnyawo dzikpɔla la gblɔ be yeƒe habɔbɔ bu be “esia sɔ kple Twp kplePwp”
Na nuxlẽla siwo le Wales: Le Welsh la, twp gɔmee nye movidzɔdzɔ eye pwp gɔmee nye mi.
Plaid AM aɖe gblɔ be habɔbɔ blibo la katã “mekpɔ dzidzɔ o” eye wodo susu bubu aɖewo ɖa.
Welsh Ɖokuigomeku Dunyahela aɖe gblɔ be yeƒe habɔbɔ la ƒe “susu le te” ɖe tɔtrɔ ŋu, gake hegade dzesii be enye dzodzo tso MWP me ayi ɖe Abunekevinyenye me.
Le afi sia la, woyɔa Welsh ƒe ŋɔŋlɔdzesi w abe ale si woyɔa Iŋlisi Yorkshire ƒe ŋɔŋlɔdzesi u la ene.
Ƒuƒoƒea ƒe Dɔwɔha, si le se la ŋlɔm hena ŋkɔa tɔtrɔ la, gblɔ be: "Ɖoɖo mamlea si ku ɖe ale si woayɔ Ƒuƒoƒemenɔlawoe la anye woawo ŋutɔwo ƒe nya godoo."
Wales Dziɖuɖua ƒe Se 2017 na ŋusẽ Welsh Ƒuƒoƒea be wòatrɔ eƒe ŋkɔ.
Le Masa me la, Dɔwɔha la ɖe nutsotso aɖe ɖe go ku ɖe ale si wobia gbe ame geɖewo ku ɖe susu la ŋu si ɖee fia be ame geɖewo da asi ɖe edzi be woayɔ Ƒuƒoƒe la be Welsh Sewɔtakpeƒe.
Ku ɖe AM ɖoƒedzesia ŋu la, Dɔwɔha la da asi ɖe Welsh Sewɔtakpekpemenɔlawo dzi WMPwo dzi, gake MWP la boŋ dzi ame geɖewo da asi ɖo esime wobia gbe wo.
AMwo le biabiam ko be woalé ŋku ɖe mɔnu bubu aɖewo ŋu, gake asidada ɖe nya ɖeka aɖe dzi azu taɖu na Habɔbɔnunɔla, Elin Jones, ame si wole mɔ kpɔm na be wòatsɔ se si woŋlɔ ku ɖe tɔtrɔa ŋu la ana le kɔsiɖa ʋɛ aɖewo me.
Se si ku ɖe tɔtrɔawo ŋu la alɔ tɔtrɔ bubu siwo ku ɖe ale si ƒuƒoƒea wɔa dɔe, kpe ɖe se siwo ku ɖe asimadamada ɖe AMwo dzi kple Dɔwɔha la ƒe ɖoɖowo ŋu.
AMwo ada akɔ ɖe ale si woayɔ woe la dzi nenye be ɣeyiɣi la de woahe glãkɛ le eŋu.
Makedoniatɔwo da akɔ hena asidada ɖe edzi be woatrɔ dukɔ la ƒe ŋkɔ
Akɔdalawo ada akɔ le Kɔsiɖagbe ahade dzesii nenye be anyo alo manyo be woatrɔ dukɔa ƒe ŋkɔ wòazu “Makedonia Anyiehe Dziɖuɖu" o mahã.
Wode akɔdada wɔna gã sia to me bena woatsɔ aɖe masɔmasɔ xoxo aɖe si le dukɔa kple Greece dukɔ, si ƒe nuto aɖe hã nye Makedonia la dome.
Atenia hã te gbe ɖe edzi be yeƒe anyiehe aƒelika la ƒe nye yeƒe anyigba ƒe akpa aɖe xɔxɔ eye wòtsia tsitre ɖe EU kple NATO ƒe hamevinyenye ŋu ɣe sia ɣi.
Makedonia dukplɔla Gjorge Ivanov, ame si tsi tsitre ɖe tiatiawɔwɔ kɔdada sia ŋu hena ŋkɔ tɔtrɔ la, gblɔ be yemaɖo kɔ akɔdada la ŋu o.
Ke, ame siwo da asi ɖe tɔtrɔwɔwɔ kɔdada sia dzi, abe Dudɔlagã Zoran Zaev ene la, he nya le eŋu be ŋkɔtɔtrɔ la nye vɔsã si woawɔ hena gege ɖe EU kple NATO hawo me.
St. Martin's ƒe Gawo Zi Ɖoɖoe Eye Hame Siwo Le Harlem la Ge Ɖe Ʋiʋli Aɖe Me
Aƒetɔ Adam gblɔ be, “Ame tsitsi siwo meƒo nu kpli la gblɔ be, tsã la, ahanoƒe kple hame le dzogoe ɖe sia ɖe dzi.
"Egbe la, wo dometɔ aɖeke megali o."
Egblɔ be ahanoƒewo bubu ya me kɔ.
Egblɔ be, “Le egbe me la, amewo bɔa ha le mɔ geɖewo nu”.
"Ahanoƒewo megale abe aƒelikawo be akpata me, afi si amewo yina edziedzi la ene o."
Le hamewo ya gome la, exa nu be hamea ƒe nunɔamesi siwo wodzra la ƒe ga manɔ anyi wòadi be ale si kplɔlawo bui la ene o, “eye madidi o la, woagatrɔ ayi ɖoƒe gbãtɔ si wonɔ la."
Egblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu be, woate ŋu aɖo xɔ siwo me ame siwo makpe ɖe nutoa ŋu wòanɔ dzɔdzɔe o la anyi ɖe hamewo teƒe .
Egblɔ be, "Ame akpa gãtɔ siwo aƒle xɔ siawo la anye yevuwo, eye awɔe be ŋkeke si dzi woatu hameawo la natsɔ elabena kakaɖedzi aɖeke meli be ame siwo anɔ xɔ siawo me la anye hame siawo me tɔwo o."
Sɔlemedela siwo nye yevuwo lae tu hame eveawo siaa hafi Harlem va zu ameyibɔwo nɔƒe - Ameha Geɖewo Nɔƒe le 1870 me, St. Martin’s le ƒe ewo megbe.
Methodist yevu sɔlemedela siwo ɖo hamea anyi do le xɔ la me le 1930 me lɔƒo.
Ameyibɔ sɔlemedela siwo hã nɔ subɔsubɔm le gbedoxɔa gbɔ lɔƒo la va xɔ xɔ la wɔ wo tɔe.
Ameyibɔ sɔlemedelawo va xɔ St. Martin nu le Osɔfo John Howard Johnson, ame si nɔ ŋgɔ na amewo wogbe be yewomagaƒle nu na ƒlekaƒlitɔwo le Ablɔ 125lia dzi o, ablɔ vevi si dzi woƒlea nuwo lena le Harlem, ɖe ale si wogbe be yewomaxɔ ameyibɔviwo alo ado wo ɖe ŋgɔ o la ta.
Dzo aɖe si dze xɔa le 1939 me la, gblẽ nu le eŋu ŋutɔ, ke esi wònye be Fada Johnson ƒe hamea me nɔlawo wɔ ɖoɖo bena yewoagbugbɔe atui la, woʋu saŋku la nu.
Osɔfo David Johnson, Fada Johnson ƒe viŋutuvi kple ame si ve xɔ ɖe eteƒe le St. Martin la yɔ saŋku la be “ame dahewo ƒe ga."
Saŋkuƒolagã si ƒo saŋkua le Siamlɔm me la yɔ ŋkɔ bubu aɖe nɛ: "Dekɔnu ƒe nuxɔasi” kple “nudɔwɔnu xoxo si womate ŋu aɖɔli o."
Dɔnyalagã Tiffany Ng tso Michigan Yunivɛsitia me la hã de dzesii be eyae nye saŋku gbãtɔ si ameyibɔ hakpala, Dionisio A. Lind, ame si ʋu yi ɖe saŋku gãtɔ la gbɔ le Riverside Hamea me ƒe wuienyi siwo va yi la ƒo.
Aƒetɔ Merriweather gblɔ be St. Martin meda ame bubu ɖe eteƒe o.
Nu siwo dzɔ le St. Martin le ɣleti ʋɛ siwo va yi me la nye nya sesẽ aɖe si ku ɖe xɔtalawo kple xɔtulawo ŋu, wo dometɔ aɖewo va to nunɔlavi siwo le haa nu la dzi, eye bubuawo hã va to Hanunɔlagã ƒe tanɔƒe.
Vestry - sɔlimea ƒe dziɖula, sime ngɔnɔla wp le - ŋlɔ nuto la le Siamlɔm me kple dzitsitsi be nutoa “adi be yea kɔ efe si le na” vestry la, togbɔbe vestry la mele eme hafi wo he ehɔtala ve o kple dɔwɔla si nuto la kplɔ ve o.
Sɔlemedela aɖewo he nya vevie le tanɔƒea ƒe ameŋkumekpɔkpɔ ŋu.
Anamu de abi ƒe wuietɔ̃ ŋutsũvi aɖe ŋu
Ƒuta dɔwɔlawo gblɔ be anamu aɖe lé ƒe wuietɔ̃ ŋutsuvi aɖe eye wòde abi eŋu le California le Memliɖagbe esime wònɔ ɖi dom be yealé bɔlu le bɔluɖeŋɔli la ƒe gɔmedzedze.
Afɔku sia dzɔ le ŋdi 7 me lɔƒo te ɖe Beacon Ƒuta si le Encinitas la ŋu.
Chad Hammel gblɔ na KSWB-TV le San Diego be yenɔ ɖi dom kple ye tɔwo le Memliɖagbe ŋdi abe miniti blaetɔ̃ lɔƒo ene hafi se ŋutsuvi la ƒe ɣlidodo bena woaxɔ na ye eye ye kple amehatsotso aɖewo yewoku ʋu yi ɖe egbɔ ɖaɖee do goe le tsi la me.
Hammel gblɔ be teti la, yebu be bɔlu ko wòlé nɔ dzidzɔ kpɔ nenema, ke “yede dzesii be enɔ ɣli dom be, ‘Nane ɖum!
Nane ɖum!'
Hammel kpɔe be eƒe akɔtaƒu la katã ho le eme, esime wòte ɖe eŋu".
Hammel gblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu be, "Medo ɣli ɖe ame sia ame ta be woado go le tsia me: 'Anamu aɖe le tsia me!'"
Wokɔ ŋutsuvi la kple yameʋu yi ɖe Randy ƒe Ɖeviwo ƒe Dɔyɔƒe si le San Diego la me eye wode dzesii be nu la sesẽ nɛ.
Womenya anamu si ƒomevi wɔ dɔ sia o.
Agbetakpɔla Capt. Larry Giles gblɔ na nyadzɔdzɔdɔwɔlawo be wokpɔ anamu aɖe le tsia me kɔsiɖa aɖewo va yi gake wobu be menye anamu si ƒomevi awɔ nu vevi ame la dometɔ aɖekee o.
Giles gblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu be ŋutsuvi la xɔ abi vevie le eƒe kɔƒu gbɔ.
Dɔwɔlawo de se ɖe Ponto Ƒuta si le Casablad va se ɖe Swami si le Ecinitas la yiyi ŋu gaƒoƒo 48 hena nugɔmekuku kple dedienɔnɔ.
Giles de dzesii be anamu ƒomevi vovovo 135 kple edzivɔwoe le afi ma, gake wo dometɔ geɖewo menye nuveviwɔametɔwo o.
Sainsbury ƒe ɖoɖowo si wo kɔ yi UK ƒe atsyɔ̃ sime
Sainsbury Boots teƒe ɖom, Superdrug kple Debenhams si atsɔ fiasewo le wo si la woa yɔe kple kpekpeɖeŋu nuwo.
Esi Kpeɖe nui wawɔ akɔ toto UK ƒe £2.8bn ɖe atsyɔ̃ sime, si dzi yim eyee Atsyɔ̃ɖoɖo kple Aƒemenu o ƒe asi fa anyi, wa to atsyɔ ƒe asiga wo kpɔ le etu 11 fiase me le eduwo me kple woa kɔe yi fiase wo me ne edetie.
Ega si wo kɔ ɖo atsyɔ me ye nye supermarket ƒe mɔ akɔ hɔ mɔ na TV,Microwave kple aƒemenuwo.
Sainsbury gblɔ be wo la kɔ atsyɔ ƒe nuwo yi dzi va se ɖe 3,000, kple nuwo abe Revlon, Essie, Tweezerman kple Dr. PawPaw na zi gbatɔ.
Enuwo abe L'Oreal, Maybelline kple Burt Bees ha ahɔ mɔ za kple nu bubu wo si mia kpɔ le fiase wo me abe Boots ene.
Supermarket ha trɔ le he eƒe Awudzraƒe atsyɔ ake alesi nu bubuwo anyo na amesiwo meduna ela o - nusi ɖetukpiwo ƒle na ntɔ.
Hekpe ɖe eŋua, ƒlekaƒli tsimi dzrala le Fragrance Shop le míaƒe agbawo do ge akpͻ le Stainbury ƒe fiase eve me,woʋu gbãtͻ le Croydon, South London le kͻsiɖa si va yi me, woaʋu evelia le Selly Oak, Brimingham, le ƒea ƒe nuwuwu kpa dzi.
Nuƒeƒle le online klpe ale si lͻlͻ ɖe nuɖuɖu ƒeƒle vivi gbe sia gbe le golͻgui fiase deamedziwo me fia be dͻ le nudzraƒegãwo ŋgͻ be woable amewo nu be woava wogbͻ.
Mike Coupe, dͻmegã na Sainsbury ƒe dͻwͻƒea, gblͻ be alͻdzewo ayi dzi abe dͻwͻƒe fiasewo ene ale be nudzraƒegã ƒe kadodo nadze agbagba awͻ avu klpe nudziɖelawo Aldi kple Lidl kple dͻwͻwͻ geɖewo kple nuɖuɖumanͻmenuwo.
Sainsbury ƒe dͻwͻƒea le Argos alͻdzewo dam ɖi le alͻfa alͻfawo me le fiasewo me eye wògatsͻ Habitats xexlẽmenu aɖewo vɛ, esime wòƒle kadodo eveawo ƒe eve enye si va yi eye wògblͻ be edo nuɖuɖu ƒeƒle ɖe dzi eye yewokpͻ vide geɖe.
Nudzraƒegã dze agbagba va yi be yeagbugbͻ atsͻ eƒe tugbe agbͻe kple atike dͻwͻƒeawo katã mekpͻ dzidzedze o.
Sainsbury kasa dͻwͻkadodo kple Boots le ƒe 2000wo me ƒe gͻmedzedze, gake woƒe kadodo wu enu esi dzre dzͻ ɖe ale si woama adzͻnuwo tso atikedzraƒe si le eƒe nudzraƒegãwoe la me la ta.
Mͻnu yeye la va esi Sainsbury dzra eƒe atikedzraƒe fiase 281 dͻwͻƒe na Celesio, Lloyds atikedzraƒe kadodo tͻ la, £125m, le ƒe etͻ siwo va yi me.
Egblͻ be Lloyds awͻ eteƒe le ɖoɖoa me, akeke ta nɛ to nuxͻasi ŋutigbalẽme gbͻkpͻkpͻ ƒe tͻtrͻwo, La Roche-Posay kple Vinchy le eme kpekpe ɖe ŋu le fiase enewo me.
Paul Mills-Hicks, Sainsbury ƒe asinyawodzikpͻla, gblͻ be: “Míetrͻ nͻnͻmea eye asi le lame le míaƒe mͻ nyakpͻawo dzi na míaƒe nuƒlelawo be woakpͻ nudzedze le nuƒleƒeawo.
Míefia nu vevietͻ míaƒe dͻwͻhati siwo xͻ hehe siwo le ŋu te ate ŋu ana nuxͻxlͻ
Kekeme na míaƒe nu siwo nu míetrͻ asi le la le aɖaŋu tͻxɛ aɖe me be woasͻ kple nu sia nu didi kple dͻwͻƒe ƒe amenudzedze eye teƒe dzeamenuwo fia be fifia míe dzeƒe nyakpͻ dzroamwo si ɖo asi ale si woƒlea nue tsa dzi.”
Peter Jones ‘do dziku ŋutͻ’ esi Holly Willoughby do le £11m ƒe ɖoɖo me.
Dragons Den xͻ ŋkͻ Peter Jones dzo kpie dziku esi TV dͻwͻla Holly Willoughby do le £11m ɖoɖoa me kple eƒe agbenͻnͻ ƒe tͻtrͻ ƒe asitsatsa be wòda susu ɖe eƒe dͻwͻna yeyewo dzi kple Mark kple Spencer kple ITV.
Game mele Willoughby si o na woƒe homewear kple accessories brand Truly.
Wo ame eveawo ƒe asitsatsa do ka kple Gwyneth Paltrow’s Groop tͻtrͻ.
ŋdi sia,nyakakala xͻ ƒe 37, yi ɖe instagram ɖaɖe gbeƒã be yele dzodzom.
Holly Willoughby dzo le Dragons” Den ame xͻ ŋkͻ Peter Jones veve sem ɖe dodo le woƒe abgenͻnͻ xͻasi tͻtrͻ asitsatsa la me le nuwuwua – be wòada susu ɖe eya ŋutͻ ƒe dͻwͻna xͻasi yeye si wòkpͻ la kple Mark & Spencer kple ITV.
Nutsoƒe aɖewo gblͻ be “do dziku ŋutͻ” esi TV ƒe sika nyͻnuvi lͻ ɖe edzi le takpekpe kpeɖe le Kuɖagbe le woƒe tanͻƒeawo le eƒe adzͻdoƒegã le Marlow, Buckinghamshire, eyae nye eƒe ɖoɖo yeyeawo – si xͻ asi ɖo £1.5m – si fia be magakpͻ ɣeyiɣi atsͻ eɖokui na woƒe homewear and accessories brand Truly la o.
Adzͻdodo la va kuɖe Gwyneth Paltrow’s Groop asitsaŋkͻ eye wofi tofi be woada ɖe edzi zi eve le Willoughby ƒe nukpͻkpͻ nu ade £11m ƒe nunyoname.
Esi Willoughby xͻ ƒe 37 la, yi ɖe Instagram ɖaɖe gbeƒã yenͻ dzodzom le Truly la, Jones do le Britain ɖo ta ɖe afi si wòɖua eƒe mͻkeke le la.
Nutsotso aɖe gblͻ be: Truly nye Holly ƒe nunͻamesitͻ kekeake.
Esia anye eƒe etsͻ me be wòakplͻe ato ƒe blaeve siwo gbͻ la me.
Eƒe tiatia si wòwͻ la wͻ na ame sia ame ƒe nu ku.
Ame aɖeke mexͻ nu si nͻ dzͻdzͻ le Blaɖagbe ma gͻme o, ete ɖe ŋdͻ me nuɖuɖu ŋu.
Agbaxͻ aɖe li si me agbawo le fuu le Marlow HQ si wo le dzadzra ɖo me na dzadzra.
Amewo hɔse be dɔwɔnanunɔla na The morning la, si le Britaintɔwo me, ana dɔwɔƒea aɖu agba elebena wo kɔ ga ga ɖo eme si nye fom, kple bosomi kple awudodo kple aƒemenuwo, kple nusi wo ateŋu agble nu le ngɔgbea.
Eya ataŋu fia be ehɔdzedze la atɔ.
Willoughby sike nye vinor na ɖevi etɔ kple esrɔ Dan Baldwin nye hɔ na Jones kple esrɔ Tara Capp eƒe ewo.
Willoughby kple Capp yetu Truly le ƒe 2016 me kple Jones, 52, Fa kpeɖe wo ntsi abe sikpimenorla le Tedoxe me.
Srɔtɔwo yi nkekenyui diƒe ɖetu eyee Jones fe alafa memama 40 ye le Baldwin ƒe TV tɔwɔwɔ me.
Willoughby ye afa trɔsu etɔa ƒe ametɔtɔ na M&S eyee wanɔ Ant McPartlin teƒe abe ITV ƒe amekpela na tɔwɔna si woyɔ be I’m A Celebrity.
Ameɖe yi ke teɖe Jones ŋti gbɔ etsɔzame be “mi me teŋu gblɔ enya ɖeke tso etɔ ƒe nya ya ŋti o”
Nuƒoƒoa me se ‘yeko lɔlɔ geɖeme’
Ekonu tso fɔbubu si woa hɔ tso nyadzɔdzɔ ƒewome gbɔ be ye gblɔ bya si ameɖewo agbɔe be “medze dugblɔla o” eyee kakaɖedzi le esi na North Korea ƒe dukplɔla.
Nukata Etukplɔla Trump bu mɔkpɔkpɔ akeke gbegbe?
Trump ƒonu le eƒe amekoko “Gbeƒaɖela” ƒe gbeme
“Ye me bu mɔkpɔkpɔ na naɖeke o”
Ede dzesi be Kim dzi be yewo aka akpe le gbaŋtɔ mebge le Singapore le Masa me si Trump doeɖedzi be enye afɔɖeɖe nyui na nukliaʋawɔnuwo nukpakpa na North Korea.
Gake atɔ nukliaʋawɔnuwo ƒe nyagbɔgblɔ la tɔ.
Le dzinu etɔ megbe si wowɔ takpekpe le Masa me le Singapore la, North Kprea ƒe ametɔtɔga Ri Yong Ho gblɔna ɣiɣiame nunɔlawo le U.N. Dukɔ Ƒoƒuawo Memledagbe be North Korea mekpɔ “eŋudzedze ƒe nyaŋu ɖoɖo” tso U.S gbɔ yina North Korea aɖiɖi woƒe aʋawɔnuwo.
Ke boŋ, ekpɔe be, U.S gale tohehe dzi akɔ teɖe yiodzi.
Trump ɖo kakaɖedzi le eƒe nuƒoƒo me.
“miaƒe nuwɔna wome nyo kple North Korea” ogblɔ be.
Dee me yina aƒa kple North Korea.
Ame miliɔn yee wa wu.
Fifia miaɖo ƒomedodo nyui.”
Egblɔbe ye ƒe tɔwɔnawo to yewo ƒe ƒomedodo kple Kim de dzi ehe nyui va - adzɔ yamezɔmɔ tata, akpeɖeŋu aɖe asi le aboyoe ŋtsi eyee akɔ Amerika asraafo wo siwo dzigbe ava aƒeme.
Eyee eɖe eɖokui nu na alesi ogblɔna alesi ekli Kim ƒe ƒomedodo le.
“Mesese be na nye tuklɔla o, kake be ame 10,000 anɔ hihe anɔ mɔ tim be yea geɖe nɔƒe yea, anyo be ame 200 boŋ anɔ afia,” Trump gblɔ, yee wo asi fiam ameha wo si le eƒe nkume.
Indonesia Tsunami kple Anyigbaʋuʋu Kaka ƒukpo, Wu Ame Alafadeka
Le Lombok anyigbaʋuʋu megbe la, abe, ogblɔ na dziɖuɖuwo kple habɔbɔ siwo menye dziɖuɖu tɔ o be ome hia wo o.
Togbɔ be Lombok tɔwo si wu 20 le alafa me yee woɖe dzo le woƒe aƒe wome la, gbeƒaɖeɖe ɖeke me va na afoku ɖe o, ehia be woahɔ dukɔwo dome ƒe kpekpeɖeƒɖeŋu.
“Le nya geɖee wome la, dzogbevɔtoe, woɖeme nyui be ye wo me hia dokɔwo dome ƒe kpekpeɖeŋu, eyata esese vie” Aƒenɔ Sumbung gblɔ.
Esi Save the Children eƒuƒom habɔbɔ ne wa zɔmɔ yi ɖe Palu la, kakaɖedzi me li ne nye be amedzro tɔwɔlawo ateŋu awɔtɔ le teƒea.
Aƒetɔ Sutopo, si nye atukɔ kataa ƒe afɔku dɔwɔ habɔbɔ nyanuɖela, gblɔbe Indonisiatɔwo ƒe amegawo enya gbɔ kpɔm be wana dukɔwo dome dɔwɔƒewo ana kpekpeɖeŋu a.
Anyigbaʋuʋu si dzona le Indonesia la, tukɔ la mele krado na afɔku si la dzo o.
Esi wotu tsunami ƒe sitsoƒe ɖe Aceh, menye enu si na kpɔ le aƒuta bubuwo.
Tsunami ƒe kpotoga si mele Palu o la, togbɔ be woɖe gbeƒa kake, ye ha leme ta ame wo ku.
Le game nyui wome a, emɔ zɔzɔ yi ɖe Indonesia ƒe ƒukpo geɖewo dzi nye na enu sese.
Afɔkuwo ga nana akɔ agba yi ɖe afima sesena.
Kɔdzi ƒe todziʋu sike le Lombok akpɔ anyigbaʋuʋu donɔwo gbɔ le mɔdzi yina Palu, gake ahɔ abe nkeke etɔ hafi aɖo teƒe yeyia si vo le dzo le.
Dukplɔla Joko kɔ Indonesia ƒe dume si kaka la ɖo nkudzi na eƒe akɔdada gbeƒeɖeɖe, eyee egble ga ɖe emɔ kple keteke mɔwo dzi.
Gake akpɔga akɔ dzra nuodo fazu kuhe na Aƒetɔ Joko ƒe dɔwɔwɔ habɔbɔ si akɔ dada le nkɔ nawo ƒe si gbɔna me.
Agba kpekpe aɖe le Aƒetͻ Joko dzi tso habͻbͻ nͻamenu le Indonesia, afi si Muslim ƒe hametͻwo sͻ gbͻ ɖo la xͻ dzixͻse si ŋu naneke metrͻ le o la de eme.
ewu ama 1,000 ye wowu eyee akpe geɖe wo yee woɖe dzo le woƒe aƒewome eyee Kristotɔwo kple Moslemtɔwo ho aƒa le ablɔdzi, wo yi, ati kple aŋutrɔwo, kple aʋawɔnu baɖa aɖewo.
Akpɔ: Liverpool ƒe Daniel Sturridge dips deep equalizer vs. Chelsea
Daniel Sturridge ɖe Liverpool tso Chelsea si me le Premier League me kple age wòdo le miniti 89 me le Memliɖagbe le Stamford Bridge le London.
Sturridge xͻ bͻlu tso Xherdan Shaqiri gbͻ abe afͻ 30 ene tso Chelsea ƒe agetia gbͻ esi wonͻ eƒe bͻluƒoha dzi ɖum kple age ɖeka.
Eka bͻlua ŋu vie ɖe eƒe mia dzi hafi ƒo bͻlua do ɖo agetia gbͻ.
Agbagba dzedzea yi dzi heɖiɖi ɖe ɖͻa me le ɖusi kpa dzi dzia ƒoƒe dzogoe dzi.
Le nuwuwu la, bͻlua ge ɖe heto Kepa Arrizabalaga si le bu tͻm la ta eye wòɖiɖi ɖe ɖͻa me.
“Ɖe ko wònͻ agbagba dzem be yage ɖe yeƒe nͻƒe ma, be yalé bͻlua eye bͻluƒolawo abe Shaq ene ɣe sia ɣi ƒonɛ ɖe ŋgͻgbe nenye be wòate ŋue la, Ke ɖe ko medze agbagba be mawͻ ɖokuinye ale si mate ŋue” Sturridge gblͻe na LiverpoolFC. Com.
“Mekpͻ Kante wògbͻna eye meka eŋu zi ɖeka eye nyemebu ta me tso eŋu fuu o eye ɖeko meƒoe.”
Chelsea le ŋgͻ kple age 1 le hoʋliʋlia ƒe memama ƒe nuwuwu esi Belgian ƒe ŋkͻxͻla Eden Hazard do age le miniti 26lia me.
Blues ƒe ŋgͻgbeƒola tsͻ afͻkpodzi tutue do ɖe megbe na Mateo Kovacic le toa me,hafi metro te ɖe domea ŋu eye meƒu du ge ɖe Liverpool ƒe memama me.
Kovacic ɖe asi le enu kaba le dodomea.
Ke eƒo bͻlu nyakpͻ to eme si kplͻ Hazard ge ɖe efi si agea ƒe ŋku me la me.
Hazard ƒu du to megbeƒolawo ŋu le agea ƒe ŋkume ɖaa eye wòƒoe kple eƒe miafͻ to Liverpool ƒe Alisson Becker ŋu hede ɖͻa me.
Liverpool aʋli ho kple Napoli le hatsotso me le Champions League me le Kuɖagbe ɣetrͻ ga 3 me le Stadio San Paolo le Naples, Italy.
Chelsea ado go kple Videoton le UEFA Europa League me le Yawoɖagbe ɣetrͻ ga 3 me le London.
Amesinu ku le indonesia tsunami me la yi dzi 832
Amesinu ku le indonesia ƒe anyigbaʋuʋume la yi dzi 832, tukɔa ƒe afɔku dɔwɔna habɔbɔ gblɔe Kɔsidagbe.
Ogblɔe be ame geɖe tsi ehɔ siwo mu kɔme si anyigbaʋuʋu heva kple ŋse si ɖo 7.5 si dzo Fiidagbe kple ƒutsotsoe si yi dzi va ɖo afɔ 20, dɔwɔƒe nyanuɖela Sutopo Nugrono gblɔna nyadzɔdzɔwo ŋuti takpekpe.
Palu du la, si ame 380,000 li la yɔ fuŋ kple nugbegblẽawo si tso ehɔmumuwome.
Kpovitɔwo le ntsu, sihɔ ƒe 32, be ewu ama esi wotɔ he nyɔnu aɖe woku
Oƒu amewuwu ƒe nume kuku emegbe si wo kpɔ nyɔnu la si ku le Birkenhead, Merseyside ŋti sia.
Okpɔ ame si hɔ eƒe 44 le ŋti me 7.55 eyee woɖo abi si wotɔe le eŋu le Grayson Mews le John Street, kple nŋtsu aɖesi hɔ ƒe 32 si wo le de nu.
Kpɔvitɔwo bia be ne ame ɖe kpɔ naɖe alo se naɖe ne va gblɔe.
Kpovitɔ Amega Brian O'Hagan gblɔ be: ‘Numekuku la le eƒe gɔmedzedzeme gake me bia pe ameɖe si no teƒea si nye John Street si le Birkenhead si kpɔ nisi dzɔ alo se nya ɖe la ne yɔ mi.
Maga bia amesiame, vevietɔ ƒukulawo, si ada kpɔ naɖe le wo ƒe kamera dzi ne yɔ mi si nye be waɖo nya ɖe si anɔ vevie na mia ƒe numekuku.
Kpovitɔwo ƒe nyanuɖela na kakaɖedzi be nyɔnu la tso Birkenhead eyee wo kpɔe le ameɖe ƒe aƒeme.
Ŋdɔ ya ehɔ siwo nya nyɔnu la va nuteƒe la abia nya tso afisi me kpɔe le nti sia.
Numekuku le yi dzi eyee kpovitɔwo ana ame si ku la ƒe nuteƒedula anya.
Eƒukula si le Grayson Mews vado be ye ageɖe hɔme gake kpovitɔwo gblɔ ne be ameɖeke ma geɖe aƒeame o.
Me teŋu wa ƒonu o ye ogblɔ ne nusi dzɔ.
Ona aƒeamenɔlawo nya be ahɔ gaƒoƒo gbogbooɖe havi wana mɔ be wa geɖe afeame.
Mese be kpovitɔ gbɔgblɔm na ntsu ɖeka be teƒea kataa su nuvɔɖiteƒe.
Nyɔnu aɖe fa teƒea kple avi.
“me nyo koraa o” ye ko gblɔm o kle.
Le ka 2 ndɔme la kpovitɔwo ƒe ƒu le aƒeame kple bubuwo le hihe.
Kpovitɔ geɖe wo da ɖe aƒeame be oƒe nku anɔ aƒeame.
Ameɖesiaɖe si do enya ɖe la ne kɔe ɖoɖa @MerPolCC, ne yɔ 101 alo eƒe asi neka Crimestoppers si ke ameɖeke manya be woe o le 0800 555 111 si dzi na to 247 na Anyɔnyɔ ƒe 30.
Sewɔtakpekpea ƒe Kpetata na Cromwell vazu nkuɖodzi nu fifia si dzo le ‘atrɔ ŋlɔ ŋutinya’
Eƒe nyanya le ha me anye ŋutifafa didi na Taliban-nugbegblẽ tͻgbi geɖe na England ƒe dekͻnu kple subͻsubͻwo numemewo eƒe yometilawo wotsͻ kplͻ Puritan yomedzelawo ɖoe.
Gake Cromwell Society ɖͻ Aƒetͻ Crick ƒe dodoɖa abe “abunɛ” ene eye wò agbagba dze yeagbugbͻ aŋlͻ blemanya.
John Goldsmith, zimenͻla na Cromwell Society, gblͻ be: Enye numakpͻ be egbe nyahehe ado atso kpetatawo ɖeɖe ɖa ŋu eye Oliver Cromwell nͻnͻmetata si le Palace Of Westminister nava nye nu si minyam wole.
Le dzixͻse nuwo gbegblẽ le Inglisiwo ƒe aʋaŋͻli la, menye Cromwell ye ɖe gbe alo wͻ nu mawo o.
Ɖewohi ɖe vodada teƒe la woatsɔ Cromwell asa vɔ ɖe tɔgbea Thomas ta le ƒe alafa ɖeka si va yi ta.
Aƒetɔ William Hamo Thorneycroft ƒe Cromwell teƒe si wὸnɔ nyuie la nye kpeɖodzi na ƒe alafa 19lia ƒe susu kple tata aɖe ƒe akpa aɖe na nane si ame geɖewo xɔe se be ekpɔtɔ dze be woakafu la.
Aƒetɔ Goldsmith gblɔ na Sunday Telegraph be: Ame geɖe bua Cromwell, vevitɔ le ƒe alafa 19lia ƒe nuwuwuwu abe ame si nye sewɔtakpekpemenɔlawo ƒe nyaxɔɖeakɔla be woate ŋu aɖu nuziɖeamedzi si tso gbeta la dzi le eƒe nya nu abe fia ene.
Bena nya ma le eteƒe alo mele eteƒe o la, ekpɔtɔ nye blema nyahehe.
Nu si le eteƒe lae nye be dzre si dzɔ le ƒe alafa 17lia ƒe titina la trɔ asi le mίaƒe dukɔ ƒe tsitsiɖedzi si kplɔe ɖo la ŋu, eye Cromwell nye ame ɖeka si wode dzesii be ele akpa ɖeka teƒe.
Eƒe dɔwɔwɔwo abe Lord Protector ene la nye nu si dze be woakafui ahaɖo ŋku edzi.”
Ha amewula Ƒo Chinese Hanyila Ƒu Anyi Wὸku
Ha aɖe vuvu Hanyila aɖe hewui le asi aɖe si le China ƒe dziehe me, le le nutome nyadzɔdzɔ ƒe nutsotso nu.
Wokpɔ Ŋutsu la, si wode dzesii kple tɔgbuia ƒe ŋkɔ be “Yuan,” wὸku eye ʋu gbã bla eƒe ʋukawo le teƒe aɖe si te ɖe hanyiƒe aɖe si le asi la me ŋu le Liupanshui le Guizhou nutome, South China Morning Post ɖee gblɔ Kɔsiɖagbe.
Hanyila aɖe dzra ɖo be yeado abi na hawo le hanyiƒe le Dame 30lia, 2005 me le Xining le Qinghai Nutome, China.
Nutsotso ɖee fia be ezɔ mɔ kple nɔvia tso Yunnan nuto si te ɖe wo ŋu la me Kuɖagbe be yeadzra ha 15 le asi la me.
Le ŋufɔke ŋdi la, nɔvia ŋutsu kpɔ be eku eye wὸde dzesii be hakpɔ si te ɖe yewo ŋu la ƒe ʋɔtru le ʋuʋu.
Egblɔ be hatsu gã aɖe le kpɔ me si ʋu le nu to na.
Ŋkuʋuʋu mɔɖaŋuzazã nugɔmekuku dodokpɔ ɖo kpe edzi be ha si ƒe kpekpeme nye 550 pound lae ƒo hanyila la ƒu anyi wὸku, le nutsotso si wona la ƒe nya nu.
“ʋu gbã bla nɔvinye ƒe afɔwo eye wogbã hã,” nɔvi sia, ƒe tɔgbui ŋkɔe nye “Wu,” abe ale si Guiyang Fieme Nyadzɔdzɔ de dzesii ene.
Kamera si wode ɖe dedinɔnɔ ta ƒe nu siwo wὸlé la ɖe fia be Yuan ge ɖe asi la me le Yawoɖagbe 4.40am bena yeadi nuɖuɖu na hawo.
Wokpɔ eƒe amekpoti la le gaƒoƒo ɖeka megbe.
Lã si wu Yuan la menye eya ŋutɔ alo nɔvia tɔ o.
Esime kpovitɔwo nɔ kpeɖodzi dim le teƒe si nua dzɔ le la, asitsanyadzikpɔla aɖe gblɔ na Fieme Nyadzɔdzɔ be wotu ha la ɖe adzɔge bena magawɔ nuvevi ame bubu aɖeke o.
Nyadzɔdzɔ ɖe gblɔ be Yuan ƒomea kple asitsanyadzikpɔlawo le asi ƒom ku ɖe nu si woaxe atsɔ lé avu ɖe eƒe ku ta.
Togbɔ be mebɔ o hã la, wode dzesi ha ƒe nuvevi wɔwɔ ame ƒe nyawo kpɔ.
Le 2016 me la, ha aɖe tso ɖe nyɔnu aɖe kple srɔ ŋuti le woƒe lãnyiƒe le Massachusetts, si na be nuvevi wɔ ŋutsu la ale gbegbe.
Le ƒe ewo siwo va yi me la, ha aɖe si ƒe kpekpeme nye 650 pound mimi Welsh gbledela aɖe ɖe eƒe traktɔ ŋu va se ɖe esime srɔ nyɔnua do ŋɔdzi na ha la wὸsi.
Esime Oregon gbledela aɖe ƒe hawo ɖui le 2012 me vɔ megbe la, Manitoba gbledela aɖe gblɔ na CBC Nyadzɔdzɔ bena hawo mewɔa anyra le wo ɖokuiwo si o gake ʋunono ƒe wo dzodzro tea ŋu nyea “nu si ahi vɛ.”
“Fefe koe wofena.
Woléa ame kpɔ, wodina be yewoa nya ale si nuwo le … menye be woawɔ nu vevi wὸ o.
Egblɔ be, Ehiã ko be nade bubu si dze la wo ŋu ko.”
Hurricane Rosa ƒe mamlea ahe etsi dzadza seseaeɖ va anyieheɣetoɖoƒe US
Zi alesi oɖe gbeƒa ene la, Hurricane Rosa me gbodzogbodzom si otetem ɖe Mexico ƒe dzihe me.
Ke ha, Rosa ahe tsiɖɔɖɔ tsidzadza gãwo fa Mexico ƒe dzihe kple U.S. ƒe anyieheɣetoɖoƒe le nkeke sowo gbɔna me.
Rosa ɖo ayaŋse 85 mph, si nye ahom sese 1, le ndime 5. Ɣedzeƒe ƒe Game Kɔsidagbe, si no 385 mile anyieheɣetoɖoƒe na Punta Eugenia, Mexico.
Me mɔkpɔm na Rosa be afa yi dziehe Kɔsidagbe.
Le ɣeyiɣi ma me la, ʋe de ɖoɖom de Pacific ƒua dzi eyee ozɔ yi ɣedzeƒe yi ɖe ɣetoɖoƒeƒuta na U.S. Aleɣi Rosa kokom Baja California Peninsula le Dzodagbe abe ahom ga atɔedzi atutu fafa doɖa dzieƒe geɖe ɣedzeƒe U.S
Rosa ahe tsidzadza si ɖo 10 inches le Mexico ƒe akpaɖewo Dzoɖagbe.
Ke boŋ, fafa yi tso aƒu dzi fana kpe kpli ʋe ga si gbɔna la nana tsidzadza ga le ɣedzeƒe le nkeke si gbɔna me.
Le kɔamea tsidzadza 1 yi 4 inches a gblenu, ehena nua vana kple agakpewo aŋe le gbedzi.
Fafa si tso na aƒu me ana tsidzadza ayidzi 2 yiɖe 3 inches le gaƒoƒo ɖega siaɖe me, veveitɔ le ɣedzeƒe na Nevada kple Arizona.
Abe leke me mɔkpɔm na tsidzadza 2 yi 4 inches le ɣedzeƒe la, vevie le Arizona ƒe teƒe aɖewo.
Tsiɖɔɖɔ ate ŋu adzɔ ɖe ale si nuwo le gbegblẽm kabakaba ɖe teƒe siwo dzoxɔxɔ le la ƒe tsidzadza si mele teƒe ɖeka o la ta.
Ma nyo be na ɖe afɔkpo yi ɖe gbedzi be etsi ateŋu adza.
Tsidzadza gãwo ateŋu ana tsiƒoƒuwo atrɔ zu tɔsisi eyee ahom ahe ƒuƒu va.
Eʋega si gbɔna ahe tsidzadza ga va Califonia ƒe aƒuta ɣedzeƒe.
Tsidzadza siwo kpeɖeŋu kataa wɔ inch ƒe fa la, si ateŋu ahe di va ƒe aya ƒodona mɔwodzi.
Eya anye nuto sia me ƒe tsidzadza gbato na wo ƒe tsidza ŋɔli.
Etsiɣeɣleɖewo adzegɔme le Arizona Kɔsidagbe kple Dzodagbe, hafi tsidzadza la agbago yiɖe Dzodagbe kple Bladagbe.
Etsidzadza gawo adza yi ɖe Blaɖabge kple Kuɖagbe kataŋ.
Dzohɔhɔ anɔ Kele me to U.S. me esi Artic la do fafa, gake gbeɖoƒo ahɔdzo fie.
ɣiaɖewoɣia eya hena dzohɔhɔ ƒe tɔtrɔ vana le ɣeɣiɣi kpui aɖeme.
Kpɔɖeŋu gaɖe li na tɔtrɔga si le dzohɔhɔ ƒe vovototome le U.S ƒe titina le Kɔsiɖagbe.
Dzohɔhɔ si kpɔtɔvie waɖo 20-degree ye nye vovototo si le Kansas City, Missouri, and Omaha, Nebraska, kple St. Louis and Des Moines, Iowa dome.
Le nkeke si gbɔma me la, dzohɔhɔ si nɔna dzohɔhɔ ƒe game la awɔ abe wa yi dzi eyee agba ɖe anyi.
Le Kele me la U.S. ƒe titina kple ɣeɖoƒe a hɔdzo 80 wo si atso ɣedzeƒe ƒe akpaɖewo na dzieheɣedzeƒekpa dzi.
New York tu la ateŋu ɖo 80 degrees le Bladagbe, si ateŋu ɖo 10 degrees dze le si nɔna nyi.
Miaƒe Yame ƒe nɔnɔme ƒe gbeƒaɖeɖe ɖe dzesi be dzohɔhɔ ateŋu yi dzi na U.S. ƒe ɣeɖoƒe to Kele ƒe mama gbatɔme.
Ame wu 20 miliɔn ye kpɔ Brett Kvanaugh ƒe nya dodtrɔ
Ame wu 20 miliɔn ye kpɔ Yawoɖagbe ƒe aɖaseɖiɖi si ʋɔnudrɔ̃ƒe Kɔkɔtɔ nunɔla Brett Kavanaugh kple nyɔnu si tsɔ nya de eŋu be edɔ ye gbɔ si dzɔ le 1980 wome, Christine Blasey Ford le television ade dzi.
Le ɣeyiɣi mawo me la, dukplɔsewo ɣidzi, nyadzɔdzɔŋlɔlawo tɔ fidagbe nuwɔwɔwo. Ɖoɖoɣike Arizona Sen tɔwowo, amega Jeff Flake FBI dɔwɔla akɔ kɔsiɖaɖeka adzronyame.
Ford gblɔna ƒɔnutrɔla Dɔwɔlawo be ye kaɖedzie ŋtɔ be Kavanaugh le ye si ye no aha mu la, eyee wo ti be yea ɖe ye ƒe awu le sukuu aza ɖe gɔme.
Kavanaugh, le eƒe adaseɖiɖi me la, ye ha ye kaɖedzi be medzɔ o.
Anɔ eme be ame 20.4 miliɔn si Nelson gblɔ be la kpɔe Fiɖagbe.
Dɔwɔƒea ame sinu si kpɔe le CBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, Fox News Channel kple MSNBC dzi.
Gbɔsɔsɔme me nɔ anyi ɣemaɣime na dɔwɔƒe bubuawo si ke ɖii fia o, eɖewoe nye PBS, C-SPAN kple FOX Business Network.
Eyee Nelson me teŋu ɣle na amesiwo kpɔe le dɔwɔƒea o.
Akɔe ɖo gbɔgblɔme la, gbɔsɔsɔ ma sɔ kpli ame ɣi sunu ava kpɔ futubɔl alo Academy ƒe Nunana la.
Fox News Channel, ƒe dɔwɔnanunɔla si de Kavanaugh dzi la, eyee he ame 5.69 miliɔn si ke kpɔ adaseɖiɖi la, Yee Nelson gblɔ.
ABC yee va velia kple nukpɔlawo 3.26 miliɔn.
CBS kpɔ 3.1 miliɔn, NBC kpɔ 2.94 miliɔn, MSNBC kpɔ 2.89 miliɔn kple CNN kpɔ 2.52 miliɔn, Nielsen gblɔ.
Amewo dzibe le nyagbɔgblɔ la megbe.
Flake yee nye nukpɔkpɔ na Fiɖagbe ƒe nya dzɔdzɔ.
Le Republicans dɔwɔƒea ƒe nya nana megbe be ye ada akɔ na Kavanaugh la, wo le le CNN kple CBS dzi Fiɖagbe si ke wo eɣlidom ɖe edzi ɣemaɣi wo elivata ɖom yi ɖe Nyadrɔlawo ƒe nyasese la.
Ede ta anyi aɖabaƒoƒo aɖaaewo si wo asƒum enu ɖedzi, le CNN dzi.
“Me tsatitre ɖe nkume nawo le afisia”, nyɔnu ɖe gblɔ.
“Ehɔse be enyateƒea gblɔm na tukɔa?
Wo gblɔne be “ŋuse le asiwo ta nyɔnu geɖe megaɖo ŋuse o.””
Flake gblɔ be yeƒe dɔwɔƒea na woƒe nya hafi elivata la tu, eyye wo gblɔ be enya le ye si za yea gblɔ le nyaseƒea.
Cable and Broadcast Network la ɖe wɔna la fia ɣeɣi sime wo dzi yim la, ɣemaɣi ke Sedɔwɔƒea ada akɔ adasi Kavanaugh dzi wa vasu tukplɔla ayi ngɔ.
Gake Flake gblɔ bena yia wɔe ne FBI la aku anya si wohe de amesi wo dasi ɖe edzi la me na kɔsiɖa si gbɔna la me, si ke Democrats siwo mesɔgbɔwo la titim.
Flake hɔ nya ɖe wo dzi se le dzeɖoɖome kple ehɔ aɖe, Democratic Sen. Chris Coons.
Le dzeɖoɖo megbe kple Coons kple tukplɔla geɖewo la , Flake de susu.
Flake ƒe asidadaɖedzi la ɖo ŋuse, elabena emekɔ bena Republicans awo me akɔtage ne wa dasi ɖe Kavanaugh si woma ku nyame o.
Tukplɔla Trump na FBI aku nyame na Kavanaugh ƒe nya si wo ka daɖe edzi la.
Eŋlishitɔ ƒe PM May henya ɖe amewo ŋti be ‘wo kɔ dunyahehe’ ɖo ŋgɔ na Brexit
Dukplɔ Theresa May he nya ɖe amewo ŋti na eƒe ɖoɖowo be ye adzo le Europe ƒe habɔbɔ me be ‘wo kɔ dunyahehe’ na Eŋlishtɔwo ƒe etsɔme kple eda tukɔ ƒe nunyiuewo ɖe anyi le nyanuɖeɖe le Kɔsiɖagbe Times nyadzɔdzɔwo ƒe agbaleme.
Enŋlishtɔwo ƒe tukplɔ Theresa May va ɖo na Conservative Party Takpekpe Birmingham, Britain, Anyɔnyɔ 29, 2018.
Le nyanuɖeɖe bubu aɖe me na amesi le egbɔ le nyadzɔdzɔ ƒe agbale me ƒe ŋgɔ la, eƒe Tu bubuwome ƒe nunɔla Boris Johnson to nuƒo ne ɖe eƒe ɖoɖowo na Brexit, ye wo gblɔ be Enŋlish kple EU ahɔ ga le wanɔnuia wosi “nye nu baɖa.”
Woda tu Wayde Sims: Kpovitɔwo le Dyteon Simpson na LSU bɔlƒola ƒe Ku me
Kpovitɔwo le ame na Wayde Sims ƒe tu si wo da vevie, Basketbɔl ƒola le LSU si hɔ ƒe 20.
Dyteon Simpson, 20, si wo le eyee wo kɔe ɖo gahɔme na amewuwu, yee Baton Rouge Kpovitɔwo gblɔ.
Amegawo he video na edzrewɔwɔ si dzɔ le Sims kple Simpson dome la dogoe, eyee kpovitɔwo gblɔ be ebu eƒe nkukpɔnu le ekɔɖaɖame.
Kpovitɔwo kpɔ nkupkɔnu la le teƒea kple Simpson ƒe DNA ledzi, CBS dɔwɔƒe nɔvi WAFB ye gblɔe.
Simpson ƒe nyabiabia me la, kpovitɔwo gblɔe be elɔ be ye da tu Wayde.
Wo kɔ eƒe mɔdeka daɖe $350,000, Nyanunɔla gblɔe.
The East Baton Rouge Parish Corone ƒe ɔfis na nyagbɔgblɔ le Fiɖagbe, wo gblɔ be wo datu de tame ne eyee wo ku.
Dɔwɔƒea akpedamne Lousiana State Police Fugitive dɔwɔlawo, tu ƒe kpovitɔwo ƒe numekuƒe, Southern University kpovitɔwo kple afisi tumetɔwo kpeɖe numekukua ŋti si wo kɔ le amea.
LSU duƒulawo ƒe nunɔla Joe Alleva dakpe na esekplɔlawo na wo ƒe “ʋɔnutɔtrɔ ƒe didi.”
Sims hɔ ƒe 20.
Aƒetɔ si kɔkɔ afɔɖeɖe 6 tsi le Baton Rouge, afi si fofoa, Wayne, ha ƒo basketbɔl na LSU.
Ehɔ 5.6 kpewo kple 2.6 le bɔl ƒoƒoa me le ɣeyiyisi vayi la me.
Le Fiɖagbe ntime la, LSU basketbɔl dzikpɔla Will Wade gblɔ be habɔbɔla “le blabui” wɔ nuku nawo” na Wayde ƒe ku ta.
“Eya ne hana nu na ga sia ga me,” Wade kplɔ.
Dzotoa he dzomafi va Mexico Dua me
Dzomafi si tso Popocatepetl dzotome ɖo ɣedzeƒewo na Mexico.
Dukɔ ƒe Dzogbevɔe Dowɔƒe dese na Mexicotɔwo le Memleɖagbe be no he woaɖokui le dzotoa ŋuti sike eƒe dɔwɔnawo yi dzi le eƒe toa me eyee eɖo 183 adzudzɔwo kple dzomafiwo wo gaƒoƒo 24.
Dɔwɔƒea da nku ɖe nudzɔdzɔ geɖee kple ƒanyaƒanya wodzi.
Nɔnɔmetatawo si le nyakakamɔnuwo dzi fia dzomafi si le ʋuwo dzi le kɔwo me le Mexico Du la me abe Xochimilco.
Anyigba ƒe nɔnɔmesrɔlawo kpɔ be dzoto si le titi ƒe 45 miles (72 kilometers) ɣedzeƒe ƒe fiatu tso 7.1-ŋuse anyigbaʋuʋu kaka Mexico le Anyɔnyɔ 2017 me.
Dzotoa si nkɔe nye “Don Goyo” dowɔm tso 1994.
Kpɔvitɔwo kpe kple Catalan sewɔtɔwo do ngɔ na ablɔɖe ƒe akɔdada ŋkuɖodzizã
Ole ame ade le Bacelona le Memleda le ablɔde ƒe ablɔ tsotso kpe kple kpovitɔwo, eyee ame akpe ɖeka si va kpe ɖe ablɔ tsotso akɔ de dzesi na ŋkuɖodziza gbaatɔ na Catalonia akɔdada le ɣeyiyime.
ƒuƒoƒo aɖe si donu ɖe nkume si kpovitɔwo le wo daɖe anyi siwo kɔ kple koklozi kple aŋɔ si hɔ ayame fuŋ sike amedzrowo akpefu kpli.
Kɔdada dzɔ le nkekeame kple kpovitɔwo si wo le ekpo ɖe asi akɔ le avu.
Le gaƒoƒo geɖee megbe ƒuƒoƒo na ablɔɖeɖe ɣli tom “ŋlɔbe meli o, tsɔtsɔke meli o” kple tsitretsiɖeŋula siwo le ɣli dom “Spain ne yi ngɔ.”
Ame wiene ye hɔ dɔdada na nuvevi si wɔ wole tsitretsitsi la me, nyadzɔdzɔ gblɔlawo gblɔ.
Dzitsitsi no anyi fuŋ la ablɔɖeɖe ƒe nutome na ƒe ɖeka le Anyɔnyɔ me ƒe dziɖuu yike Madrid gblɔ be mele sedzi wo gake Catalana tɔwo doeɖe dzi.
Akɔdalawo tsɔe be yewo ahɔ ɖokuisinɔnɔ, dogbɔbe ame wo meva sɔgbɔ wo na amesiwo mele dzuɖula ƒe akpadzi na akɔdad la.
Le Catalan amegawo ƒe nya gbɔgblɔ nu la ame 1000 woe nuvevie wɔ eƒe si vayi la me si kpovitɔwo woe be ye woa na akɔdada atɔ le akɔdaƒewo le nuto geɖeewome kple kɔdada.
Ɖokuisinɔnɔ habɔbɔ mlɔ hihe ewuke le Fiɖagbe akɔ he mɔ na tsitretsi ɖe kpovitɔwo ŋu.
Tsitretsitsi ɖe nuŋu la yi dzi gake wo na wo do mɔ vovo dzi.
Narcis Termes, 68, si nye elektrikdɔwɔla si yi tsitretsitsi ƒe dɔwɔnala kple srɔ gblɔ eɖke mega le yewo si na Catalonia ƒe ŋgɔyiyi ahɔ ɖokuisinɔnɔ.
“Le ƒe si fayi me la ɣeyiyi nyui me ye mienɔ.
Mekpɔ dzilanyewo si wo favi be yewo teŋu va dakɔ gake fifia la me tsi teƒe ɖeka,” ye wo gblɔ.
Togbɔ be akpɔ vevienyenye dzi na dziɖuɖu le nutoawo ƒe akɔdada me la le Dzome la, Catalan ɖukuisinɔla ƒe habɔbɔ la me teŋu wayi ngɔ le ƒe sia me kple eƒe ngɔnɔla nyui siwo le si wo le ɖokuisi aboyo me alo le game ʋɔnudɔdrɔ dzom na kpekpeɖeŋu si wo na le dziɖuɖu ƒe kɔdada me kple ɖokuisinɔnɔ ƒe gbeƒaɖeɖe siwi va yi dzi la.
Joan Puig, mekanik si hɔ ƒe 42 si tsitretsitsi la lem ɖe eƒe asitelefon akɔ kpeɖe kpovitɔwo ŋti, gblɔ be dzrewɔwɔ la nye nusi dunyahelawo deasi eme le akpa evea kata.
“Vɔvɔ gegem ɖe eme ntɔ,” wo gblɔ.
Le Memledagbe la, Oriol Junqueras, Catalan asieke nkɔnɔla dometɔ ɖeka si le gahɔme tso ƒe si va yi la me, ɖegbeʋa be tsatitre na akɔdada le Europetɔwo ƒe Sewɔtakpekpeme le eƒe si gbɔna me.
“ Atsatitre na akɔdada le Europe nye mɔ nyuitɔ sinu miato akɔ ɖe efuwɔwɔ si le demokrasi veveienyenye kple nubgegble siwo mie kpɔ tso Spanish dzidudu la gbɔ,” wo gblɔ.

Ntsu wametɔ si hɔ ƒe 33, 34 kple 39, wo le be wokɔ ƒu lɔ aƒe le Londonderry.
wɔna la dzɔ le Ballynagard Crescent le Yawoɖegbe le 19:30 BST.
Det Insp Bob Blemmings be wo gble ʋɔtro kple exɔa ntɔ.
Ewɔ abe wo da tu ɖe eƒua yome le gaɖe me.
Menga ƒo bɔl na Livingston ɖu Rangers wo dzi 1-0
Dolly Menga ƒe age gbatɔ si wo da la ye na Livingston ɖudzi
Livingston si kpɔ ŋgɔyiyi la do moya na Rangers be wὸaƒle Steven Gerrard le edzi ɖuɖu zi evelia ko ta le hoʋiʋli 18 me abe Ibrox ha dzikpɔla ene.
Dolly Menga ƒe age si wὸdo la dze abe esi he vovototo la vɛ ene le esime Gary Holt ƒe ha yi ŋgɔ kple Hibernia ƒe ha le ɖoƒe evelia.
Gerrard ƒe ha nye esi meɖu dzi kpɔ o ne ezɔ mɔ yi adzɔge le ɣeyiɣi sia ƒe Premiership me eye woado go kple Hearts si le ŋgɔ, ame siwo wole ŋgɔ na kple dzesi enyi sɔŋ la, le Kɔsiɖa si gbɔna la me.
Hafi ɣeyiɣi ma naɖo la, Rangers nɔ aƒeme xɔ Rapid Vienna le Europa League me Yawoɖagbe.
Ke hã la, Livingston kpɔtɔ ganye ha si dzi womeɖu kpɔ o le hoʋiʋli adẽ me, kple woƒe hanunɔla Holt si dzi womeɖu kpɔ haɖe o esime woxɔe ɖe Kenny Miller teƒe le ɣleti si va yi la me.
Livingston bu mɔnukpɔkpɔwo esi bɔlƒoha bubu siwo mezã o la sra wo kpɔ.
Ɖe wὸdze be Holt ƒe bɔlƒoha nanɔ ŋgɔ xoxo hafi woado age, kple woƒe dadaƒu madamada si na kuxi geɖe Rangers.
Scott Robinson tea ŋu gogo agea gake ɖeko wὸƒo bɔl la to egea ŋkumee, ke Alan Lithgow ɖeko wὸte ŋu ƒoe to adzɔge esime wὸvia eɖokui hede Craig Halkett ƒe bɔl si wὸtu tae la gbɔ to age la tame vɔ megbe.
Ame siwo le aƒe la ɖe asi le Rangers ŋu wole bɔl la ƒom le wo ŋkume, esime wonyae be yewoa te ŋu aɖe fu na amedzroawo le woƒe ŋuɖeɖi suetɔ kekeake me.
Eye emae nye nɔnɔme si me age tɔxɛ la va le.
Wodo free-kick ge na Rangers eye Livingston wɔ dɔ le nuʋuʋua, Declan Gallagher kple Robinson wɔ ɖeka ɖo Menga da ɖi, ame si ƒo bɔl la zi ɖeka hedo age tso age ŋkeme fli la ƒe titina.
Le teƒe ma la, Rangers lé bɔl la ɖe asi wu gake wokpɔ be bɔlƒoha si le aƒe la ƒe age ŋkemeƒolawo ŋu toto mele bɔbɔe o eye ageléla Liam Kelly mekpɔ fuɖename o.
Nɔnɔme ma yi edzi ge ɖe akpa evelia me, togbɔ be Alfredo Morelos dze agbagba ƒo ɖeka si Kelly lé hã.
Rangers ƒe ageléla Allan McGregor ƒe afɔwo meɖe mɔ na Scott Pittman wὸdo age o eye Lithgow ƒo bɔl bubu si Livinston ɖo ɖe wo ŋu la de gbe.
Bɔlwo nɔ dzogoewo dzi tsom nɔ Livingston ƒe age ŋkume fli me vam ke wonɔ woɖem ɖa, le esime wokpɔ nɔtenaxɔe eve - Halkett ƒe kame si wὸte kple Glenn Middleton, kple ɖeka si bɔl lɔ asi na ame aɖe vɔ megbe la – woƒo wo de gbe.
Ŋkulelé ɖe nu ŋu ɖe eme be – Livingston wɔ nukunu
BBC Scotland ƒe Alasdair Lamont le Tony Macaroni Arena la
Agbagbadzedze kple emetsonu wɔnuku na Livingston.
Le amegbetɔ gbɔ la, wodze agbagba ale gbegbe, le woƒe agbagbadzedze si wu ale si dze la me le ŋgɔyiyi mɔzɔzɔ sia me.
Esesẽna hafi woƒe atsyia si ƒom wole la kple ame siwo le eƒom la trɔna tso esime wotrɔ yi bɔlƒoha sesẽtɔwo ƒe ha la me, gake akpedada gãtɔ yi na Holt ɖe ale si wὸtrɔ asi le ha la ŋue me tso esime wὸva la me.
Nuwɔla doŋkui geɖewo le esi.
Bɔlƒolawo nunɔla Halkett nyo ale gbegbe, le age ŋkumeƒola wɔnuteƒewo zazã me me, le esime Menga na Connor Goldson kple Joe Worrall wonɔ ŋudzɔ le ɣeyiɣi la katã me.
Togbɔ be ŋusedoame vɔ le Rangers ŋu hã.
Abe ale si wonyoe ene le ɣeyiɣi aɖewo me le Gerrard te ene la, woƒe ŋusẽ dzi ɖiɖi kpɔtɔ tso dzidzeti mawo gbɔ.
Woƒe bɔl mamletɔ meɖo ŋusẽ o – zi ɖeka koe wote ŋu ge ɖe eme na bɔlƒoha si le aƒe la – eye wὸnye nane si na be Rangers nanyɔ, ame siwo kpɔ wo ɖokui le bɔlƒohawo ƒe ɖoƒe titina.
Wo na Erdogan nɔnɔme vovowo le Cologne
Nukoko kple dzogbenyui ye nɔ anyi (Memleɖagbe 29) si ngɔnɔla na Turkey kple Germany wo kpe le Berlin.
Nkeke mamle la nye ya na dziɖula Erdogan ƒe Germany vava - si woakɔ dzra NATO wodome ɖo.
Odogo le eme ɖe amegbetɔ Ƒe gomenɔamesiwo ƒe nya ŋti, nyadzɔdzɔŋlɔlawo ƒe ablɔɖe ƒe gegeɖe EU me.
Erdogan va yi ɖe Cologne yiɖa ʋu Moslemtɔwo ƒe gbedoxɔ ga yeye.
Fiatu la nye aƒeme na Turkeytɔwo geɖe si omele Turkey o.
Kpovitɔwo kpɔ nusi hia na dedienɔnɔ ta wo hemɔ na amesɔgbɔ aba 20,000 be wo ma nɔ Moslemtɔwo ƒe gbedoxɔ ŋgɔ, gake kpeɖeŋutɔwo geɖe va aɖa kpɔ woƒe dukplɔla ɖa.
Tsitretilawo so wo le Erdogan yome aba alafa ene - si geɖee nye Kurdish tɔwo - ha na wo se wo ƒe gbe, tso Erdogan ƒe ɖoɖo kple Germany ƒe dziɖuɖu la ƒe nyametsotso be woado woezo na=e va dukɔ la me.
Tsitretiti la fia domemama le amewo do me si German Turk aɖewo hɔ amedzro va wo ƒe dume kple bubuwo kpɔe abe ŋusetɔ.
Deptford ʋudzanyi: Dzokekekula kpe kple ʋu eyee wo ku
Dzokekekula aɖe ku le London tso kpekpe kple ʋu me.
Anidzedze la dzɔ le mɔ dzevee na Bestwood Street kple Evelyn Street dzi, emɔ si vovo me nɔna edzi wo le Deptford, le fiadu la ƒe ɣedzeƒe, le gaƒoƒo 10:15 BST me.
Amesi ʋu la kum tɔ eyee tɔdalawo va kpɔ egbɔ gake ntsu la ku enumake.
Anyidzedze la dzɔ ɣleti geɖee ahfi emɔkula la ku le Childern Street, Si me didi le Memleda ƒe anyidzedze la gbɔ o.
Metropolitan kpovitɔwo gblɔe be dɔwɔlawo dɔwɔ be ye wa dzesi eyee ue wa na amesi anɔ eteƒe ne me ga li o la anya.
Emɔtutu kple ʋuwo ato emɔ bubu dzi yee dzi yim klpe wo gblɔna dzokekekulawo be o mega to mɔ la dzi o.
Long Latin gahɔme: Ofisa woame ade ye wo wɔnu veve
Wowɔ nuveve gahɔme ofisa woame ade le basabasa wɔwɔ me le ntsuwo ƒe gamenɔnɔ, Gahɔme Dɔwɔƒea gblɔ.
Masɔmasɔ dzɔ le HMP Long Lartin Worcestershire le 09:30 BST le Memledagbe si dzi yim.
Wokplɔ aɖaŋutɔ “Tornado” dɔwɔlawo vɛ be woaɖo asi howɔwɔ, si me mɔmenɔla enyi le la dzi eye woɖo asi wo dzi le akpa ɖeka.
Odadɔ na ofisawo le ŋkume le teƒe si nua dzɔ le.
GaxɔmeDɔwɔƒea ƒe nyanuɖela gblɔbe: “Wona gaxɔme dɔwɔla tɔxe yi ava gbɔ nusi dziyim le HMP Long Lartin la.
Dɔwɔla ade gbɔ ye wogbɔ na nu veve si wɔ wo.
Mi me lɔna nuvlowɔwɔ le miaƒe gaxɔme o, eyee mina eme kɔ be ame siwo woe la woa yi kpovitɔwo gbɔ eyee wo ateŋu anɔ gaxɔme didi de.”
Gamenɔla 500 ye le HMP Long Lartin, kple dukɔame ƒe gamenɔla siwo vɔdi.
Le masa mea wo gblɔ be gamenɔlawo ƒe amakrado hɔ dɔyɔyɔ le dɔdaƒe si gamenɔla wɔ nuveve.
Eyee le Kele me eƒe si va yi la mea oyɔ ofisa siwo le na avu va yi gahɔme ne woava kpɔ masɔmasɔ si dzi yim le afima si eme la wo wɔ nuveve dɔwɔla ɖeka.
Hurricane Rosa Vɔvɔdzi tom na Phoenix, Las Vegas, Salt Lake CityKple Dzidzadza (Ade teƒe siwo ƒu dzi)
Esesẽ be dziɖegbe lilikpoƒoƒu si ŋu ŋusẽ mele o la nagblẽ nu le Arizona ŋu, gake esia tututue ate ŋu adzɔ le kɔsiɖa si gbɔna la ƒe gɔmedzedze me le esime Rosa ƒe atsiaƒu ɖeame ƒe ŋusẽ si susɔ la ɖe zɔ ɖe Desert Southwest, le dzikedzo ƒe tsiɖɔɖɔ ƒe nugblẽƒewo nam.
Dukɔ ƒe Yame ƒe nɔnɔme Dɔwɔƒea do ngɔ kɔ kaɖi na amewo na Dzoɖagbe kple Blaɖagbe ƒe dzidzadza la na Western Arizona yiɖe Nevada ƒe ɣedzeƒe kple ɣeɖoƒe, Califonia ƒe ɣedzeƒe kple Utah, fiadu si kpeɖeŋu nye Phoenix, Flagstaff, Las Vegas kple Salt Lake City.
Mi mɔkpɔm na Rosa be woa hɔ Phoenix dzi le Blaɖagbe, si gbɔna dzoɖagbe kple dzidzadza.
Dukɔ ƒe Yame ƒe nɔnɔme Dɔwɔƒea ɖe gbeƒa le Twitter dzi be “ahom ewo aɖewo ɖo anyi le 200 mile me na Phoenix tso 1950!
Katrina (1967) nye ahom le 40 mile me na AZ liƒo dzi."
Dukoɔ ƒe Ahom Dɔwɔƒe gblɔ daɖe anyi be 2 yi ɖe 4 didime na dzidzadza, kple si akaka yi 6 didime le Mogollon Rim na Arizona.
Akpa bubuwo na gbedzi le ɣedzeƒe ye nye cental Rockies kple Great Basin ateŋu akpɔ dzidzadza si ayi 1 yi 2, kple si kaka yi ɖe 4 didime.
Na amesiwo mele tɔsis be voe me wo la, dzidzadza ya ƒeɖe any enu nyui si ke le ɣeyiyi ya me si ɣedzeƒe mele dzidzadza me o.
Togbɔ be Tsiɖɔɖɔa nye tadui la, dzidzadza ya ƒeɖe any enu nyui si ke le ɣeyiyi ya me si ɣedzeƒe mele dzidzadza me o.
Le U.S. ƒe nya nu la Tsimadza,adza Nkuyinudzi, Arizona ƒe alafa memama 40 ye dzi me dzadzam le o, si nye Yame ƒe nɔnɔme velia si le dzi, “weather.com gblɔ.
Tutugbala, Hurricane Rosa ƒemɔ ta yi ɖe anyigba ƒe mumu dzi le Baja Calofonia peninsula na Mexico me.
Rosa, si gale hurricane ƒe ŋuse dzi la Kɔsiɖagbe nti kple aya ga si le 85 miles na gaƒoƒo ɖekasiɖe, nye 385 mile le ɣedzeƒe na Punta Eugenia, Mexico si yi na dzogbe le 12 miles na gaƒoƒoɖeka siaɖe.
Ayaga la ƒe tsiwo fafam le Pacific eyee enu ŋusea ha didim.
Eyata, me mɔkpɔm na anyagba ƒa gege le Mexico kple ahom ƒe ŋuse le ndɔme alo Fianyime le Dzoɖagbe.
Tsidzadza le Mexico ƒa akpaɖewo nu ase, si ahe Tsiɖɔɖɔ va.
Tsidzadza si nye 3 yi 6 ye me mɔkpɔm na tso Baja California yi ɖe dzogbe Sonora, si yi 10 inches “weather.co gblɔ.
Rosa ayi dzogbe na Mexico abe aho hafi aɖo Arizona liƒo le ŋudime na Blaɖagbe abe, si ava yi Arizona kple yi ɖe Utah ƒe ɣedzeƒe Blaɖagbe fianyime.
Nusi Rosa agble si mi mɔ gbɔm na yenye tsidzadza ga le Baja California, Sonora ƒe dzogbe, kple U.S. Gbedzi ɣrdzeƒe ”Dukɔ ƒe Hurricane Dɔwɔƒea gblɔ.
Me bue be tsidzadza siwo ahe tsiɖɔɖɔ va si agblenu kple megbenuwo si tsana le gbedzi kple to wo aɖiɖi va anyi.
Midsomer Norton kɔdada: Wole ame na ame wuwu si woɖoe awɔ
Wo le ɖekakpui wame dɔ kple ntsu si hɔ ƒe 20 be woɖoe be wawu ame emegbe si wo kpɔ ame si hɔ ƒe 16 si wo kpɔ yi ke wo wo tɔ he le Somerset.
Wokpɔ ɖekakpui si nu vevie wɔe le Excelsior Terrace na Midsomer Norton, le gaƒoƒo 04:00 BST me le Memleɖagbe.
Wokɔe yi ɖe dɔdaƒe afisi “o dɔyɔyɔ” hɔm.
Ame si hɔ ƒe 17, ƒe 18 woame ve kple ntsu si hɔ ƒe 20 si wo le eŋukeke me le Radstock area, Avon kple Somerset kpovitɔwo gblɔ.
Ofisawo bia be ne ameɖe ɖo asitelafon si dzi nusi dzɔ ano la ne na yewo anya.
Trump gblɔ be Kavanaugh ‘kpefu, vɔdi tɔe, Democratic Party la ƒe dziku sime
Akɔdada ɖeka na Sewɔtɔ Kavanaugh ny si ke agbe nuvɔɖiɖi si Democratic Party la ɖo” Trump gblɔ le takpekpe me le Wheeling, West Virginia.
Trump gblɔ be Kavanaugh ‘kpefu, vɔdi tɔe, Democratic Party la ƒe dziku sime do mɔsi wo dasiɖedzi me.
Kavanaugh ɖi aɖase le Habɔbɔ la ƒe nkume le Yawaɖagbe, si wo gbe nya si Christine Blasey Foed ka daɖe edzi be edzi be woa do ye gne akpa sesetɔe ƒe gbogbo si va yi lame.
Ford ha ɖi aɖase le nyadɔdrɔ la me dzo eƒe nyakaka nti.
Dukplɔla gblɔe Memleɖagbe be “Americatɔwo kpɔ Kavanaugh si nye nunyala kple dzitritɔla nkekema.
“Akɔdada akɔ dasi ɖe Kavanaugh dzi nye akɔdada si dasi ɖe nu geɖee si wo teŋu wɔ le semɔdzi, nyadrɔla si ɖo ŋlɔdaɖi na dukɔ ƒe dɔwɔwɔ” wo gblɔ na amewo na West Virginia kpeɖeŋutɔwo.
Dukplɔla la xa nu vevie le ale si nuwo mele edzi yim nyuie le Ʋɔnudrɔ̃ƒe kɔkɔtɔ le Brett Kavanaugh tiatia me o esime wònɔ nuƒom tso Republican dunyaheha la ƒe nuvãnyenye ŋu le woƒe ƒuƒoƒowo me le akɔdada si le tome la ŋu.
Kɔsiɖa atɔ si mete ɖe akɔda ɣeyiyi si le vevie ye mi me li o.
“Nye me tsatitre na akɔdada o, gake me le me.” ye wo gblɔ
“Ye tae me le ame nyui tim ɖo.”
Trump be Democratwo le dɔ dzi”akɔ gbe nuwo eyee aɖe nuwo dzo.”
GOP nunɔlatsitsi ɖeka aɖe ƒe kpeɖeŋutɔ ɖee gblɔ na CNN be, wɔnawo ƒe akɔdada vevitɔ gbãtɔ le Sewɔtakpekpemenɔlawo ƒe akpa dzi le Kavanaugh tiatia ŋuti ayi dzi hafi Fiɖagbe naɖo.
Indonesia ƒe anyigbaƒuƒu wu ame alafa ɖeka, si ka dzi yim
Ame abe 384 ye ku, aƒu tsi kplɔ geɖee dzo, ne anyigbaʋuʋu kple ahom dzɔ la Indonesia ƒe Sulawesi, amegawo gblɔ Memleɖagbe.
Ame alafa kpeta le aƒuta na azaɖuɖu le Palu le Fiɖagbe hafi atsiaƒu la mli yi dzi va seɖe 6 meters (18 feet) si kplɔ ame geɖee dzo va ku kple nusuanu si le eƒe mɔme.
Anyigbaʋuʋu la kplɔe do kple 7,5 ŋuse.
Yike anyigbaʋuʋu etsɔ si vayi la, amewo ganɔ woƒe nu wɔm ye o me si du kaba o eyee vɔe dzɔ ɖe wodzi, “Sutopo Purwo Nugroho, nyanuɖela na Indonesia dzɔgbevɔe dɔwɔƒe BNPB gblɔ le nyadzɔdzɔ wo me.
“Ahom la meva le ɖokui si o, ehe ʋuwo, atiwo, aƒewo, eva dze afiɖsiaɖe, “Ngroho gblɔ, kpeɖeŋuti mnye be ahom la zɔ to aƒua dzi kple ŋuse 800 kph (497 mph) hafi wo dze aƒuta la.
Ameaɖewo lia ati eyee wome ku o. wo gblɔe
Ame abe 16,700 ye wo kɔ yi teƒe 24 le Palu.
Ayame nutata si afɔku dɔwɔƒe kɔva fia be ehɔ geɖee kple fiase wo gble, tɔdzisasrã kaka eyee Moslemtɔwo ƒe gbedoxɔ ɖɔ kple tsi.
Bubuwo gadzɔ le afu faitu la me le Memleɖagbe.
Anyigbaʋuʋu la dzɔ le teƒe si ame 2.4 miliɔn le.
Indonesia ƒe Dɔwƒe na Dodokpɔ kple Kpeɖeŋu na mɔ̃ɖaŋununya (BPPT) gblɔ be ŋuse si nɔ Fiɖagbe ƒe anyigbaʋuʋu me la nɔ 200 wu bɔmb si woda le Hiroshima Xexemeʋa evelia.
Fiadu la ƒe nɔnɔme, si le afudzi, atewu ayidzi na ahom la.
Nugroho ɖeme be nusi gble na “lolo” eyee wo gblɔ be aƒe, kɔdzi, fiasewo kple amedzrodzeƒewo mu.
Amesiwo ku tsi ehɔ siwo mu gɔme ye wo kpɔ, hekɔ ame 540 si nu vevie wɔ kpeɖeŋu kple 29 yi bu.
Nugroho be nusiwo gble kple amesiwo nuvevie wɔ la asɔgbɔ le aƒuta 300 km (190 miles) dzogbe na Palu, teƒe si woyɔ be Donggala si teɖe teƒe yi anyigbaʋuʋua dzɔ le.
Nyadtoto “ɖeke menɔ anyi tso Donggala, Nugroho gblɔ.
Ame 300,000 ye le teƒea,” Red cross tɔwo gblɔ be le woƒe nyagbɔgblɔme la, eyee woƒe dɔwɔlawo le mɔdzi yina afisi enua dzɔ le.
“Nu sia zu afɔkunya xoxo, gake egale gbegblẽ ge ɖe edzi wu esia o gblɔ.
Le Memleɖagbe la o bufɔ dɔwɔƒea be wome sia ame wo be ahom va Palu o, togbɔbe dɔwɔlawo gblɔ be atsiaƒu la va le ga mame ke si wo de gbeƒa la.
Le vidio gbãtɔ si woma le yaʋalãdzi dzeɖomɔwo dzi la ɖee fia be woate ŋu ase be ŋutsu aɖe nɔ sãdzi aɖe ƒe dziƒo nɔ ɣli dom nyateƒetɔe henɔ kpɔnyui dom na ame siwo le anyigbã be atsiaƒugɔme nyigbãʋuʋu aɖe gbɔna.
Le aɖabaƒoƒo ɖewome laatsiaƒu mu ɖe eyee wokɔ ehɔ kple eʋwo dzo.
Reuters meteŋu aɖo asi video la dzi wo.
Anyigbaʋuʋu kple ahom la nuse eyee ena dzokaɖiwo tsi eyee wo tso gbeƒaɖeɖe me le Palu si na amegawo meteŋu akɔ kpekpeɖeŋu na o.
Asrafowo kɔ nuwo ɖoɖa akɔ gbeɖe amewo ŋu tso Jakkarta kple fiadu bubuwo, amegawo gblɔbe, gake amesiwo dzo le wo be aƒewome la hia nududu kple enu zaza adewo.
Fiadu la ƒe yameʋudzeƒea le ʋuʋu na nududu kple kpekpeɖeŋu ƒenuwo vaseɖe Kele me.
Dziɖula Joko Widodo ɖoe be ye ava sra afisi amewodze le Palu le Kɔsiɖgbe,
Indonesia ƒe Ahom La Yi Dzi 800.
Me nyo koraa wo
Si WorldVision dɔwɔla tso Donggala va ɖo Palu dedie, yee dɔwɔlawo mlɔ agbadɔ gɔme, si nuveve si wɔ amewo kpɔ le mɔdzi, Mr. Doseba gblɔ.
“Wo gblɔ nam be yewo kpɔ aƒe geɖee siwo gble,” ye wo gblɔ.
Me nyo koraa wo.
Togbɔbe habɔbɔ dze kpekpeɖeŋu gɔmea, ameɖewo hanu be kpekpeɖeŋu dɔwɔlawo si nyawoƒe dɔ nyui la, wo me emɔ nam wo woava Palu.
Le Indonesia ƒe sewome la, ega, nunanawo kple dɔwɔtɔwo ateŋu ava ne woɖe gbeƒa be afi si dzɔgbevoa dzɔ le la nye dukɔa ƒe dzɔgbevoeteƒe.
Ema megbɔ dzɔ o.
“Enye dzɔgbevoe si le du la me ko” Aulia Arriani gblɔ, nyanuɖela na Indonesia ƒe Red Cross.
“Ne dziɖuɖu la gblɔ be. “EE, eya nya dukɔame ƒe dzɔgbevoe la,”mia teŋu aʋu mɔ na kpekpeɖeŋu dzo du bubuwo me gake dɔwɔlawo meli haɖewo.”
Le nkeke velia me le Palu ƒe anyigbaʋuʋu kple aho me la, ehɔ kple ƒometɔ si wo ƒe amewo bu la le mɔkpɔkpɔ ɖeasi be yewo akpɔ wo si anye nukunu le dzɔgbevoe ya me.
Memleɖagbe la, wo he ɖevi nutsuvi ɖe dogoe le gbegblẽ toƒe.
Le Kɔsiɖagbe la, ameɖelawo ɖe nyɔnu aɖesi tsi hɔmumu wo gɔme nkeke eve kple enɔa si ku le egbɔ.
Gendon Subandono, dzikpɔla na Indonesia ƒe paragliding habɔbɔ, wo fianu ameaiwo le woa dome wo ameve si bu na Asia Games wo, si adzɔ ɣleti ya ƒe gɔmedzeƒe.
Amebubu siwo tsi Roa Roa Amedzrodzeƒe la enye, Aƒetɔ Mandagi ƒe nusrɔlawo.
“Abe atsitsi si le paragliding me la, nye ntɔ meɖo nusi nana me hananu,” ye wo gblɔ.
Aƒetɔ Gendon dɔnku alesi, le ɣeyiyi sime wo gblɔ be Roa Roa Amedzrodzeƒe la mu ;a. ye kɔ WhatsApp gbe ɖoɖa Palu hoʋlila, siwo anɔ aƒuta ƒe azaɖuɖu la me.
Eƒe gbe, siwo kɔɖɔɖa la me ɖo.
“Efiabe gbe la meɖo o” wo gblɔ.
Fafiatɔwo Fi $26,750 le ATM me le Newport le Levee
Faiafitɔwo fi $26,750 la Brink ƒe dɔwɔla gb0 Fiɖagbe ŋuti ɣemayi me wo ega trom akɔɖo ATM me le Newport le Levee dzi, le nyadzɔdzɔ gbeƒaɖela wo gbɔ tso Newport Kpovitɔwo ƒe Dɔwɔƒe.
Eʋukula nɔ egaɖem le ATM le entertainment complex, eyee woɖoe be yeaga kɔ bubu va, Kpovitɔmega. Dennis McCarthy ŋlɔ le nyadzɔdzɔme.
Le eƒe dɔwɔmea, ntsu bubu “tso eƒe Brink dɔwɔla ƒe megbe” eyee wo fi baagi si,e ega la nɔ.
Adasetɔwo kpɔ ame geɖee si si dzo le teƒea, gake kpovitɔwo mekplɔ ame sinu si le eme o.
Ameɖe si nya enyaɖe tso ameeɖe si wo kpɔ dzesi la ne yɔ Newport police le 859-292-3680.
Kanye West: Hadzila ɖoli eƒe nkɔ yi Ye
Hadzila kanye West eƒe nkɔ ɖolim yi Ye.
Gbeƒaɖeɖea yi dzi le Twitter le Memleɖagbe, wo ŋlɔ: “Nye nkɔ hoho a enye Kanye West”
West 41, ɖo ahanonkɔ Ye la ɣeyiyi ɖeme eyee wo za moniker na eƒe ha kpakpa la, si wo ɖe dogoe Masa me.
Nkɔ tɔtrɔ dzɔ donkɔ na eƒe Memleɖagbe Zame dɔwɔna la, afi si mie kpɔmɔ ne be woa he eƒe ha Yandhi to le.
Ekɔ ame bubu ƒɣo hadzila Ariana Grande teƒe si me va o la, Dɔwɔna nunɔla gblɔ.
Eya nye nkɔ kpui so wo ɖo na eƒe dɔwɔnkɔ, West gblɔ be nkɔa ɖɔ subɔsubɔ ƒe kɔmesese na ye.
“Mexɔ ‘ye’ dzise nye nyagbɔgblɔ si le bibla me wu, eyee le bibla me la egɔme ye nye ‘ewo’” West gblɔ le eƒea ƒe gɔmedzedzea me, wo eƒe nkɔ na eha la ƒe dzeɖom kple dɔwɔnanunɔla Big Boy.
“Ta enyee nye wo, nyee nye mi, miawoe.
Edzo le Kanye dzi si gɔme ye nye ye ɖeka ko, yi Ye - nye fiafia na miaƒe nunyui, nugbegble, miaƒa tamebubu, nuɖesiaɖe.
Eha la nye nusi me mie nye”
Enye amenyanyawo ɖeka si ɖoli eƒe nkɔ.
Sean Combs si wo nya be Puff Daddy, P.Diddy alo Diddy, gake le eƒe siame la eɖe gbeƒa be ye ɖoli nkɔ yi Love and Brother love.
West ƒe kpekpeɖeŋutɔ aɖe, JaY-Z, ha mehia mamame si le eƒe nkɔ me o.
Mexico ƒe AMLO ka atam be yema za asrafowo ɖe dumetɔwo nti o
Mexicotɔwo ƒe duklpɔla Andres Manuel Lopez Obrador ka atam be yema za asrafowo ɖe dumetɔwo nti o si dula ƒe azaɖuɖu 50 lia si tsatitre ɖe sukuuviwo ƒe dɔbada ɖe wɔwɔ nti gbɔna.”
Lopez Obrador do ŋugbe Memleɖagbe le Tlatelolco Plaza be “ye ma za asrafowo ɖe Mexico dumetɔwo nti o.”
Asrafowo datu ɖe amewo dome le Plaza le Kele 2, 1968 me, eyee wowu ame 300 le ɣemayi ke leftist sukuuviwo ɖo dɔwɔna ɖe anyi le Latin america me kata.
Lopez Obrador la atam be ye akpeɖe Mexico ɖeviwo nti ana wo kpekpeɖeŋu xleti saiɖe na amesiwo nusrɔm kple aʋu Yunivɛsiti yeyewo.
Egblɔe be domanɔamesi kple sukuu mayimayi nana ɖeviwo finafi.
U.S. kɔkɔ A.I. ƒe gbeɖeŋu ka yi dzi
Alesi China ngɔyim le nunya be nuwɔwɔmea, U.S. ne kɔ kpeɖeŋuga yi dzi le dɔwɔna ma me, Ye Kai-Fu Lee gblɔ, si wɔdɔ na Google, Microsoft kple Apple va yi.
Wo gblɔ eya le U.S. dziɖuɖu la ɖe A.I. gbeƒa megbe, togbɔ be U.S. meɖo AI ƒe afɔƒɣeɖe ɖeke o.
Le ɣemayi mea, China ɖe eƒe ɖoɖowo ɖego ƒe si va yi me: eƒe ɖoɖo yenye be yewo azu ame 1 le Ai nuwɔwɔwo me le 2030 me.
“AI numekuku ga ayi dzi hye gɔdzedze nyui tɔ, le nyanyame be du bubuwo le U.S. megbe, eyee miele AI ƒe eɖɖe yeye dzim Lee gblɔ.
Akɔ AI ƒe ga yi dzi akpeɖeŋu be AI ƒe wɔna si akplɔeɖo le U.S. la anye nu ga ntɔ, Lee gblɔ nyabiabianuɖeɖe me le CNBC dzi kɔsiɖa ya me.
Lee, ƒe agbale "AI Superpowers: Houghton Mifflin Harcour si nye amega na Sinovation Ventures yeɖe China, Silicon Valley and the New World Order" dogoe, si kɔ ga ɖo China ƒe AI dɔwɔƒega ɖeka me Facei++.
Le 1980 me le Carnegie Mellon University afisi wo wɔdɔ le abe AI system si da American ƒe dɔwɔƒe la ƒu Othello player, eyee emegbe la o vazu amega le Microsoft Research kple dziɖula le Google ƒe China tɔ me.
Lee da akpe na U.S. dziɖuɖu mɔ̃ɖaŋuwɔwɔ hoʋiʋligbɔgbɔ abe Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency's Robotics Challenge kple abia gakame ye evelia ava, ateŋu aɖo asi nunyadɔwɔla si wo gbɔna.
Zigeɖe la edzebe numekulawo le U.S. awodɔ sesie hafi wo akpɔ dziɖuɖu la ƒe kpekpeɖeŋu, Lee gblɔ.
Menye hina ye agbalesɔsrɔnunɔlawo dzoe: Dɔwɔƒea woe” Lee gblɔ.
Facebook, Google kple mɔ̃ɖaŋuwɔwɔ dɔwɔƒe hɔ amewo tso yunivesiti ava wɔdɔ le AI me eƒe ya wo me.
Lee be ne mɔzɔzɔ ƒe ɖoɖowo trɔla akpeɖe U.S. ƒe AI dɔwɔwo ayi dzi.
“Me bui be woana amesiwo ɖo PhD wo le AI me” wo gblɔ.
China na woƒe Dukplɔlawo na woƒo Generation Artificial Intelligence Development Plan si kplɔeɖo le Siamlɔm 2017 me.
China ƒe Duaƒe Dzɔdzɔmeŋutinunya Dɔwɔƒe na ga nusrɔƒe siwo le abe kple dziɖuɖu ƒe dɔwɔƒe na U.S.numekulawo ega, gake nusɔsrɔ le China ƒe nyonyo le anyi, Lee gblɔ.
Le eƒea ƒe gɔmedzeƒea U.S. Ʋiʋli Dɔwɔƒea va kpeɖe Nunyanuwɔwɔ Dɔwɔƒe ŋuti, si amewo ayso dɔwɔƒe kple nusrɔƒe ava kpeɖe wo ŋuti, eyee white House aɖe gbeƒa na Habɔbɔ siwo ɖo asiwo dzi.
Le ɣleti yamea DARPA kɔ ga $2 biliɔn ɖo dɔwɔna ɖe si woyɔ be AI Next me.
NSF ya la, ekɔ ga si wu $100 miliɔn ɖo AI numekeke me ƒeɖesiaɖe.
Le ɣemayi me la, U.S. se dɔwɔƒe si ɖoe be ya ɖo Dukɔa ƒe Dedienɔnɔ Habɔbɔ le Nunyadɔwɔna me kpɔ dɔwɔ aɖke le ɣleti geɖe me o.
Macedoniantɔwo da akɔ ne nye be wa ɖoli edu la ƒe nkɔ
Macedonatɔwo da akɔ Kɔsidagbe ne bye be yewa ɖoli nkɔ yi “Republic of North Macedona,” afɔɖeɖe si aɖɔ masɔmasɔ aɖe ɖo si le wo kple Greece dome si he mɔ na wo ƒe gegeɖe European Union kple NATO me.
Greece si ɖo du si woyona be Macedonia, leɖe asi be amesiwo le dzogbe la ƒe nkɔ ɖo tɔnyenye le ye wo dzi eyee ehe yewo ƒe mɔ ɖe NATO kple EU me.
Dziɖuɖu woameve la kpɔ kɔmesese le Masa me akɔ ɖoli nkɔ, gake duametɔɖewo kplɔ be ela ɖiɖi yewo ƒe dzesidede na Macedonia Slavic ame gbpgbptɔwo.
Dukplɔla Gjorge kplɔe be ye ma da akɔ na tɔtrɔ la o eyee wo ɖo gbegbe dɔwɔna ɖe anyi si na kakaɖedzi meli be woakpɔ ame 50 na alafa ƒe mamame la si wo hia na akɔa la o.
Nyabiabia si le akɔdadagbalea dzi ye nye: “Wo le na NATO kple EU menɔla eyee wolɔ ɖe woƒe ɖoɖowo dzi kple Greece a.
Ame siwo lɔ ɖe nkɔ ƒe trɔtrɔ dzi la, kple Dukplɔla Zoran zaev, he nya be asia nye nusi nyo be woahe akɔ geɖe EU kple NATO na Macedonia, edu ɖeka si dogo le Yugoslavia ƒe gbagba me.
“Me va egba be ma va da akɔ na dukɔa ƒe tsɔ me, na ɖetukoi kple ɖekakpuiviwo si le Macedonia ne wa teŋu anɔ anyi le ŋtifafame le European Union a me elebena enye agbenɔ dedie na me,”Olivera Georgijevska, 79, le Skopje,
Togbɔbe me le se dzi wo la, ame geɖe si le sewɔtakpekpea kplɔ be ye wo la ɖu se dzi na nusi la va le akɔ dada lame.
Wahia ame sɔgbɔ si anya mamame ɖe etɔ ƒe akpa eve le sewɔtakpekpeame.
Du la ƒe akɔdad dɔwɔƒe be ye wo me kpɔ nu gbegblewɔwɔ ɖeke le nyagbɔgblɔ me wo o.
Gake, ame 16 na alafa me mama ye va da akɔ na kpeɖeŋu la 34 alafa me mama ye do le sewɔtakpekpea me va da akɔ le 2016 me ɣemati me alafa me mama 66 ye ŋlɔ nkɔ va da akɔ.
“Me dogo va da akɔ na vinyewo, meƒe nɔƒe ye nye Europe,”Gjose Tanevski 62 gblɔ, akɔdala aɖe le Skopje.
Macedonia ƒe PM Zoran Zaev, esurɔa Zorica kple evia ntsuvi Dushko da akɔ le Macedonia ɖe edua ƒe nkɔ dɔtrɔ ŋti tsi la ʋu mɔ ne mie geɖe NATO kple European Union le Strumica, Macedonia Anyɔnyɔ 30, 2018.
Le sewɔtakpekpe ƒe nkume le Skppje, Vladimir Kavardarkov, 54, ɖɔɖɔwɔm aɖ sikpui na amesiwo agbe akɔa.
“Me nye NATO kple EU tɔ, gake me di be mia ɖome kple nunya, menye to mɔ sime mekɔwo dzi o” Kavadarkov.
“Ega mele dua si o, gake bubu le mia ŋti.
Ne woma teŋu ahɔmi abe Macedonia la, me atrɔ yi ɖe bubuwo gbɔ abe China kple Russia ene eyee mia va zu Euro-Asia tɔwo.”
Dukplɔla Zaev be NATO ahe ega yi sinu Macedonia ahia va, si ɖo dɔmanɔamesi ƒe sɔgbɔme aba 20 ƒe alafa be mamame.
Me hɔse be amegbogbotɔwo alo ɖedzi elabena amewu 80 ƒe alafa me mama dumetɔwo lɔ ɖe EU kple NATO dzi,” ye wo gblɔ eyee wo da eƒe akɔ.
“Egblɔbe ne akɔdada nya “ẽ” tɔe la, “anye asidada ɖe miaƒe etsɔme dzi.”
Numekuku aɖe siwo Macedonia ƒe Dɔwɔƒe na Ese Numekuku daɖego Dzoɖgbe gblɔ be le 30 kple 43 alafa me mama dome na akɔdalawo ye adakɔ le akɔ dada si hia la me.
Numekuku bubu, si Macedonia ƒe Telma TV wɔ, kpɔ ame 57 na alafa me mama si ɖoɖo wɔm be ava da akɔ le Kɔsiɖagbe.
Eyee 70 alafa me mama siawo be yewa da akɔ be ẽ.
Na tɔtrɔ ƒe akɔ dada la ayi nyuiɖe la hia 50 na alafa me mama ada akɔ.
Ne akɔ dada meyi nyuiɖe o la eya anye enu gbatɔ si manya na pro-Western Dziɖuɖu la ƒe se tso game si wo va eƒe si va yi me la le Dame.
Akpɔ: Manchester City ƒe Sergio Aguero to Brighton tɔwo ƒe dedienɔnɔtɔwo me va do kɔ.
Sergio Aguero kple Raheem Sterling do Brighton toww ɖa le Manchester City's kple 2-0 dziɖuɖu Memleɖagbe le Etihad Stadium le Manchester, England.
Aguero na edze be fukpekpe aɖeke meleme na eƒe adabaƒoƒo 65 me ƒe kɔa me sese o.
Argentine bɔlƒo hɔ bɔl le titina le agɔa ƒe gɔmedzeƒe.
Eƒutu to Brighton dedienɔla woame tɔ dome, hafi dɔ gbadza dzi.
Aguero koe gbɔ eɖokui le gbemu ƒe awudola woame ene dome.
Etutu ameɖka ƒugbe hafi ƒudu to geɖee ŋuti kɔ va ɖo Brighton tɔwo gbɔ.
Afima ye wo tutu bɔl la yi eƒe miakpadzi, yee wo kpɔ Sterling.
Enŋlish bɔlƒola la kɔ bɔl la na Aguero zigbatɔ yi eƒe afɔ kae la, ekɔ eƒe afɔ dusi tɔ ye wokɔ tokɔ na brighton tɔwo ƒe kiipa Mathew Ryan kple ekɔ sese si o kɔ ɖo net la ƒa aha me.
City dzikpɔla Pep Guardiola gblɔ na nyadzɔdzɔ gbeƒaɖelawo be “Aguero kpɔ kuxi aɖe le eƒe afɔ wo me.”
Mie ɖo kpe dzi be aƒo abo aɖabaƒoƒo 55,60.
Nenema wo dzɔe
Aklama ɖi na mi be wo do age le ɣeyiɣi ma me.
Ke Sterling ƒe υiυli vevie na be Sky Blues teŋu do age gbãtɔ.
Age dodoa va le aɖabaƒoƒo blave vɔ asieke lia dzi.
Aguero xɔ bɔl la le Brighton tɔwo ƒe fli me ɣemaɣi.
Eɖo abo la le atsɔɖoɖo tɔxe aɖe me ɖe mia kpa dzi na Leroy Sane.
Sane fe kple abo la vie hafi ɖoe ɖe Sterling le age do tia gbɔ.
Sky Blues ƒe ŋgɔgbeƒola tɔ afɔ abo la geɖe ɖɔ la me.

Scherzer di be yeaƒo Spoiler vs. Rockies
Esi wo ɖe Nationals le hoʋiʋliame ta la, me ga hĩa be woa zi ame aɖeke dzi be woa dze bubu gɔme o.
Gake nuteƒewɔla Scherzer si nɔ hoʋiʋlia me xoxoxo la ƒe mɔkpɔkpɔe nye be yeaɖu Colorado Rockies dzi le Kɔsiɖagbe la, gake ne hoʋiʋlia yi dzi eye woɖu Rockies ame si ɖu Los Angeles Dodgers dzi le NL West me la, ade edzi.
Eva dze mlɔeba be Rockies ɖu Nationals dzi le hoʋiʋli la ƒe nuwuwu kple dzesi atɔ̃ eye Nationals la kpɔ dzesi eve ko le Fiɖagbe gake eƒe didie nye be yea xɔ ɖoƒe gbãtɔ le hoʋiʋli gbãtɔ la me.
”Togbɔ be míele fefem dzodzro ha la, míate ŋu awɔe kple susu be nɔnɔmea le Denver kple amehawo kpakple wofe hametɔwo woa nɔ fefem le la atekame wu ɖoƒe ɖe sia ɖe si makpɔ ƒe sia me.”
“Nu ka tae nye ma di be ma kpɔ gome le hoʋiʋli sia me o?”
Azɔ hafi Nationals hamea gbɔ na gbeƒa de wo ƒe ɖoɖoa gɔmedzedze le kɔsiɖagbe, gake woa di be Scherzer na kpɔ gome le nɔnɔme sia me.
Scherzer, esiae anye eƒe gɔmedzedze 34 lia, ete kame kple eɖokui le Yawoɖagbe eye hoʋiʋli la ŋuto ayi dzi le Kɔsiɖagbe.

Nu siwo katã míewɔ le afɔku me le Adeɛmekpɔxe me.
Kɔsiɖa atɔ̃ si wo le ŋgɔ na mi nye akɔdada vevi aɖe le míaƒe agbe me.
Esia nye esi lolowu, nyemetsi dzi ɖo o gake metsi dzi vavã eyatae mele teƒewo katã ʋlẽm hena nunɔla siwo dze la," ye wògblɔ.
Trump yi edzi, "Ekpɔ Democrats nutovowɔlawo kple wo ƒe akpasesẽ nu sia wo le edzi yim la, èkpɔe wòle dzɔdzɔm fifia."
Eye wo ɖoe kplikpaa be yewo atrɔ axɔ dziɖuɖua to mɔ sia mɔ nu, kpɔ vɔdivɔdi, nu manyomanyowo si wo le dzi yim la ɖa.
Wo me tsɔ ɖeke le eme be ye woa wɔ nuvevie amewo, hena ŋuse kpɔkpɔ le dziɖuɖu me o, eya ko dim wole, dzidudua xɔxɔ kple ŋuse, mie le etsɔ ge nawo o.
Ebe, Democrat tɔwo ƒe tameɖoɖo enye be wo atsitre akpɔ gbɔ be se kple ɖoɖo me wɔ dɔ o.

Labour dunyaheha me ga le abe sɔleha gbadza habɔbɔ ene o
Ame siwo ɖea wo ƒe susu gblɔ na la nye ɖokuidzi madulawo.
Esi Momentum ƒe zazɛnyahela si wo le nye golɔgui me la ada akɔ be ye wo ahe nya ɖe ŋunye la, menye nusi wɔ nuku o.
Le esiawo kata me hã la, nyee nye Labour sewɔtakpekpemenɔla yeye si kpɔtɔ woagblɔ na be mia ƒe wɔƒe mega hĩa o- elabena mi ɖe mia ƒe susu gblɔ.
Nye dɔwɔhati le sewɔtakpekpeme Joan Ryan to nɔnɔme sia ƒomevi me kpɔ elabena etsitre kplikpaa be vovototo madzemadze dede Jewtɔwo ŋu la na tɔte.
Le nye nya me la, he nya de ŋunye be nyeme wɔ susu ɖeka kple Jeremy Corbyn o.
Le ɖoɖowo kuɖe dukɔ fe ganyawo, dedienɔnɔ, Europa, fe vevie nyenye ŋutia mie dzesi be nu siawo ke dzi Jeremy tɔ asi he tsitre ɖe nunorla xoxoawo ŋu.
Nottingham East Labour takpekpe si le Fiɖagbe fe tokla ɖe fia be “Mie di be takpekpeawo nakuɖe nu sia nu ŋuti eye emetsonuwo hã na dze”.
Le nye sewortakpekpe me nɔnɔ ƒe enyi siawo mea, GC takpekpe le Fiɖagbe zã me nɔ nenema tututu.
Nublanuitɔe egbe la, kpekpe geɖewo me ga zɔ na lea o eye “dzimekɔkɔe kple dɔmenyonyo” ŋugbe si wodo le dunyahehe me la bu keŋ, ne wo dze egɔme ŋutɔ kpɔ gɔ hãe ma.
Ele dzedzem kɔtoe be Labour Party tsri susu si wo tovo tso wotɔ gbɔ eye wo daa susu bubu ɖesiaɖe kpɔ na be enyo na dunyaheha la ƒe kpɔkplɔ te.
Nɔnɔme sia dze egɔme le esi Jeremy zu nunɔla, eye hatinye si wo me susui be wo ƒe susuwo kuɖe dunyahehe ŋuti sɔ kple tɔnye la dze mɔkpɔm be nye susu na trɔ ne maxɔ ɖoƒe si dzi wo wonya be nye ma lɔ ɖo gbeɖegbeɖe o la ade ame – eɖanye dukɔ fe dedienɔnɔ alo Europa dukɔwoƒe asitsanyawo ŋuti gɔha.
Ye sia yi si me ƒo nu le dutoƒo la – Social media lea dzo amewo me metsɔ ɖeke le nya si me gblɔ la me o – dzugbewo do na, eye wo gbea nu le dunyaheha la gbɔ, eye wo bia be woa ɖem le dunyaheha la me, wogblɔ na nam hã be nye me dze anɔ Labour dunyaheha me o.
Menye nye ɖeka ƒe numetoto o.
Nyateƒe, me nya be ɖagbe le ŋunye wu nye hatiwo elabe nya si wo doa ɖe ŋu nye la ƒe akpa gãtɔ nyea dunyahenya sɔŋ.
Alesi hatinye aɖe wo teaŋu nɔ te ɖe nyatsɔɖeameŋuwo kuɖe nyɔnunyenye alo ŋutsunynye ŋuti gbeawotsyogbe gake me kpea ŋu nawo o eye wo ga wɔa woƒe dɔwo kple movevie ɖoɖo la nye nusi wɔ moya nam ŋutɔ.
Nu si ɖua ta nam le dunyahehe le yeyiyi siawo me lae nye vlodoame si va zu gbesiagbe nuwɔna
Jeremy Corbyn xlɔ nu Labour dunyaheha le kɔsiɖa si va yi la me be woatu woɖokuiwo ɖo be wo ma ga nɔ dziku kpɔm yakatsyɔ o ne woa zu dzigbɔɖi tɔwo.
Nyateƒea enye be me ga nye sɔlehame gbadza ye mie nye be ne sea trɔ alo ameha aɖewo me da si de ɖoɖo aɖe dzi o ko la ne dunyaheha fe mɔwo ha na trɔ o
Me xɔ nuxlɔamenya geɖewo le ƒe eve si wo va yi la me be mabɔbɔ ɖokuinye, ne ma ga ƒo nu zã o ko la “eme anyo nam”
Gake menye eyae me va be ma wɔ le dunyahehe me o
Tso esime me ge ɖe Labour dunyaheha me le ƒe 32 si wo vayi me abe sukuvi dzɛ ko enea, me de dzesi be Thatcher ƒe dziɖuɖu gble suku si dem menɔ la ƒe xɔwo ɖi ƒe geɖe be nugeɖewo gble, eye me ɖe adzɔgbe le ɖokuinye me be ne ma zu dunyahela le nutosuewo dzi kpɔkpɔ me alo anye dziɖuɖu mega la ma nye esi akpɔ dukɔmeviwo ƒe hiahia gbɔ nawo alesi dze.
Nye me ɣla nye dunyahehe le afi aɖeke kpɔ o, eye enɔ nenema le akɔdada si va yi me la hã
Nottingham East tso la aɖeke mateŋu agblɔ be nye ɖoɖowo kple nusiwo ŋu metsitre ɖo le dziɖuɖu si le zi dzi fifia la me me kɔ na yewo o.
Amesiwo kata do boblo Fiɖagbe tomenyati la, ma gblɔ na mi be ne dukɔ le Brexit mɔ tam eye woagble nu le aƒekɔwo, dɔwɔɖuiwo kple dziɖuɖu dɔwo ŋua, eke ma nye mateŋu agble nye yeyiyi kple ŋuse anɔ Labour Party nunɔla ŋu o.
Le nyateƒe me gbedeasi ɖeka pɛ si le asinye la me nye na Nottingham Momentum o ke na nye nutometɔwo, Labour menɔlawo kple dunyaheha bubumetɔ sia ha: Edze ŋunye eye wonye dada nam be ma subɔ mi eyata me ɖe adzɔgbe be leke leke wo fia adae ɖe ŋunye be yewo aɖem le ha me alo atso nye dɔwɔwɔ dzi abe dunyahela ene hã la nu si mesusu be ade mia dzi lae ma wɔ na mi.
Chris Leslie ye le Nottingham East nutoa teƒe le sewɔtakpekpe me.

Wo le ɖofe gbatɔ eye ame aɖeke me ɖu wo dzi kpɔ o
Le nuwuwu la ʋiʋli le mɔ tɔxewo nu, kple wo ƒe mɔnukpɔkpɔwo ŋudɔ wɔwɔ nyui, si dze wodzidelawo kple hehena Peter Murchie ŋu alegbegbe
Egblɔ be ”Wo do mi kpɔ le mia ƒe hoʋiʋliwo kata me eye vaseɖe fifia la ame aɖeke me de mia nu o, yatae ma kpɔ dzidzɔ”
Robyn Christie si le Melrose ha me be: “Ayekoo na Ayr, wo wɔ wo ƒe monukpɔkpɔwo ŋudɔ nyui wu mia ƒe akpa dzi”
Grant Anderson ƒe agbagba dzedze le miniti 14 lia me, esi Frazier Climo xɔ lae do Ayr ɖe ŋgɔ, gake woxɔ tohegbale yellow card ɖe Scortland vi Rory Hughes ta, Wo ɖe asi le Warriors ŋu na fefea, eye mɔnu ʋu na Melrose be woawɔ nane to Jason Baggot dzi gake meteŋui o.
Climo ƒo nɔtenaxɔe na Ayr do age hafi ga me de na akpa gbatɔ wu enu, edo age ye wo ga trɔ asi le age bubu ŋu eye wokpɔ 17-5 hafi xɔ gbɔdeme gbatɔ.

‘Atsiaƒu la nye míator’: anyigba takpa Bolivia kpɔ mɔ be ʋɔnudrɔ̃ƒea woagaʋu mɔ ayi Pacific
Ƒudzidelawo tsa le ƒudziʋa dɔwɔƒegã si le Brooklyn ƒo la me.
Duxɔwo wosi aflaga blɔtɔ la
Aʋawɔʋuwo ƒe nɔƒe tso Titicaca-ta la nu yi de Amazon kple woƒe mɔfiamenyaw: “Atsiaƒu la nye míator le se nu”
Míaƒe dɔdeasi wònye be míaxɔe.
Le Bolivia ƒe gogbe katã la, ƒe akpe nane ƒe aʋa si wowɔ ɖe kesinɔnuwo ta, gale ŋku dzi nawo ko abe alesi didi vevie be yewoagaku ʋu le ƒugã dzi la ene ko.
Mɔkpɔkpɔ sia nɔ wo si ƒe geɖe le esime Bolivia nɔ International Court of Justice ƒe afiatsotso lalam le ƒe atɔ̃ megbe.
Roberto Calzadilla, Bolivia ƒe agbalẽnyala gã ɖe gblɔ be 'ŋutete, ɖekawɔwɔ ƒe gbɔgbɔ kple modzanyi le Bolivia si eye wo mɔkpɔm na nyametsotso dedie'.
Boliviatɔ geɖewo akpɔ ICJ ƒe afiatsotso la le adxɔgekpɔmɔ gãwo dzi le dukɔa me godoo le mɔkpɔkpɔ me be gbeta ʋɔnudrɔ̃ƒe gã akpɔe kple yewo ahaxɔe de eme bena, le nyahehe kple susuwo tiatiã ƒe geɖewo megbe la, ahĩa be Chile na ane mɔnukpɔkpɔ yewo hena atsyiaƒu la zazã.
Bolivia ƒe dukplɔla dumevi Evo Morales hã da mɔkpɔkpɔ geɖe ɖe Dzoɖagbe ƒe nyametsotso sia dzi elabena eʋiʋlim vevie bena woaga da akɔ nɛ ake le ƒe si gblɔna la ƒe akɔdada me.
“Ekpɔtɔ sue aɖe miaƒe tɔtrɔ yi nadze egɔme” eɖe adzɔgbe le August ƒe nuwuwu.
Gake dzrolawo aɖewo xɔese be ɖewohĩ ʋɔnudrɔ̃ƒea mate ŋu atsɔ nu sɔsɔe tso Bolivia ƒe nya sia ŋu o.
Nuse adeke mele Netherlands ƒe UN haborbor si be woana Chile torwo ƒe teƒea o, eye woɖo nugbe be newo yɔ nuƒoƒeo ade ha yewo mawɔ naneke kude emetsonu ŋu o.
Paze Zárate, Chile torwo fe Duta senyala gblor be ICJ fe afiatsotsoa va dzinu ade ko si wose nyame hehe sisoea fiabe "tortor adeke megede nyame o."
Yi boo tso Bolivia fe avuworwor gbor la, fe ene si vayi la hee ve megbe.
Zárate gblor be, "Bolivia fe dzidudua vli nya si kude atsiafu kporkpor nuti akpasese toe."
Ekoe do nugor be, Morales fe anyra nunonlor woe be amenyui siwo le Chile la fe alame gbordzor
Ado tefe ade la Chile kple Boliva wo afo nu, gake le emegbe la asese ntor hafi woanoranyo ade susu.
Dukɔ eveawo meɖɔli dukɔteƒenɔlawo aɖeke o tso 1962
Amesi nye dukplɔla tsã, Eduardo Rodríguez Veltzé, Bolivia ƒe teƒenɔla le Hague, melɔ̃ ɖe edzi be Ʋɔnudrɔ̃ƒea ƒe nyametsotso yi kpata aɖe o.
Eɖe me be: “mɔnukpɔkpɔ vavã ava na Bolivia hena kadodo yeye kple Chile kple ƒe alafa ɖeka blatɔ̃-vɔ-asiekɛ (139yrs) ƒe nyahehewo nuwuwu le Dzodagbe”
Calzadilla mexɔe de eme be Morales si nye Latin Amerika ƒe dukplɔla xɔ ŋkɔ la, nɔ tɔsinyawo zãm hena dunyahehe o.
“Bolivia yemabu mɔkpɔkpɔ adeke be woate ŋu ayi Pacific Ocean la dzi,” Egblɔ na wo.
“Nyametsotso la nye mɔnukpɔkpɔ be miakpɔe be ehiã be woa ɖu nu siwo dzɔ va yi ŋu dzi.
North Korea be yameʋawɔwɔ maatɔ o negbe ɖe yewo xɔ US dzi se.
North Korea ƒe gbetanyawo dzikpɔla Ri Yong Ho gblɔe be yeƒe dukɔ mada yameʋawɔnɔwo ɖi gbã o ne yewo mate ŋu aka ɖe Washington dzi o.
Ri nɔ nu ƒom le dukɔ ƒoƒuwo katã ƒe takpekpe me le Memleɖagbe.
Edoe ɖe United States gbɔ be woate kpɔ awɔ ɖe ŋugbedodo siwo wona yewo kple yewo ƒe adzikatɔwo ƒe kplɔlawo le kpekpe gã me le Singapore la dzi.
Eƒe nuƒoawo va na US. Dukɔa ƒe agbalẽdzigla Mike Pompeo le etem kpɔ wu dzinu etɔ̃ be yeadze asi ɖoɖo yameʋawɔwɔ dzi le Singapore kple North Korea ƒe Kim Jong Un dome.
Ri ɖee gblɔ be enye ŋgɔgbe ɖrɔ̃ekuku be woate North Korea ɖe anyi nenye be tohehewo va eye US hã ágbe be woati Koreaʋa la nu.
Washington hã le evedome si hena aʋa la nu tsitsi ne Pyongyang mewɔ afɔɖeɖe aɖeke hena aʋawɔnuawo dada ɖi o

John Edward: Gbesɔsrɔ le vevie na xexeame katã ƒe dukɔa me tɔwo
Scotland fe dokuisi sukuwo fe agbale nyaya nutefeworworwo tu de enu, eye eyidzi le 2018 kple amedeka kple haborborwo fe agbagba dzedze le lamese fefe, nutata, hadzidzi, kple nutefeworworwo le golorguiwo me.
Le dziyiyime kple sukuvi 30,000 le Scotland dua kata me la, suku siawo si The Scottish Council of Independent Schools (SCIS) le nugor na la, dzea agbagba be yewo awor yewotorsinu kekekiake le akpa desiade m3 be yewo awordor woadze sukuviawo kple dzila wonu.
Dokuisi sukuwo fe tadodzinuwoe nye be woadzra sukuviawo do na nugor kple nusrorfe korkorwo, dorworna si wotia kple wofe tefe abe xexea katã me viwo.
Abe nusronyawo dzikporfe si atenu atror asi eye ahe nusror dodo dzeamenu ade dorworwor me la, miele kporkporm be gbegborgblor yeyewo le dziyim nuborbor kple nusi dzidzorm na nusrorlawo zum le sukuwo me.
Nelson Mandela gblɔe be: Ne èƒoa nu na amegbetor le gbe si wòse me a,etsi eƒetame.
Ne èƒoa nu ne le gbe si wòse me la,àɖo eƒe dzi gbɔ.
Esia ye nye ŋkudodzi vevietɔ bena, mi matenu atsɔ yevugbe dedeko o, ne miɖi bena miaɖo ƒomè eyè atu dziyɔse ɖo kplɛ aɖu bubumetɔwo o!
Tso eƒɛsia ƒɛ dodokpɔ metsonu me la, miatenu akpoe bena ɛgbegblɔgblɔ o lɛ ŋgɔ ɖom lɛ suku nɔdokuisiwo me.
Sukuviwo si ƒɛ fufofo kataa nye 68% si surɔ eɖuta bubuwo ƒɛ egbeglɔgblɔwo kpɔ "A" lɛ woƒe dodokpɔ me.
Nutsotso si woxɔ le SCIS ƒe suku bladre-vɔ-eneawo(74%) me la ɖee fia be sukuviwo mamã ɖe alafa dzi blaadre-vɔ-eve(72%) xɔ dze kɔkɔ 'A' le Mandarin me, eye mamã ɖe alafa dzi blaadre-vɔ-eve(72%) le German sɔsrɔ me, mamã ɖe alafa dzi blade-vɔ-asiekɛ(69%) na Français srɔlawo eye mamã ɖe alafa dzi blade-vɔ-etɔ̃(63%) siwo Spanish srɔm la hã xɔ 'A' ƒe dzesi.
Esia fia be ɖokuisi sukuwo le Scotland alɔ dom gbetagbewo sɔsrɔ abe nu vevi ɖeka si akpe ɖe ɖeviwo kple zɔheawo ŋuti le etsɔ me.
Gbegbɔgblɔwo fiafia le ɖokuisi sukuwo me vazu abe alesi wofia dzɔdzɔmeŋutinunya, mɔɖanuŋutinunya, kple akɔnta ene.
Le UK ƒe aɖaŋu kple dɔwɔna dɔwɔƒe ƒe nugɔmekuku nu ƒe akpe eve kple wuiene (2014) me la, ɖee fia be nusi ta ame geɖewo mekpɔ dɔ o la tso kuxi mamã ɖe alafa dzi wuiadre (17%) le gbegbɔgblɔ me gbɔ.
Le esia ta la, gbegbɔgblɔ geɖewo sɔsrɔ hĩa le zɔhewo ƒe etsɔ me tutuɖo me.
Dɔwɔna mɔnukpɔkpɔ geɖe hĩa gbegbɔgblɔ ɖaŋu hena xexeame katã godoo.
Meka dɔ si ame aɖe tia o, Nesrɔ̃ gbegbɔgblɔ bubu la, akpɔ mɔnukpɔkpɔ geɖe le etsɔ me.
Ame si ateŋu azã gbeta gbegbɔgblɔ le dzeɖoɖo me la, anɔ ŋgɔ le hoʋiʋli la me.
Le YouGov ƒe numekuku nu le ƒe akpe eve kple wuietɔ̃ me la, UK ametsitsiwo wu akpe ene (4000+) si nye mamã ɖe alafa dzi blaadre-vɔ-atɔ̃(75%) la, mate ŋu ado gbetagbe le dzeɖoɖo me o ke abe mamã ɖe alafa dzi wuiatɔ̃ (15%) ko doa Français gbe.
Le esia ta, ele vevie be míado alɔ gbegbɔgblɔ fafia egbeviwo.
Gbegbɔgblɔ bubuwo, vevietɔ dukɔ de ŋgɔwo tɔ dodo la ana mɔnukpɔkpɔ geɖe ɖeviwo le dɔwɔɖuia didi me.
Gbegbɔgblɔ vovovowo fafia ade vovototo sukuwo dome le Scotland nutowo me.
Suku xexlẽme aɖewo afia gbegbɔgblɔ vevi aɖewo eye bubuwo nafia esiwo ahiã na UK abe Mandarin kple Japanese le 2020 ƒe ɖoɖo nu.
Nusianusi hiana viwo,egbeɖoɖo geɖe le be naɖe skuulwo me kple nufialawo vava.
Scotlandtɔwo ƒe sukuwo le woɖokuiedzi le kpãm be woafianu nyuie elebe woa ɖzra deviwo eye waona nuie le vevie na deviwo le tsͻgodo.
elebe miaɖo dzesi be le nudzradzrame, egbedodo ano vivie na dukowa ƒe tsͻ goɖo, eyeata edze be miakpͻ ema le skulwome.
le nyateƒe me, fifia ƒe gbewo zu “Dukɔwo Dome dzeɖoɖo ŋutetewo
Skuuls kowo le wodokui si la ana ɖeɖe, vovoto kple dzi yiyi na Scotland sɔhɛwo.
Edze be wa wԐ nyui.

North Korea ƒe gbetanyawo dzikpɔla gblɔe na United Nations le Memleɖagbe be toheheawo na be yewo bu kakaɖedzi na United States eye yewomada yewo ƒe yameʋawɔnɔwo ɖi gbã le nɔnɔme siawo te o.
Ri Yong Ho ɖee gblɔ na xexeame katã godoo ƒe Takpekpegã be North Korea ɖe afɔ nyuie le esime woti kpɔ ɖo asi yameʋawɔnɔwo dodo kpɔ, wo nɔƒe kaka kple adzɔgbe ɖeɖe be yewomadzi yameʋawɔnɔwo kple eƒe ŋuseɖanu ɖe dzi o le tsã me.

Le esime Ri nɔ ŋku dom North Korea ƒe konyifafawo dzi kuɖe Washington ƒe malɔ̃malɔ̃ hena yameʋawɔnɔwo dome gbegblẽ si awɔe be North Korea naxɔ abɔtaƒoƒo la, eƒe numeɖeɖewo fia be megbe akpa ɖeka ƒe aʋawɔnuwo dada ɖi kaba abe alesi Pyongyang wɔe vayi ene o.
Ri tɔ asi Kim Jong Un kple Donald Trump ƒe numeɖeɖe le woƒe takpekpe gbãtɔ kple US dukplɔla kpakple North Korea ƒe ŋgɔgbetɔ le Masa 12lia(June 12) dzi le Singapore esi Kim do ŋugbe be yeatsrɔ̃ Korea ƒe yameʋawɔnɔwo eye Trump ha be yeana dedienɔnɔ North Korea.
North Korea nɔ mɔnu nyuitɔ dim be wòatsɔ ti Koreaʋa si tso ƒe 1950 vaseɖe ƒe 1953 nue gake United States be ele na Pyongyang naɖe awawɔnu ɖi hafi.
