Ronaldo ƒe lɔyawo le dzradzradowɔm be yoakplɔ Der Spiegel ƒe nyatsɔtsɔwo yide ʋɔnu, siwo le yɔyɔm be nyamadzɔmadzɔ nyawo kaka le ame ƒe ɣlaɣlanyawo nu"le Reuters ƒe nya nu.
Lɔya Christian Shertz glɔ be bɔlƒola la bia fehehe na "nɔnɔme nyui ŋu nyawo ƒe gblēgblē le gã ƒomevi si sɔ kple dasedidi la ƒe kpekpeme, sinye amegbetɔ se vevitɔwo deka ƒe dzidada le ƒe siawo me."
Nusia dzɔ le ƒe akpe eve kple asieke ƒe dzinu adelia dzi le Palms medzrozēƒe kple casino xɔ ade me le Las Vegas.
Esime wo dogo wo nɔewo le zã hanoƒe la, Ronaldo kple Mayorga trɔyi bɔlƒola ƒe xɔ me, fima wo do aʋu nē le gbime, abe alesi nyakaka gbalē si yɔ Clark County nutome gblɔe enē le Nevada.
Mayroga gblɔ be Ronaldo dze klo nē le wɔna sia megbe eye gblɔe nē be yenye ame nyui le "blasiekevɔ asieke de alafa dzi" ɖe anyi kple "deka de alafa dzi"
Agbalēwo gblɔ be Ronaldo do kpe dzi be wovea dɔ wonɔe wo gbɔ, gake wove wo lɔ de dzi.
Mayorga gblɔ nyala na kpovitɔwo eye wotsɔ eƒe abi foto siwo ede le kɔdzi tsɔ fiɔ wo, gake emegbe la elɔ de ŋutifafa nyametsotso ade dzi elabena ele vɔvɔm na vɔteƒedodo eye le xa nu be "yea do ŋukpe yedokui le ameha dome."
Ƒe blatɔvɔ ene nyɔnu gblɔ be yedzi be yea gbenu le ŋutifafa nyametsotso wɔna dzi abe alesi wo kpɔtɔ le tsakatsaka me kudo nusi dzɔa nu.
Ronaldo kele yi Real Madrid tso Manchester United le esime ʋudodo nyasia va, eye le dzome ŋɔli wo ʋu yi Italian dzɔtsutɔwome le Juve le euro gã miliɔn alafa deka ƒe asitsatsa wɔna me.
Brexit: UK afa konyi mavɔtɔe le ʋu wɔlawo ƒe bubu ŋuti
UK "afa konyi sia mavɔtɔe" ne enye be wo bu eƒe ɖoƒe abe xexe kplɔla le ʋuwɔwɔme le Brexit megbe, Bizinɛs Ŋuŋlɔla ye gblɔe.
Ega sɔ kpe be kudo nya si Toyota UK glɔna BBC be nenye be Britain dzo le Europe Dekawɔwɔ me le wɔna deke mawɔwɔ me ela tɔte nuwɔmɔnu le eƒe dɔwɔƒe le Burnaston, gogo Derby.
"Mie hiã wɔna de," Aƒetɔ Clark ye gblɔe.
Japantɔ ʋuwɔla gblɔ be kpekpe le megbetsitsi kude dɛa nu le wɔna deke mawɔtɔeme la ana be Brexit ate agu dɔwɔnawo.
Burnaston ƒe asinudɔwɔƒe - si wɔ Toyota Auris kple Avensis - he ʋu abe akpe alafa deka blatɔ̄ vɔ atɔ̄ vɛ le ƒe si vayime si blasieke de alafa dzi ku yi Europa Dekawɔwɔ du kpɔtiawome.
"Nyeƒe nukpɔkpɔ enye be ne Britain dogo le Europa Dekawɔwɔ le dzinu etɔlia ƒe vɔvɔme la mia kpɔ be nuwɔwɔnu atɔ te le miaƒe dɔwɔƒea me," Marvin Cooke, Toyota ƒe nudzikpɔkpɔ Tatɔ le Burnaston ye gblɔe.
UK ƒe ʋuwɔla bubuwo kɔ woaƒe vɔvɔ de dzi kude UK ƒe dzodzo le Europe Dekawɔwɔme le nubabla deke manɔemetɔe kudo aleke dɛ tsotso asitsatsa awɔdɔ do, Honda, BMW kple Jaguar Land Rover le wome.
BMW, abe kpɔdeŋu enē, gblɔ be ela tu eƒe asinudɔwɔƒe vi si le Oxford le dzinu dekame kplɔ Brexit do.
Nya vevietɔwo kude nusi ʋuwɔlawo gblɔ wawoenye gbaxɔxɔ ka ƒe xaxa le esime nyadzilɔlɔ wɔna deke menɔanyi kple Brexit.
Toyota ƒe nuwɔwɔnu ƒe fli le wɔdɔ le "le game" te, kple dɔwɔnuwo ƒe vava le adabaƒoƒo blatɔ vɔ adrē sia me tso nudzralawo gbɔ le UK kple Europa Dekawɔwɔ ƒe du kpɔtiawo me hena ʋu dɔdɔwo wɔwɔ.
Nenye be UK dzo le Europa Dekawɔwɔ le dzinu etɔlia ƒe ŋukeke blave vɔ asieke dzi le dodo deke mawɔmawɔme la, tsakatsaka ate kpɔmɔ le dɛ dzi abe alesi asinudɔwɔƒea le gblɔgblɔm be esia ate he megbetsitsi kple dɔwɔnuwo mademade.
Esia anye nusi mate ŋu ava ma na Toyota be woale wu ŋukeke deka ƒe dɔwɔnuwuwo le eƒe Derbyshire ƒe asinudɔwɔƒeame, dɔwɔƒe gblɔ be alea la nuwɔmɔnuwo atɔ te.
Mr Clark gblɔ be Theresa May ƒe Chequers dodo le ŋugɔ Kadodo kple Europa dekawɔwɔ le dzadzradome pɛpɛ be yeade border mɔxexewo da."
"Mie hiã wɔnade wɔwɔ. Miedzi dodo nyuitɔ keake si la na mɔ mi abe alesi megblɔ vayi enē, menye be miakpɔ dzidzɔ le fifi be dzidzedzekpɔkpɔme o ke boŋu be mia lé mɔnukpɔkpɔ sia de asi.
"Dasedidi sia metso Toyota dedeko gbɔ o ke dɔwɔƒe vovowo hã gbɔ be miedo la nɔ gbesɔsɔe ayiedzi kple nusiwo kata kenye miaƒe agbaxɔxɔ ka ƒe dzidzedze."
Toyota mete gblɔ game si dɔwɔmɔnu dzudzɔ la axɔ o, gake ɣeyiɣi didi ade ye, ka mo be asixɔxɔ bubuwo adidi asinudɔwɔƒea ƒe dɔwɔwɔ nyui kple edɔ bubu wohã.
Peter Tsouvallaris, si wɔdɔ le Burnaston ƒe blave vɔ ene sɔŋ eye enye tatɔ na Unite sɛdikat le asinudɔwɔƒea, gblɔ be etɔwo le nuxam ŋutɔ: Le nye nuteƒekpɔkpɔnu la, zi deka si dɔwɔnawo adzo la ome gale trɔtrɔ ava gbede o.
Dzidudua ƒe nyanudela gblɔ be: "Miedo anyi dodo nyui kple xɔasitɔ na miaƒe ŋkɔgbe dekawɔwɔ kple Europa dekawɔwɔ"
Trump kple Rosenstein ƒe takpekpe aga teyi megbe ke, Aƒe ɣime ye gblɔe
Donald Trump ƒe takpekpe adodoe kple sedɔwɔla gã ƒe gɔmenɔtɔ Rod Rosenstein ate ga "teyi megbe kple kɔsida deka" zi alesi vɔnu gã ƒe ametiatia Brett Kavanaugh ƒe tsitretsitsi gale edzi yim, White House gblɔe le kɔsidagbe dzi.
Rosenstein kpɔna adaŋudela Robert Mueller ƒe dɔwɔna dzi, amesi le nukum tso Russia ƒe akɔdada nyawome, le kadodome kple Trump kple Russiaƒe kpekpedeŋuwo kple dzɔdzɔenyenye ƒe moxenu si ate kpɔeme vava tso dukplɔla gbɔ.
Biabia enye be mia nya nenye be Trump anya sedɔwɔla gã ƒe gɔmenɔtɔ le dɔanu alo o ma eye atsɔ Mueller ƒe ablɔde atsɔ do xaxame, Whashington ƒe nukpoloeƒolawo gblɔ nyasiawo le dzinu ade wome.
Le dzinu sia ƒe gɔmedzedzeme la, New York Times ka nya ta be Rosenstein gblɔ be yedo eka de si ale yeƒe nuƒoƒo kple Trump eye tso ema nua ateŋu ade Dukplɔla le zia dzi le blave vɔ atɔlia ƒe se dzi.
Rosenstein gbe nu le nyala nu.
Dzodagbe si vayi me la, eyi Aƒe ɣime, nyamawo ŋuti la edzi be yea ɖe asi le dɔ ŋu.
Le esia teƒe la, takpekpe kple Trump, si anɔanyi le America le New York, akpɔ eteƒe le Yawudagbe dzi.
Trump gblɔ be "yemedzi" la nya Rosenstein le dɔa dzi o gake takpekpe la teyi megbe be woatsɔ gbe nu le tsitretsitsi ade me si dukɔ ƒe sewɔtakpeƒe kodzodolawo ƒe dekawɔwɔ se kudo Kavanaugh kple nyɔnu ade si samē le gbɔdɔdɔ agbenɔnɔ gblegble ade me, Dr Christine Blasey Ford, wo vea di adase.
Le Fidagbe dzi, Trump de mɔ na FBI ƒe nyagɔmekuku le kɔsida deka me kudo nyasiwo tsiatre de Kavanaugh nu, he sedɔwɔlawo ƒe akɔ yi de megbe ke.
Trump ƒe agbalẽtaƒe ŋuŋlɔla, Sarah Sanders, Zē le Fox News dzi le kɔsidagbe.
Wo biē nya kude Rosenstein ƒe takpekpe ŋu, eye wogblɔ be: "Azã dodo deke mekpɔ li nē o, ela te anye kɔsida sia, mate kpɔa be ate ga teyi megbe le kɔsida dekame ke hado nu bubuwo siwo le dzɔdzɔm de vɔnu gã nu.
Gake mila kpɔ eye me lɔna esiayi ma na nyayeyewo kple agbalētaƒela"
Nyakakala dewo atsiatre de nyagblɔglɔ ma nu: Sanders mewɔ nyakaka kpui deke le Aƒe Ɣime kpɔ o tso kaka dzinu asiekelia ƒe ŋukeke ewo dzi.
Host Chris bia be ŋukata ma.
Sanders gblɔ be nyakaka wɔna kpui mabɔmabɔ meyne be Tivi nyakakatɔ xɔasiwo tsritsri ŋuti o, vɔa egblɔ be: "Nyema gbe lɔlɔ̃ ɖe esia dzi be wodze na amewo ŋu o."
Edo susu da be Trump ƒe gododo kple nyakakatɔwo adzi de edzi.
"Dukplɔla wɔ biabia dodoŋuti takpekpe wu dukplɔla siwo kata do ŋugɔ nē," egblɔe , egatsɔ kpe le ɖasedidi kpɔdeŋu manɔemetɔe: "Miele ŋuku de agbɔsɔsɔmawo ŋu."
Gododo kpuiwo ate gayi edzi, Sanders ye gblɔe, gake " ne nyakakatɔwo kpɔ mɔnu be woa bia nya America dukplɔla ŋutɔ la, ema anyo wu be woaƒo kplim.
Miedza agbagba be miawɔ esia zi gede eye miatɔ mikpɔ abe alesi miewɔdɔ kude esia ŋuti zi gbogbode le kɔsida mamlɛtɔwome eye esia la dɔli nyakaka kpui wɔna teƒe esime miateŋu aƒonu kple America dukplɔla."
Trump xɔna biabiawo esiayime ke wodzo le Aƒe Ɣime alo kpɔa gome le takpekpe alo nyakaka takpekpe kple ameŋukuta gawo ƒe xɔxɔme.
Amedekaha ƒe nyakaka takpekpe mebɔ o.
Le New York le kɔsida siame la dukplɔla ede nukaŋuti, ewɔna vovo zezē kple nyamatɔe le nyakakatɔwo ŋukume.
Lamese ƒe ŋuŋlɔla ŋlɔ nu na Europa Dekawɔwɔ dɔwɔlawo le NHS Scotland kude Brexit ƒe vɔvɔ ŋuti
Lamese ŋuŋlɔla ŋlɔ na Europa Dekawɔwɔ ƒe dɔwɔla siwo le dɔwɔm le Scotland ƒe NHS gblɔ edua ƒe akpedada eye di be woanɔ kame kple Brexit.
Jeane Freeman MSP ŋlɔ agbalē do da awɔ abe dzinu ade fiafia hafi UK dogo le Europa Dekawɔwɔme.
Scotish dzidudua wɔ tiatia be yeadzi mɔnu si ana be Europa Dekawɔwɔ dumeviwo akpɔ dɔ le eƒe dɔwɔƒe adewome.
Le eƒe anyē me la, Aƒenɔ Freeman gblɔ be: "Le dzome ŋɔlime la, nyahehe le UK kple EU le gogodo ƒe nya ŋuti gayi edzi, heyi lɔlɔnu nyatsotsome le nuŋeɣi siame.
Gake UK dzidudua gado ŋusē eƒe dzradzradowo kudo wɔna deke mawɔtɔme.
Menya be esia anye tsakatsaka ɣeyiɣi na mia kata.
Enumata ye medzi la do kpe fifia alesi medo bubu dɔwɔlawo ƒe kpekpedeŋu, meka woaƒe dumetɔnyenye.
Hadɔwɔlawo le Europa Dekawɔwɔa kata me la, kple godo, tsɔ nuteƒekpɔkpɔ kple adaŋu si do ŋusē eye dzra lamese nyawo ƒe dɔwɔwɔ do, eye devi na dɔnɔ kple ameha siwo mie subɔ na.
Scotland nye miaƒe aƒeme esiayi eye miedzi vevie ŋutɔ be mianɔ mia gbɔ."
Wo wɔdɔ na Christion Abercrombie kpatakpatame le eta ƒe abi megbe
Wo wɔdɔ na Tennesse Tigers ƒe bɔlƒola Abercromie kpakpatɔe le ta ƒe abi megbe le Memledagbe ƒe gege 31-27 tsitre do Vanderbilt Commores ŋʋ, Tenessee ƒe Mike ye ka nya ta
Tennesse ƒe bɔlfiɔla gã Rod Reed gblɔna nyakakatɔwo be abi la va eme le gaƒoƒo suē ade mē hafi bɔlƒoƒo akpa gbatɔ la avɔ.
"Eva toto fli dzi eye wowɔ abe ekuƒegni le afima ene," Reed ye gblɔe.
Bɔlƒiɔla kple lamese dɔwɔlawo do gbɔgbɔ na Abercombie hafi kɔkɔ do numlɔdzi eye wokplɔ dogo hena ŋukulele dziyiyi.
Amega de le Tennessee Duame gblɔna Chris Harris tso WSMV gbɔ le Nashvile, Tennessee, be Abercombie dogo le dɔwɔwɔame le Vanderbilt Medical Center.
Haris ga sɔkpe be "nya deke meli kudo abi ƒomevi si wonye alo abi ƒe kekeme fifi o" eye Tennessee Dua le agbagba dzem be yeanya gakeme abi wɔe.
Abercrombie, awudzē ƒe eve sukukɔkɔ nusrɔvi, le eƒe ɣeyiɣi gbãtɔ kple Tennesse Duame le eƒe ʋuʋu dzole Ilinois megbe.
Ewɔ bɔltsotso nyui zi atɔ hafi wodogo le fefeme, esi wɔe be wowɔ bɔltsotso nyui zi woenyi le eƒe ɣeyiɣime.
Amedzro nuƒlelawo do la xɔ mɔdede ƒe agbalē xɔasi ade le esime woƒle aƒe le UK
Amedzro nuƒlelawo axɔ mɔdede gbalē xɔasi ade le esime woƒle aƒe le UK kple gã kpekpe siwo zãna tsɔ kpe na de amesiwo medo aƒe woŋu le Tory ƒe dodo yeye la gɔme
Nyametsotso sia agble Corbyn ƒe lɔlɔnu dzidzedze be yale dzi na dekpui akɔdalawo
Mɔdede gbalē fɔfɔ azi de amesiwo metuna adzɔ le UK ŋuti
Gadzradoƒe kpɔmɔna esia be ate he ga miliɔn alafa deka blave euro ga vɛ le ƒe dekame atsɔ kpe de amesiwo medo aƒe o ŋuti
Amedzro nuƒlelawo axɔ mɔdede gbalē xɔasi ade le esime woƒle aƒe le UK kple gã kpekpe siwo zãna tsɔ kpe na de amesiwo medo aƒe woŋu le Tory ƒe dodo yeye la gɔme
Wɔna la anɔ abe agbagbadzedze atsɔ gblē Jeremy Corbyn ƒe lɔlɔnu dzidzedze atsɔ le dzi na tekakpui kɔdalawo kple ŋgbedodo be ya di aƒe maxɔasi na amewo kple vide gawo lele.
Mɔdede gbalē sia azi de amewo kple asitsahawo siwo metuna adzɔ o le UK, kple ga kpekpe atsɔ kpe de dzidudua ƒe lɔlɔnu be ya ʋli mɔme mlɔmlɔ.
Adzɔ dzikpekpe - si le kpe mɔdede gbalē, agbɔsɔsɔ gã hehevɛ le dzinu eve megbe do aƒe vewo dzi kple aƒe ɣaɣawo dzi - ate yi sɔgbɔ abe etɔ de alafadzi.
Gadzradoƒe kpɔ mɔ na wɔna siabe woate he ga miliɔn alafa deka blave vē le ƒe deka me
Mie bui be amesiwo mele UK ƒle woetɔ de alafa dzi le aƒe yeyewo le London, asiga wo yɔyɔ awɔebe asese na nuƒlela gbãtɔwo be woada afɔ do aƒe ƒe atrakpui dzi.
Etsi teƒe gbogbodewo le duame - vevietɔ le dugãme - trɔ zu "ŋɔli duwo" hado amedzro gbogbodewo siwo ƒle aƒewo gake le woaƒe agbe wɔm le duta.
Dodo yeye sia vame le kɔsida dewokome si Boris Johson wɔ yɔyɔ na mɔdede gbalē ƒe asididi gamea woate akpe de dekakpuiwo siwo dzi lado woaƒe aƒe gbãtɔ.
Etsɔ nyadé xɔtutu dɔwɔƒe gãwonu siwo kpɔtɔ kɔ aƒe ƒleƒletsi de dzi tsɔ le ƒle anyigbawo gake omele wozam o, eye wɔ yɔyɔ na aƒenɔ May be dzudzɔ gakpekpe de aƒewo dzi gamea ne woadzra Britain ƒe "aƒe ŋukpenyawo" do.
Aƒetɔ Corbyn degbefã ŋkulele de aƒe ƒe wɔna vovowo ƒe trɔtrɔ, xɔfetu dzikpɔkpɔ kple nuwuwu hena menyanya le xɔ hayawome kuɣi manɔtɔe.
Edzi be yeana dukɔdzikpɔlawo hã ŋusē gã de woatu aƒe yeyewo.
Aƒenɔ May gblɔ be: Le ƒe mamlɛtɔmela me gblɔ be makɔ nye ƒe dudɔnunɔla gbãtɔ nɔƒenyenye atsɔ dzra Britishtɔwo ƒe drɔwo do - bena agbe nanyo na dzidzime yeyewo sia.
Eye esia gɔme enye xɔ ƒe asi gblegblewo dzadrado.
Britain lanɔ esiayi ʋuʋu na amesiwo dzi lanɔ, wɔdɔ eye awɔ woaƒe agbe le fi.
Gake, mateŋʋ anɔ dzɔedzɔe be woanɔ fafa na amesiwo mele UK, medzro dɔwɔƒewo, be woaƒle aƒe abe dɔwɔla sēsē British nɔlawo enē.
Le amegbogbodewo ƒe drɔe be yɔado aƒe trɔ zu nu didiade, eye bubu mademade ƒe mɔwo mlɔmlɔ kpɔtɔ nye nyateƒe.
Jack Ross: "Nye dzidzi mamlɛtɔ enye be makpɔ Scotland dzi"
Sunderland ƒe amega Jack Ross gblɔ eƒe"dzidzi mamlɛtɔ enye be woanye Scotland ƒe dzikpɔla le doƒe adewo.
Scotɔ, ƒe blanē vɔ eve, do dzidzi be yeafɔ North-East hala, ke fifia le xɔ teƒe etɔlia le liga deka, kpɔtɔ dzesi etɔ xɔxɔ be woanɔ edzi.
Edzole le Light fefewɔƒe le dzome ɣeyiɣime kple St Mirren kplɔkplɔ yi de Scotɔwo ƒe dudɔnunɔla gbatɔ gbɔ le ƒe xoxome.
"Medzi be maƒo bɔlna nye dua abe bɔlƒola enē.
Mexɔ Kuku B ko, Ross gblɔna BBC Scotland ƒe Sportsound.
"Gake metsi kple Scotland kpɔkpɔ le Hampden ŋutɔ kple efonye abe vifē enē, eye enye si kplɔnam va megbe esiayi.
Mɔnukpɔkpɔ ma ava nenye be mekpɔ dzidzedze nyui le ha dzikpɔkpɔme dede ko.
Amesiwo de ŋugɔ na Ross abe Sunderland dzikpɔla enē woenye Dick Avocaat, David Moyes,Sam Allardyce, Martin O'Neill, Roy Keane, Gus Poyet kple Paulo Di Canio.
Aloa Athleticƒe amegã xoxoa gblɔ be mekpɔ gɔmesese deke le ŋukɔ xɔasiwo kplɔkplɔdo abe habɔbɔ gawo, le essime wogbe ŋugɔdodo na Barnsley kple Ipswich Town.
Le gbɔnye la, dzidudu le gaƒoƒo siame atso nukpɔkpɔ sia gbɔ" mate kplɔ ha sia ayi de Premier League?"
Hado nuwo ƒe nɔnɔme kpe mɔnukpɔkpɔwo le ha siame, anye Premier League tɔ vɔvɔ deke manɔemetɔe,"eye gblɔe.
"Menye edɔvi wonyi be ado afima o, gake mate kpɔa dokuinye abe dzidzedzetɔ la afisia nenye be mate gatrɔ ha sia va afisia."
Ross wɔ ƒe etɔ ko le eƒe dzikpɔkpɔdɔme le ɣeyiɣi si ewɔ le Dumbarton abe ha ƒe dzikpɔla gɔmenɔtɔ kple dzinu woatɔ si ewɔ le Heart ƒe Bɔl fialawo ƒe dɔwɔtɔwo dome.
Emegbe la ekpe de Alloa ŋu tso eƒe gegeme atrɔ xɔ eƒe doƒe tɔlia, eye trɔ St Mirren tso gege flidzi yi dzidula ŋukɔxɔxɔ le ƒe si vayi ƒe ʋliʋli me.
Eye Ross gblɔ be yekpɔ akɔfafa fifi wu ga sime yenye bɔlƒola le Clyde, Hartlepool, Falkrik,St Mirren kple Hamilton Academical.
"Mɔdogoƒe vavã wonye" eɖo ŋku edzi, Alloa dzikpɔkpɔdɔ xɔxɔ.
"Medoe dzesi vavã be dzikpɔkpɔdɔ yedze nam, wu bɔlƒoƒo.
Ewɔ moya gake mewɔ avu nyuie, si na be mekpɔ agbe si nu mesusu eye mele dzidzɔkpɔm le doƒe kɔkɔwo dzi.
Gake, bɔlƒoƒo sēsē.
Nugedewo li si miedo la to wome le kɔsidame.
Mega kpɔtɔ to na nusiawome nuxaxa kple dɔa ƒe dzizizi gake dzikpɔkpɔdɔ nyo nunye.
Mekedzi esiayi be makpɔ nu dzi eye fifia mele ewɔm, mekpɔ akɔfafa le nye lamē le nye tsitsi agbewome kata"
Miate doto nyamedzodzro kata le Sportsound, le Memledagbe, dzinu asiekelia ƒe ŋukeke blatɔ dzi, le Scotland redio dzi le ga woeve kɔyi ga dekame BST.
Game adodoe hena dzidzenu enye ga atɔ̃ ku afa le fiēsime le Memleda ŋukeke dzi, abe alesi ŋukukua gblɔe enē.
Dzome ŋɔli ƒe dzodzo sēsē yɔ asi de Britain ƒe ahanoƒe ʋliʋli gake ƒoƒu dzizizi de nuduƒe kawodzi.
Ahanoƒe kple fiɔse habɔbɔwo kpɔ nusasa ƒe kɔkɔ yi dzi 2.7 de alafa dzi le dzinu adrēliame gake nuduƒewo didi 4.8 de alafa dzi, abe alesi nɔnɔme defia enē.
Peter Martin, Nudzadzra ƒe adaŋudela le CGA, si de nɔnɔme sia fia, gblɔ be : Ɣe dziyiyi kple England ƒe kpekpedeŋu didia na Xexea Bɔlƒoƒo wu ale wobia na be dzinu adrelia kplɔ dzinu adelia le kpɔdeŋu dekame, esime hanoƒe fɔ dzi 2.8 de alafa dzi, tovo nuduƒe si nu ƒo sēsē.
Nuduƒe asitsatsa gege 1.8 le afafa dzi le dzinu adelia ga gble de edzi le dzinu adrelia dzi.
Ahanoƒe kple ahafiɔsewo wɔdɔ tso fifia sēsē le asi dekawome kɔkɔ wu nuduƒeƒe si didi la.
Nududu hanoƒe wotsa kpe fu le ɣe me, gake me sēsê abe nuduƒe dɔwɔƒewo enē o.
Ewɔ abe amewo doago na aha dedeko ta.
Le hanoƒe kple fiɔse kata dzikpɔkpɔme la, ha dzadzra fɔ dzi abe 6.6 de alafa dzi."
Paul Newman, vovokpɔkpɔ kple amedzroƒe ƒe numedrotɔ le RSM gblɔ be: "Numetsotsowo yiedzi alea miekpɔ tso dzinu enelia ƒe vɔvɔme.
Yame ƒe nɔnɔme kple amehawo alo lamesēfefe ƒe wɔna vevietɔwo kpɔtɔ nye mɔnu gãwo na asitsatsa le gota.
Mewɔ yaa be nuduƒe habɔbɔwo kpɔtɔ le aʋuwɔm o, nenye be nusasa didi 4.8 le alafa dzi le ƒe sia de ƒe si gbɔna dzi la ɖea fu ŋutɔ kudo asixɔxɔ dzizizi esiayitɔe.
Dzome ŋɔli didia kple dzodzo sɔŋ make nye ɣeyiɣi bara na dɔwɔla siwo le nududu ƒe akpa dzi o eye ɣeyiɣi la gblɔe na mi ne dzodzo ƒe didi si miekpɔ le dzinu enyiliame ahe trɔtrɔ si miehã vɛ na mia."
Nusasa kata ƒe agbɔsɔsɔ le ahanoƒe kple nuduƒewo, nusaƒe yeyewo hã, enye 2.7 le aladzi le dzinu adrelia me, fia dzesiwo ƒe gblagbla.
Coffer Peach Tracker asinudɔwɔwɔ ƒe nusasa dɔwɔla si kpɔna UK ƒe ahanoƒe, fiɔse kple nuduƒe ƒe nyawo dzi ƒoƒu eye kunume tso agbadzedze nyawo nu tso dɔwɔwɔ habɔbɔ blanēvɔ adrē gbɔ, kple dɔwɔwɔ tsi ƒoƒu biliɔn asieke ƒands gã, eye wonɔanyi le asinudɔwɔwɔwo kata ta.
Deka le devi atɔ̃ do kame mɔnuwo ƒe ametɔnyenye si woxla de woa dzilawo.
Deka le devi atɔ̃ - dewo suē abe ƒe woedeka - do kame mɔnu ƒe ametɔnyenye si woxla de woa dzilawo kple woaƒe nuƒialawo, numekukuwo defia.
Numekuku tso sɛkɛndry sukuvi akpe blave defia "Insta axa gblegble" sɔgbɔ ɖewo
Nyasia kɔ vɔvɔwo de dzi bena gbɔdɔdɔ nuwo le kaka
Blave de alafadzi sukuviwo gblɔ be yodo nane ƒomenyenye vevietɔ atsɔ fiɔ wodzilawo
Deka le devi atɔ̃ - dewo abe ƒe woedeka - le ʋu kame mɔnu ƒomenyenye si woxla de ametsitsiwo.
Numekuku tso sɛkɛndry sukuvi akpe blave de kaba kaba gbɔsɔsɔ fia le Insta gblegble ametɔnyenye - le kame kple foto mamã nɔƒe Instagram.
Nyasiawo kɔ vɔvɔ de dzi be gbɔdɔdɔ nuwo le kaka.
Blave de alafa dzi sukuviwo gblɔ wowɔ dɔ kple dedie ametɔnyenye si wotsɔna fiana wodzilawo, le esime wodo tɔxɛwo hã.
Enɔ de dze evia nyɔnuvi ƒe woetɔ ƒe kame nɔƒe xlaxla dzi tete wokpɔ detugbuivi de si le wɔwɔ yɔyɔ na amewo be woava do "aʋu kpli."
Nudzodzro, tso Digital Awareness UK kple sukudzikpɔla ŋutsu kple nyɔnu" Conference (HMC) tso suku siwo le wodokui sinu, kpɔ blanē de alafa dzi le ƒe woedeka yide ƒe woenyi do amenyenye ve, kple ame afã dewo siwo lɔ be yodo ametɔnyenye tɔxɛwo.

Wo tia Eilidh Doyle abe Scorttish duƒulawo ƒe dzikpɔlavi le tatɔwo ƒe ƒe takpetakpe gãme.
Doyle nye Scotland ƒe duƒula si xɔ atsɔdodo wu eye ganye Ian Beattie ƒe amegã kafu nyatsoyso sia abe mɔnukpɔkpɔ gãde na amesiwo le kplɔ lãmesēfefe be woakpɔ gome le eƒe nuteƒekpɔkpɔ gã le dukɔ vovo me.

Doyle be: "Me lɔ be matsɔ dɔ abe duƒulawo ƒe gbe eye mele mɔkpɔm be mate wɔdɔ akpe de mia ŋʋ vavã eye makpe de Scotland ƒe lamesēfefe kplɔkplɔ."

Notsi gbɔgbɔ ƒe gbefadede si le sɔ enɔwo kple enyiwo mã susuwo le kame
Notsi gbɔgbɔ dwɔƒe de mã susuwo le kame kple gbefãdede si sɔ nɔ siwo nanɔ viwo kple nyi si hã na notsi via.
Be woatsɔ do dzesi gododo na nya siwo gblɔ be enye "dodoezizi notsitɔ gbatɔ le xexeame", tɛknolodzi dɔwɔƒe Elvie de asi le gbefãdede afetɔ ade le nɔnɔmetata nu be woade fia amewo vovo si pɔmp yeye la na enɔ si wogblɔe
Enɔ ŋutɔtɔ enē dewo du ɣe le gbeƒuƒu yɔ kple nyi ƒe ava le hadzidzi de dzi si be nyawo nye esia: "Ɛ, me nanɔ dokuinye, gake nye medo asike o," eye "nenye be mime doa dzesi o la esiawo menye lãno o, wonye anɔwo"
Hadziha yi na edzi be: "Gbɔe, gbɔe, mele nududu na nye vidziwo, gbɔe gbɔe , mele na no, mele dzra nye nyɔnuwo do"
Ke hã la, gbeƒãdede, si wo kaka le dɔwɔƒe ƒe Facebook axa dzi la, na nyahehe le kame.
Kple ame akpe bladrē vɔ asieke si kpɔe kple nutsotso alafawo, nɔnɔmetata sia xɔ wɔna vovowo tso nukpɔlawo gbɔ, kple ame gedewo siwo gblɔ be esi dzo de notsidzaƒe asinudɔwɔwɔ ƒe "ŋɔdziwo" ŋu.
" numetsotso digbɔ ŋutɔ, za nyiwo akɔ degbefã na asitsanu sia.
Abe miawo enē, wodo la afɔ fu eye adzi vi alea be woawɔ notsi, tovo be woaƒe viwo nɔna fifim le wasi le ŋukeke adewo ƒe vidzidzi megbe," ameade xlɔ.
Elvie notsi gbɔgbɔ sɔ le bebeme kple no wu ade si wokɔ nana ano vi (Elvie/Mother)
Amebu na nutsotso: "Gɔmesese tsatsaka na nyɔnu kple vidzie sia.
Gake ɛ, ŋukata woma zãwo akɔ adegbefã notsi gbɔgbɔ na enɔ siwo dzi la kpɔ woa viwo dzi o ma?
Amebu sɔ kpe: "Abe gbefãdede madevi de."
Ame bubuwo ɖe gbefãdedea dzi, kple nyɔnu ade si lɔ̃ be ye kpɔ ha la abe "nudikokoe."
"Me buibe atsu alo asi ƒe susu ye.
Meke le deka doge nenye be mega kpɔtɔ le na ano vi.
Ano gbɔgbɔ wɔnanam pɛpɛ abe nyi enē.
Gbefãdede sia le fuflui vide gake metsɔe alea wole enē.
Asitsatsanu nyiuiade wonye," amede ŋlɔ.
Amebu na numetsotso: Esianye nukokoe gbefãdede dzidze tu ɖe enɔ siwo gbɔna anotsi (enuenu le dɔwɔƒewome alo kpɔhawome) eye wo di na "nyiwo" enē.
Esia menye notsidzraƒe ƒe asinudɔwɔwɔ ƒe kafufu alo ʋɔnudrɔdrɔ ƒe gbefãdede ye o."
Le nɔnɔmetata megbe la, nyɔnu habɔbɔwo defia be woakata le ɣe dum kple pɔmp xlaxla le woaƒe ano wu wome.
Susu si le megbe na gbefãdede sia nɔte do nukpɔkpɔnu kudo nyɔnu gedewo siwo gbɔ ano de pɔmp me gblɔna yewo lese le lame abe nyiwo ene.
Elvie Pɔmp ke hã la, le ɖoɖoezizi keakeme, medo gaka alo tsile o eye sɔ le bebeme kple no wu si wotsɔ nano vi, nana nyɔnuwo vovo be woa ʋa, le woviwo eye woateŋu ado go le esime wole notsi gbɔm.

Tsatsa devi alafawo ʋuʋu fafatɔe yi kamp gbadɔwome le Texas dɛ dzi
Tsatsa deviwo si wole de anyi ƒe xlexleme yi dzi togbɔ be dɛ tsotso kpɔtɔ de kple de matrɔmatrɔ, hado amiɖeɖe nya ŋu kple dodo sēsē si Trump kɔva la wɔe wosese be woakpɔ amesiwo ade megbe na deviwo.
Le dodoame, megbedela sɔgbɔtɔwo ŋutɔ hã nye amedzro siwo medo agbalē o, eye wole vɔvɔm be yoatsɔ yewoƒe ŋutete si na yewo kpɔtɔ le duame tsɔ do xaxa me nenye be yewo wɔ azɔli be yɔa xɔ devi ade.
Xaxa sɔgbɔ de edzi le dzinu adelia me, esime dekawɔwɔ megawo degbefã be megbedela vavãwo kple ametsitsi bubuwo le woaƒe aƒewome atsɔ woaƒe asi dzesiwo vɛ, eye be nyawo lanɔ mamã kple amedzronya megawo.
Kɔsida mamlɛtɔ, Matthew Albence, tsitsi megã le amedzonya kple Kɔnuwo Amezizi, didase le takpkpe bena dɔwɔƒe lé ame woevevo siwo wɔ biabia na megbedede na devi suewo si womedo ameadeke o.
Dɔwɔƒea, le emegbe la na ŋusēsēdo be bladrē de alafadzi tso amesiwo lé womedo amewuwu ƒe wɔna deke o.
"Abe blanyi de alafa dzi tso ameha siwo nye megbedelawo alo megbedelawo ƒe aƒemetɔwo le duame manɔsenutɔe, eye akpa gã le ameha me la nye amewula medzrowo.
Ke miele edzi yim le kplɔ ameha mawo do," Aƒetɔ Albence ye gblɔe.

Amesiwo wobu madzemadze na kpekpedeŋu woatrɔ wo kabakaba.

Syria gblɔ na America, French kple Turkish ŋusēwo be woaɖe ɖa fifila
Le ƒonu na Dukɔ Dekawɔwɔ ƒe Takpekpe Gã, Dudɔnunɔla si kpɔna Amedzonyawo gbɔ, Walid al-Moualem wɔ yɔyɔ na Syrian sisilawo be woatrɔ agbɔ va aƒeme, togbɔbe edua ƒe aʋawɔwɔ le eƒe ƒe anyi me.
Moualem, si tsɔ dɔ abe dudɔnulagã ƒe gometɔ, gblɔ be amedzro ŋusēwo le Syrian nyigbadzi masɔmasɔe, kudo susu be yewo le wɔ aʋa kple ŋɔdziwɔlawo, "eye wola wɔ kpliwo abe alesi wo susui."
"Wodo laʋu dzo fifila eye wɔna deke manɔemetɔe,"egblɔna takpetakpea.
Moualem tegbe de dzi gblɔ be "ŋɔdzi ʋala vɔ hã vɔ" le Syria, fisi ame wu akpe alafa deka blade ku tso kaka ƒe akpe eve kple woedeka, kple ame miliɔnwo si ʋudzo le woaƒeme.
Egblɔ be Damascus ayidzi "wɔ ava vevie sia vasede esime mie trɔ ɖɔ Syrian duwo tso ŋɔdzi habɔbɔ kple amedzro anyinɔnɔ masɔmasɔe."
Srafowo akpeve tso United State wole Syria dukɔme be wɔana hehe kple aɖo aɖaŋu na Kurdish srafo kple Syrian Arabs tɔwo si tsi atitre ɖe dukplɔla Bashar al-Assad ŋuti.
France srafowo ƒe xexleme awu akpeɖeka le aʋawɔdukɔɖewome.
Kuɖe aʋasilawo nyaŋua, Moualem gblɔ be fifia fafa li azɔ eyata aʋasilawo wuateŋu agbɔ, ebufɔ yevudukɔ aɖewo be wɔawoe kaka vɔvɔ madeamedzi mawoe vɛ.
Egblɔ be, Woyɔ ablotsi dukɔwo kple lɔlɔnufa habɔbɔwo be woate ŋu awɔe be aʋasilawo na gbɔ.
Wo tsɔ dunyahehe nyawo kɔɖo nusi nye lɔlɔnufa nyawo ŋu.
United State kpe ƒuƒoƒo aɖewo tso Europe dukɔme ɖegblɔ be, kpekpeɖeŋu dɔwɔna ɖeke mayi edzi le Syria dukɔme o vaseɖe sime dunyahehe ɖekawɔwɔ va Assad kple amesiwo tsi atitre ɖeŋu.
UN ƒe amega dɔdɔwo le gbeta gblɔɛ be nugɔmesese si Rusiatɔwo kple Turkeytɔwo wɔ fifia ɖokpe dzi le nugbegble wɔla akuaku wo ƒe nɔƒe le Idlib na mɔnukpɔkpɔ dunyahehe nyawo.
Rusia kple Turkey tɔwo ƒe wɔna tsi afɔku geɖewo nu esime Rusia tɔwo da megbe na Syria srafowo le teƒea si ame miliɔni etɔ sɔŋ le
Mlɔeba la, Moualem tegbeɖedzi he gblɔe be, seɖoƒe li na nugɔme sesea eye wo gblɔɛ kple kakaɖedzi be asrafowo akɔ woƒe wɔnawo akpe Jihadistɔwo kple dzrewɔlawo si tso Al-Qaeda to Nusra ƒe ŋkume be woaɖewo ɖa.
UN medɔdɔ Steffan de Mistura kaɖedi be madidi o dziɖuɖu kple emeyiwo tsi atitre ɖewo ŋu ƒe amewo kpakple kɔmiti yeye sia woɖokpe wɔawɔ takpekpe gbatɔ be wɔawɔ aʋawɔwɔ megbe se na Syria be wɔateŋu ada kɔ.
Moualem ɖokpe naɖewo dzi na Syria dziɖuɖua le woƒe dɔwɔna le kɔmitia me hegblɔ be wɔaɖoasi ametiatiawo ƒe dɔwɔnawo dzi be wɔagbugbɔ aleŋku ɖe se yeye si wowɔ la ŋu eye kɔyi edzia, amebubua ɖeke madenu eme o.

Dumega siwo nye “administratawo” ɖe eme le dzinu atseke ƒe memama me be yewodi be dumegawo ƒe tapkekpea na yi edzi eye newoa ɖe tohehe ɖe EI Salvador dzi.

Esiata Amerika ƒe afɔdomenɔ etɔawo gbugbɔ trɔ yi EI Salvadot, Panama kple Dominican Republic eye womele enya yeye sesẽ alo tohehe adeke tso Washington.

Graham Dorrans nye aboƒola na Rangers abo ƒo ha be, dziɖuɖu kakaɖedzi le yesi hena gododo kple Rapid Vienna abo ƒo ha.
Rangers abo ƒo ha anɔ aƒe ado woezɔ na Rapid Vienna abo ƒo ha le nyanya me be dziɖuɖu na yewoa, ana ɖoƒe aɖe si awɔe be yewoa kpɔ ŋgɔyiyi le Europa ƒe aboƒoƒo me le hatsotso G me le esime woda dasɔe kple Villarreal abo ƒo ha le Spain dukɔ me le ɣleti sia ƒe gɔme dzedze me.
Le abi si woxɔ ɖe eƒe klo ta, Graham Dorrans si nye dome ƒo a na Rangers abo ƒo ha meteŋu ƒo abo zigbatɔ vaseɖe esime wo da dasɔe kple Villarreal abo ƒo ha, gake exɔese be Rangers abo ƒo ha aza hoʋiʋlia ƒe metsonu atsɔawɔ nugɔme dzedze hena nugawo wɔwɔ.
Ke eɖe gblɔ be, dasɔea nye nye dzesi nyuie aɖe na yewo elabena, Villarreal nye abo ƒo ha nyuie aɖe.
Mie geɖe abo ƒoƒoa me kple kakaɖedzi be miaɖudzi gake mie kpɔ dzesi ɖeka tso eme.
Ɖewomahi mia teŋu aɖu dzi hafi le nuwuwua, gake le wo kata mea, dasɔea nye metsonu nyuie aɖe.
Nyateƒe mea, wodze agbagba wu mi le akpa gbatɔ eyata, miawo ha miehe adodo le akpa evelia eye le nuwuwua, miawoe nye akpa si dze agbagba wu.

Le mɔkpɔkpɔ me la, mίate ŋu akpɔ dzesi etɔ gake anye kametete sesẽ ŋutɔ elabena woƒe hoʋiʋli si va yi la metsonu nyo gake, ne zi la da megbe na mί ko, meka ɖe edzi be mίa te ŋu ado ŋusẽ nu akpɔ emetsonu nyui.
Ƒe si va yi la tɔ sesẽ, nusianu si dzɔ la kple nu vevi si wɔm la domi kpakple tɔtrɔ siwo va eme le nye bɔluƒoha ŋutɔ hã me la, gake vivisese aɖe le teƒea azɔ.
Ame siwo wotia la nyo eye bɔluƒolawo le vivi sem vavã; hehe si woxɔ la nyo.
Le mɔkpɔkpɔ me la, mίate ŋu ayi dzi ado ŋusẽ nu azɔ, aŋlɔ ɣeyiɣi si va yi la be ahakpɔ dzidzedze.
Nyɔnuwo mele alɔ dɔm o ɖe dzudzɔ xɔxɔ gadzadzraɖo ƒe vɔvɔ ta
Togbɔ be numekuku la menɔlawo nya nu ku ɖe ale si wodi be woalé be na wo ŋu nyuie hã la, ame ʋɛe aɖewo nɔa nu ƒom tso eŋuti na woƒe ƒometɔwo.
Abe ame siwo le numekuku la me le Dukɔ blibo la me ƒe afã gblɔ be yewo nɔa nu ƒom na yewo srɔwo tso lãmesẽ menɔnɔ ɣeyiɣi didi ƒe home ŋuti.
Ame 10 ɖe alafa dzi koe gblɔ be yewo ƒo nu tso eŋu na yewo viwo.

Afi siae nadze egɔme le.
Ƒo nu na wὸ kpeɖeŋutɔ kple ɖeviawo: Mate ŋu adzra wὸ ƒome ɖo be woalé be na wὸ nenye be mena wonya wὸ didiwo do ŋgɔ o.
Wɔ dɔ wὸ aɖaŋuɖola kple wὸ ƒome be miadzro teƒe kple ale si woalé be na wὸe la me, elabena tiatia mawo ate ŋu anye nu vevi si afia asi ga si woaxɔ.
Kplɔ wὸ gaɖaŋuɖola vɛ: Wὸ aɖaŋuɖola ate ŋu akpe ɖe ŋu wὸ hã be nate ŋu agblɔ mɔ si dzi nato axe nu mawo negblẽ la ƒe fewo.
Afi si nakpɔ ga le na wὸ dzikpɔkpɔ ɣeyiɣi didi la tiatia ate ŋu alɔ ɣeyiɣi didi ƒe ametakpɔɖoɖo si le miade la, hybrid cash-value gbetakpɔɖoɖo ɖe eme be wὸakpe ɖe ŋu wὸ axe fe siawo alo wὸ ŋutɔ nakpɔ ɖokui wὸ ta kple wὸ nunɔmesiwo – zi ale si ke ga le asiwὸ.
Dze agbagba naɖe wὸ segbalẽwo ɖe go: Ɖe asi le sekametete ŋu ne wὸadze gɔme.
Di health-care proxy da ɖe eteƒe bena nate ŋu adi asi na ame si dzi naka ɖo la be wὸakpɔ wὸ atike hiãhiã gbɔ na wὸ bena wὸate ŋu awɔ ɖe ɖoɖo si dze la dzi le nu siwo nye wὸ didi la ŋu nenye be mate ŋu aƒo nu o.
Gawu la, bu segbalẽ si ɖe mɔ be ame bubu nawɔ dɔ na wὸ le wὸ ganyawo me la ŋu.
Edze be natia ame si dzi neka ɖo la be wὸawɔ tiatia na wὸ le wὸ ganyawo me eye wὸakpɔ gbɔ be yexe wὸ fewo nenye be mate ŋu awɔ naneke na ɖokui wὸ o.
Megaŋlɔ nu vivivi siwo hiã la be o: Tsɔe ko be dziwὸla tsitsi hiã dɔyɔƒe yiyi kpata eye wὸle mɔ dzi yina dɔyɔƒe.

ŋutsu si kpɔ afɔkua, anɔ eƒe ƒe blane me sɔŋ le Oxford Grove si e IIfracombe, Devon esime wo da akɔta, dɔme kple abɔ nɛ.
Kpovitɔwo ɖe tudada si dzɔ le ga eve kple afa me gblɔ be enye nu ko dzɔ menye le ɖoɖo ɖeke me o.
Afɔkukpɔla mekpɔ amesi dɛ o.
Eƒe abiwo menye nusi ɖeƒu na eƒe agbe o eye kpovitɔwo ɖe kuku na nuteƒekpɔlawo be woava ɖi ɖase.
Anyigbaʋuʋuwo kple esi dzɔna ɖe tɔme sia dzɔ le Indonesia dukɔme.
Anyigbaʋuʋu sesie aɖe kple tɔme tɔ sia wu amewo si woƒe xexleme manɔ vi wu alafa etɔ, blanyi vɔ ene(384) le Indonesia dukɔme le Palu le fiɖa gbe eye nunɔlawo gblɔ be kukulawo yi dzi.
Esime woɖe nuƒoƒowo ɖa, nunɔlawo si kpɔ gbɔdzɔe meteŋu kpɔ nutsotso aɖeke tso Donggala regency gbɔ o sinye teƒe si le Palu ƒe dziehe si teɖe 7.5 kpepkeme teƒe siwo anyigbaʋuʋu na le vevie.
Ame xexleme si wu akpe wuiade(16,000) sɔŋ ʋu le Palu esime afɔku la dzɔ.
Esiawo nye nyateƒe vevi aɖewo kuɖe Palu kple Donggala si le Sulawsi ƒe tɔdome.
Palu nye kapita citi na Sulawesi nutome si le Sulawesi tɔdome ɣetoɖoƒe si le nuwuƒe mɔ miamia la dzi eye le eƒe akpe eve kple wuidre(2017) me la, amewo ƒe xexleme anɔ akpe alafa etɔ bladre vɔ asieke, alafa enyi (379,800).
Eduametɔwo ɖuna ŋkeke bla ene za tsɔ ɖoa ŋku anyigbaaʋuʋu si dzɔ kple esiawo dzɔ ɖe tɔwo me dzi.
Donggala nye regency si keke wu didime si anɔ abe kilomita alafa etɔ to tsia nu yi Sulawesi tɔdome si le dziehe ɣetoɖoƒe.
Le eƒe akpe eve kple wuidre(2017) me la, regency nye du lolo le nutoame si eƒe amewo xexleme anɔ abe akpe alafa eve bla asieke vɔ asieke, alafa eve (299,200) sɔŋ.
Tɔƒoƒo kple agbledede woe nye dɔwɔna gobui si le Sulawesi ƒe titina gɔlɔguiwo me vivietɔ le Donggala ƒe tɔnuwo.
Tomenu si wo yɔna be Nickel kuku ha le vivie le nutoma me gake edeha ɖe Morowali si dze ŋgɔ Sulawesi ƒe tɔnu.
Le habɔbɔ si kpɔ na afɔkunyawo gbɔ le Indonesia dukɔme ƒe nyanua, le eƒe alafa ɖeka si va yia, tɔme nyigbaʋuʋuwo geɖe dzɔ le Palu kple Donggala.
Le eƒe akpe ɖeka alafa asieke bla etɔ vɔ enyi(1938) me, tɔmenyigbaʋuʋu wu amewo za eye woƒe xexleme awu alafa eve eye xɔwo kaka wu alafawo le Donggala.
Tɔmenyigbaʋuʋu le Donggala ɣetoɖoƒe le ƒe akpe ɖeka alafa asieke bla asieke vɔ ade(1996) me si wɔe be ame asieke bu woƒe agbe.
Woakpɔ Indonesia dukɔ le afi si anyigbaʋuʋu na le kabakaba.
Anyigbaʋuʋu sesea aɖe kple tɔme tɔwo sia dzɔ le ƒe si vayi me nye siawo:
Akpe eve kple ene(2004). Anyigbaʋuʋu sesie aɖe si dzɔ le Indonesia Aceh ɣetoɖoƒe tɔnu golɔguiwo me le Sumatra dziehe le ƒoave ŋkeke bla eve vɔ adea me wɔe be tɔme tɔ ha dzɔ le dukɔ wuiene(14) me hewu amewo si woƒe xexleme nye akpe alafa eve bla eve vɔ ade(226000) sɔŋ to India tɔsisi la nu eye wo sɔgbɔ wu afa si dzɔ le Aceh.
Akpe eve kple atɔ(2005). Le tɔdoxe nuwuwu kple afɔfiɛ gɔme dzedze me la, anyigbaʋuʋu sesie zigeɖe le Sumatra ɣetoɖoƒe tɔnuwo.
Ame alafawo ku le Nias tɔdome, to Sumatra tɔnuwo.
Akpe eve kple ade(2006). Kpekpeme ɖe si nye 6.8 va dze Java anyiehe afisi nye Indonesia tɔdome si amewo sɔgbɔ wua, wɔe be tɔmenyigba ha ʋuʋu le anyiehe tɔnuwo hewu amewo si woƒe xexleme teɖe alafa adre sɔŋ.
Fe akpe eve kple asieke Anyigba wuwu le du has Ade si the de panda nu si Fe kpekpe le 7. 6 le Sumatra Fe yedzefe du ga me
Amen Wu akpedeka ku
Fe akpe eve kple ewo 7.5 anyigbãʋuʋu ƒe kpekpeme si dzɔ ɖe Mentawai tɔdomekpowo dometɔ ɖeka dzi la, si le adzɔge na Sumatra, le atiaƒu ƒe ameɖeɖe hem vɛ va se ɖe mita 10 si gbã kɔƒe geɖewo eye wὸwu ame siwo ƒe gbɔsɔsɔ te ɖe 300 ŋu la.
2016: Anyigbãʋuʋu vi aɖe si dzɔ le Pidie Jaya nutome le Aceh la, he gbegbẽ kple dzodzonyanya vɛ na amewo esime woɖo ŋku nu si gbegbe gblẽ tso anyigbãʋuʋu kple atiaƒu ƒe ameɖeɖe dziŋɔ si dzɔ le 2004 me la dzi.
Atiaƒu ƒe ameɖeɖe si do tso anyigbãʋuʋu me la medzɔ le ɣeyiɣi sia me o, gake ame siwo ku la sɔgbɔ wu 100 tso xɔwo ƒe mumu me.
2018: Anyigbãʋuʋu sesẽ siwo dzɔ ɖe Indonesia ƒe tsaɖilawo ƒe tɔdomekpo si le Lombok dzi la, wu ame siwo sɔgbɔ wu 500, dzɔna zi geɖe ɖe tɔdomekpo la ƒe anyiehe lɔƒo dzi.
Anyigbãʋuʋu la gbã xɔ geɖewo eye wὸna tsaɖila akpe akpewo tsi yame gbɔ.
Wolé Sarah Palin ƒe Vi Tsitsitɔ ɖe Anyrawɔwɔ le Ame ŋu le ƒe me ƒe Agɔdzedze ta.
Wolé Track Palin, ame si nye Alaska dziɖuɖumegã kple Sarah Palin si nye dukɔkplɔla ƒe kpeɖeŋutɔ hafi woayi ɖe akɔdada me ƒe vi tsitsitɔ ɖe asidodo ɖe ame gbɔ ƒe agɔdzedzewo ta.
Wolé Palin, ame si xɔ ƒe 29, si tso Wasilla le Alaska la, ɖe nazabubu be ewɔ anyra le ame ŋu le aƒe me, kple gbegbe be womegalé ye o la ta, le nutsotso si Alaska State Troopers ɖe ɖe go ƒe nya nu.
Le kpovitɔwo ƒe nyatakaka nu la, esi nyɔnu si wὸle aƒe me kpli la dze agbagba be yeana nutsotso kpovitɔwo tso nugbegblẽ si wobu be ewɔ ŋuti la, exɔ eƒe kaƒomɔ le esi.
KTUU ɖee gblɔ be, wozi Palin dzi ɖe Mat-Su Pretrial Facility me ke woate ŋu aɖe asi le eŋu woayi aƒe me gbɔ kple $500 si mehiã megbeda o.
Nyadzɔdzɔ ha gblɔ be, eyi ʋɔnu Memleɖagbe, afi si wὸɖe eme le kple “kakaɖedzi be yemedze agɔ o” esime wobia nya si le esi la ta se.
Wotsɔ Class A ƒe agɔdzedze etɔ ɖe Palin ŋu, si fia be woate ŋu adee mɔ va se ɖe ƒe ɖeka alo woana wὸaxe agɔgefe $250,000.
Wogabu fɔe kple Class B ƒe agɔdzedze, si ƒe tohefe nye ŋkeke ɖeka le gaxɔme kple $2,000 xexe.
Menye esiae nye zi gbãtɔ si wobu fɔ Palin ɖe nugbegblẽwɔwɔ ta o.
Le Dzome 2017 me la, wobu fɔ Palin be eƒo fofoa, Todd Palin.
Edada, Sarah Palin, yɔ sedzikpɔla (kpovitɔ) hena nutsotso ku ɖe ale si wotsoe la ŋu.
Fifi laa la nya la le Alaska Veteran’s Cour.t
Wotsɔ aƒeme funyanya wɔwɔ ame ƒe nya ɖe eŋu le Dzove 2016 me, tatra ɖe nutsotso tso anyrawɔwɔ le aƒeme ƒe agɔdzedze me, kple aʋawɔnu lelé ɖe asi nenye be emu siwo do ka kple nudzɔdzɔ la.
Eƒe ahiãvi tsɔ nya ɖe eŋu be etu kɔ mo na ye.
Dɔwɔla xoxowo ƒe ha ƒo nu tso Sarah Palin ŋu le 2016 me esi wobe via ƒe agbedzeaglã nɔnɔ do ka kple PTSD si do tso eƒe dɔwɔwɔ me le Iraq.
Indonesia ƒe anyigbãʋuʋu si dzɔ le atsiaƒu gɔme: wu ame alafa geɖewo.
Ne mede ɖeke o hã, ame 384 sɔŋ ku to anyigbãʋuʋu si dzɔ ɖe Indonesia ƒe tɔdomekpo si le Sulawesi le Fiɖagbe la me.
7.5 ƒe kpekpeme si le anyigbãʋuʋu la si la wɔe be atsiaƒu gɔme ʋuʋu eye tsi la ɖe aƒe akpeakpewo.
Dziɖegbeŋusẽ kple kaƒoƒo kawo mele dɔ wɔm nyuie o eye ame siwo ku la ƒe xexlẽme ayi dzi le ŋkeke siwo gbɔna la me.
Anyigbãʋuʋu la gblẽ nu kpata le Sulawesi titina si nye dzigbe-ɣedzeƒe na Indonesia ƒe toxɔdu, Jakarta.
Vidiowo le yaʋalãwo dzi hele nudzɔdzɔ la ɖem fiafiam.
Ame alafa alafawo ƒo ƒu hena ƒukpodzi zã ɖuɖu le Palu du me le esime tututu atsiaƒu gɔme ʋuʋu ɖe ƒukpo la.
Dukɔ blibo la ƒe ʋɔnudrɔlawo nɔ kufiatsotso dim na ame vɔɖi si wobu be eyae gblẽ nu le NYC.
Dukɔ blibo la ƒe ʋɔnudrɔlawo le New York le kufiatsotso dim na Sayfullo Saipov, ame si wobu be eyae gblẽ nu si wu ame enyi le New York City – tohehe si ƒomevi womegana ame aɖeke kpɔ o le agɔdzedze le dukɔ dzi me tso ƒe 1953 me.
Wobui be Saipov, si xɔ ƒe 30 la, zã Home Depot nuhayalawo ƒe ʋu tsɔ wɔ nugbegblẽ le gasɔ mɔ si le West Side Highway le Lower Manhattan, hele afɔzɔlawo kple gasɔdolawo klim le eŋgɔ le Kele me.
Bena woatso afia be kufiatsotso dze la, edze be ʋɔnudrɔlawo naɖee afia be Saipov wu ame enyiawo le “nyanyame” eye le eƒe “nyanyame” ke wὸto wɔ nu vevi ŋutɔ amewo, ɖe nyanya si wona wo ƒe taɖodzinu ta be woadi kufiatsotso nɛ la ƒe nyae wotsɔ ɖe eŋu le New York ƒe Dziehe Nutome.
Nu eve mawo katã ate ŋu ahe kufiatsotso vɛ le ʋɔdrɔgbalẽ ƒe nya nu.
Esi kɔsiɖawo va yi le nugbegblẽ la megbe la, dukɔ blibo la ƒe ʋɔnudrɔla gãwo bu fɔ Saipov kple tohedzesi 22 si me ame 8 wuwu hã le be woado hlɔnuwɔlae, vevitɔ esi dukɔ blibo la ƒe ʋɔnudrɔlawo zãna le nugbegblẽ si woɖo wɔ la ƒe nyawo me,kple fɔbubu ɖe hlɔdodo kpakple motowo gbegblẽ ta.
Nugbegblẽ sia wɔwɔ hiã “ɖoɖo kplikpa wɔwɔ kple tamebubu blibo,” ʋɔnudrɔlawo gblɔ be nuƒoƒo tso nɔnɔme si me Saipov wɔ nua ɖo ŋu la “dzi ŋɔ, nye tagbɔsesẽ eye wὸgbɔ eme.”
“Sayfullo Habibullaevic Saipov wɔ nu vevi, gblẽ nu, eye wὸbu ƒometɔwo kple xɔlɔwo ɖe Diego Enrique Angelini, Nicholas Cleves, Ann-Laure Decadt, Darren Drake, Ariel Erlij, Hernan Ferruchi, Hernan Diego Mendoza, kple Alejandro Damian Pagnucco,” nu siawoe tameɖoɖo kaklanagbalẽ ɖe gblɔ.
Ame siwo dze afɔku la dometɔ atɔ nye tsaɖilawo tso Argentina.
Ƒe ewo sɔŋ nye esi va yi esi me New York ƒe South District tso kufia na ame.
Wobu fɔ Khalid Barnes, ame si ŋu wotsɔ nya ɖo la, be ewu atikedzrala eve aɖe gake le nuwuwu la, wotsɔe ke mɔ le Anyɔnyɔ 2009 me.
Zi mamletɔ si wotso kufia yi edzi le New York dukɔƒoƒuwo ƒe nya me le 1953 na Julius kple Ethel Rosenberg, srɔtɔ siwo wowu le esi wobu fɔ wo be woxɔ sebla be yewoanye adzame ŋkutsala siwo anɔ nutsotso nam Soviet Union le Cold War si yi edzi le ƒe eve siwo do ŋgɔ la me.
Wowu Aƒetɔ kple Aƒenɔ Rosenberg kple zikpui si me wode dziɖegbe ŋusẽe le Masa 19lia, 1953.
Saipov, ame si nye Uzbekistan dumevi, ɖe dzimematrɔmatrɔ ƒe dzesi fia le ŋkeke kple ɣleti siwo kplɔ nugbegblẽ si dzɔ la ɖo, le ʋɔnudrɔgbalẽwo ƒe nya nu.
Kpovitɔwo be, eɖee gblɔ na nugɔmekulawo be yeƒe dzi dze eme le nu si yewɔ la ta.
Saipov gblɔ na amegãwo be nu si do ŋusẽ ye lae nye ISIS vidio si yekpɔ le yeƒe kaƒomɔ dzi le ʋɔnudɔdrɔ la nu.
Kpovitɔwo ɖee gblɔ be, ebia tso yewo si be woaɖe mɔ na ye yeatu ISIS flaga ɖe yeƒe aba gbɔ le dɔnɔkɔdzixɔ me.
Egblɔ be yemedze agɔ le fɔbubu dzesi 22 sɔŋ si wotsɔ ɖe ye ŋu la me o.
David Patton, dukɔƒoƒuwo ƒe nyataʋlilawo dometɔ ɖeka si le Saipov teƒe la, gblɔ be ʋɔnudrɔlawo ƒe nyametsotso wɔ “nuku ŋutɔ” na yewo.
Patton gblɔ be yewo bui be tiatia be woatso kufia wu be woaxɔ agɔdzedze kukuɖeɖe na yewo ahatsɔe ake mɔ si ŋuti asiɖeɖe le eŋu mele bɔbɔe o la nye eme eme ƒe funyafunya wɔwɔ ame siwo dzi nya dzɔ ɖo la ɣeyiɣi didi ŋutɔ ƒe nya.
Saipov taʋlilawo do ŋgɔ bia tso ʋɔnudrɔlawo si be womagadi kufiatsotso o.
Tory MP gblɔ be wonetsɔ NIGEL FARAGE ɖo Brexit ŋuti dzeɖoɖo nu.
Nigel Farage fi adzɔgbe be “yeaƒo dukɔ ƒe asrafowo nu ƒu” egbe le tsitretsitsi gbɔlɔlɔ si ayi dzi le Tory takpekpe me la me.
Ukip ŋgɔnɔla xoxoa ɖee gblɔ be edze be dunyahelawo nase “fuɖeɖe ŋkɔ” tso ame siwo mebui be Europa ƒe ɖekawɔwɔ adze dzi o la gbɔ - abe ale si Theresa May ŋutɔ ƒe MPwo doe ɖa be nenɔ ŋgɔ na dzeɖoɖo kpe EU ene.
Peter Bone si melɔna be tɔtrɔ nava ale si nuwo yia edzi o ŋu la gblɔ na ameha la le Bimingham be ne Aƒetɔ Farage ɖe wὸnye Brexit Sscretary la, anye ne UK ‘megale ha la me’ fifia o.
Gake kuxi si Aƒenɔ May do goe le asitɔtrɔ wɔwɔ le eƒe asrafo siwo ma ale gbegbe ŋu la ɖe dzesi kple Tories ŋume siwo susɔ ƒe ɖekawɔwɔ kple tsitretsitsi gbɔlɔlɔ ha bubu si tsi tre ɖe Brexit ŋu le du la me.
Sewɔtakpekpemenɔlawo nunɔla le agbagba dzem be yealé eƒe Chequers lɔlɔ ɖe nu dzi ɖoɖo ɖe te togbɔ be tsotso ɖe ame ŋu tso Brextitɔwo, Remainers kple EU gbɔ hã.
Eƒe akpadzitɔwo ɖoe kplikpaa be ayi dzi adze agbagba be yeabla nane kple Brussels togbɔ be nane gblẽ le megbe hã – be woazi Ame siwo mebui be Europa ƒe ɖekawɔwɔ adze dzi o la kple Dɔwɔha la dzi be woatia esi woatsɔ le eƒe nu si le esi la kple ‘zitɔtɔ’ dome.
Aƒetɔ Bone gblɔ na Leave Means Leave takpekpe le Solihuli be yedi be ‘yeaka asi Chequers’.
Edoe ɖa be woawɔ Aƒetɔ Farage woanye dɔwɔhati eye waonɛ dɔdeasi be woaɖo dze kple Bussels.
Egblɔ be ne eyae wodee asi na la, anye va se ɖe fifia ne yewo do le eme.
Wellingborough MP gblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu be: ‘Matsi tre na Brexit gake ehiã be mίaka asi Chequers’.
Egblɔ be, tsitretsitsi nana EU. ‘Mίewɔ xexeʋa vɔ be mίanye kluviwo o.
Mίedi be mίawɔ mίa ŋutɔwo ƒe se le mίa ŋutɔ mίaƒe dukɔ me.’
Aƒetɔ Bone tu afɔ nya sia be amewo ƒe susu si woɖena gblɔna la trɔ tso 2016 ke: ‘Susu sia be British tɔwo trɔ woƒe susu eye wodi be yewoanɔ anyi ko la nye aʋatso blibo.’
Tory Brexiteer Andrea Jinkyns ha nɔa azɔni si nye nyadzɔdzɔdɔwɔla akukua wotɔ dzi. nya suesi gblɔ mele enye be: Dukplɔla ƒe kpeɖeŋutɔ ɖoto ameawo.
Nudzikpɔlawo medze dukɔ blibo ŋu o, eye akpa si mele miadzi ha mada akɔ be newoava edzi o. Gakpeɖe emaŋu eyae nye mia ƒe dukplɔhabɔbɔ kple miadzivi siwo dogo xɔ mɔwo dzi eye heda akɔ na mi ha melɔ ɖe edzi o
Meɖekuku miɖe nudzikpɔlawo ɖa eye miaɖoto ameawo.
Le gbedeasi aɖe hena aƒenɔ May, ekɔekpeɖe ŋu be: Dukplɔla ƒe kpeɖeŋutɔ ƒe dɔ megea le esi o nenye be ewɔ wogbedzi.
Mr. Farage gblɔ na dunyahela siwo nɔ takpekpea me be elebe woakpɔ tohehe nenye be wodi be yewoa de yewo asi alo atrɔ le yewo yome le 2016 ƒe akɔdada ta.
Egblɔ be enya sia etrɔ zu amenɔvidzimaxɔmaxɔse si le yewo yomenɔlawo kple ŋgɔnɔlawo dome

le gbedeasi he na ameha siwo edzo le l ã me nawo, egblɔ kpeɖeŋu be: Medi be nana mia ƒe dunyahelagã siwodi be yewoatrɔ le Brexit yome woaxe fe ɖe ta.
Mile ameha adri siwo na mi dziɖuɖu le Brexit akɔdadame nuƒoƒom le dukɔa me eye miadzudzɔ o va seɖe esi mia xɔ ɖokoesinɔnɔ eye miezu dukɔ ɖeka si woyɔ be Kingdom eye wole eɖokui kplɔm.

Warren ɖoe be ‘yealé ŋku ɖe’ gege ɖe dukɔkplɔla nyenye ƒe hoʋiʋli me ŋu ‘tsitotsito’
U.S. Sen. Elizabeth Warren gblɔ be ‘yealé ŋku ɖe’ gege ɖe dukɔkplɔla nyenye ƒe hoʋiʋli me ŋu tsitotsito’ le Adamekpɔxe me ƒe akɔdada vɔ megbe.
Boston Globe na nutsonutso be Massachusetts Democrat ƒe nu tso eƒe etsɔme ŋu le takpekpe aɖe me le Massachusetts ƒe ɣetoɖoƒe le Memleɖagbe.
Warren, ame si ƒe nuƒo tsia tsitre ɖe Dukɔkplɔla Donald Trump ŋu edzi edzi la, le ho ʋlim kple GOP Nutome Teƒenɔla Geoff Diehl be woagatia ye ake, ame si kpe ɖe ame bubu aɖe ŋu wonye zimenɔla na Trump ƒe Massachusetts 2016 boblododo la.
Eƒe nya le amewo nu hoo be ɖewohĩ aʋli ho kple Trump le 2020 me.
Memleɖagbe ŋdɔ ƒe wɔna si yi dzi le Holyoke ye nye eƒe takpekpe 36lia si wὸwɔ kple nutometɔwo le takpekpe ɖoɖonu esime ke Trump xɔ zia.
Takpekpea menɔla ɖeka biae be yeanya ne ɖe wὸɖoe be yeaʋli ho na dukɔkplɔlanyenye.
Warren ɖo eŋu be ɣeyiɣi de “na nyɔnuwo be woayi Washington aɖɔ mίaƒe dziɖuɖu gbagbã la ɖo, eye elɔ nyɔnuwo ƒe tanɔƒenɔnɔ ɖe eme.”
Wolé ame ɖe tu dada si wu LSU ƒe Sims
Kpovitɔ siwo le Baton Rouge, La., la ɖe gbeƒã Memleɖagbe be asi ka ame aɖe ku ɖe tu dada si wu LSU basketbɔl ƒola Wayde Sims ŋu le Fiɖagbe.
Baton Rouge Kpovitɔwo ƒe Dɔwɔƒe ɖe gbeƒã be yewolé Dyteon Simpson, ame si xɔ ƒe 20, le 11 a.m. ET nyadzɔdzɔ takpekpe.
Woɖe vidio aɖe ɖe go tso Fiɖagbe tudada ŋu, hele kpekpeɖeŋu biam be woade dzesi ŋutsu si dze le nɔnɔme la me.
Woda tu hewu Sims, ame si xɔ ƒe 20, le afi si te ɖe Southern University kpodzi ŋu le Fiɖagbe ŋdi.
Kpovitɔwo ƒe amegã Murphy J. Paul gblɔ na nyadzɔdzɔ dɔwɔƒea be “Tukpe de abi ta na Wayde Sims si wɔe be wὸku,” le 247sports ɖe sia ɖe.
Wayde geɖe eme be yeaxɔ na exɔlɔa eye Simpson da tue.
Wobia Simpson eye wὸlɔ be yenɔ teƒe si nua dzɔ le la hele lãnu ɖe asi, eye wὸgalɔ hã be yeda tu Wayde Sims.
Wolé Simpson le nudzɔdzɔ la megbe eye wozi edzi da ɖe East Baton Rouge Parish Kpovitɔwo ƒe Dɔwɔƒe.
A 6-foot-6 junior si tsi ɖe Baton Rouge, Sims ƒo bɔl zi 32 eye wὸdze 10 gɔme le bɔlƒoɣi si va yi la me si woatsɔe ko be eƒoa miniti 17.4 ɣesiaɣi, exɔa dzesi 5.6 kple gbugbɔgaƒo 2.9 le bɔlƒoƒo ɖe sia ɖe me.
Russian Grand Prix: Lewis Hamilton te tu Sebastian Vettel le xexea me godoo ƒe dzesi xɔxɔ me le esi eƒe bɔlƒoha nɛ dziɖuɖu vɔ megbe.
Eme va kɔ le ɣeyiɣi ma me be Valtteri Bottas to do ŋgɔ na Lewis Hamilton le Memleɖagbe si Mercedes bɔlƒoha ƒe nudɔdɔ awɔ wɔƒe gã aɖe le hoʋiʋli la me.
Tso ageti la gbɔ la, Bottas dze gɔme nyiue eye wὸɖi gbɔ Hamilton kloe esime wὸʋli eƒe ɖoƒe ta le akpa gbãtɔ eveawo me eye wὸkpe Vettel be wὸate kame kple bɔlƒohametɔ.
Vettel doŋgɔ yi edoa me alo gɔme eye woɖe asi le Hamilton ŋu be woageɖe eʋu sugbɔa me le pakiɛ nu si wole be eme na kɔ.
Mercedes a yi to godoo he dogo ɖe Vettel ƒe megbe gake Hammilton yi ŋgɔ esi woɖe afɔ le afɔ nu ƒe azɔni aɖe sina be Ferrari kula gbugblɔ asi le megbe le eme henɔ zɔzɔ evea kpɔm be le etɔlia nu yea ʋli ye ɖokui ta le etɔlia dzi.
Max Verstappen nye mamlɛ si dze egɔme le megbe ɣlidodo ƒe ɖoɖonu gake eva le adrelia le esime woƒo xla zigbatɔ vɔ le eƒe ƒeblave zã ɖuɖu me.

Dukplɔla Donald Trumph ko sewɔhatakpekpegametɔ Dianne Feinstein le “rali” esi woɖo kpe edzi be yee meto fitonu hehe agbalẽ sitso Christine Blasey Ford gbɔ si de Brett Kavanauah si woɖe be woayi wɔdɔ le ʋɔnudrɔƒega enyame be edɔ nyɔnu aɖe gbɔ le madzemadze dzi.
Esi dukpɔla nɔ nuƒom le “rali” le Virginia ƒe ɣetoɖoƒe, meɖoe ƒonu tso ɖaseɖiɖi si Ford na le sewɔhatakpekpeƒe ƒe ʋɔnudrɔdrɔ nyamekuha ƒe ŋkume gake egblɔ be nusi le edzi yim le sewɔtakpekpegame la fia be amewoɖoe eye womele nyateƒe tom o.

“Egblɔ nam be maɣlee eye meɣlee abe ale si wogblɔe ene.”
Gake eƒe gbegbea mesɔ na dukplɔla si ƒonu le eŋu le memledagbe za “ralia”. Enya nusi magblɔ na woa, esia le nyateƒemee nye ŋutilã tsɔtsɔ aƒo nu ƒe gbegblẽtɔe.
Ɖewomahi nyɔnuvia me wɔe o, gake esia nye ŋutila nya gbɔgblɔ baɖa si mekpɔ kpɔ.
Esime wo yi dzi le amesi wotia ɖo ʋɔnudrɔƒe kɔkɔ ɖem le game la, amesi nyɔnu etɔ aɖe tɔakɛ kuɖe gbɔdɔdɔ gbenɔnɔ baɖa ŋua, dukplɔla doe ɖa be Democrat tɔwo le nyasiwo le ɖiɖim la zam ɖe wo ɖokuiwo gbɔ.

Hoʋiʋli kɔkɔ. Dundee Stars, abo ƒo ha do age atɔ na Belfast Giants, abo ƒo ha woxe etɔ ɖe eŋu.
Patrick Dwyer nye amesi do age eve na Giants abo ƒo ha esime wo kple Dundee abo ƒo ha do go.
Dundee Stars, abo ƒo ha wɔ tɔtrɔ tso alesi Belfast Giants abo ƒo ha ɖu wodzi le fiɖagbe le hoʋiʋli kɔkɔ me heɖu dzi kple age atɔ eye Belfast Giants abo ƒo ha xe etɔ ɖe eŋu esime wo va wogbɔ le memleɖagbe.
Patrick Dwyer kple Francis Beauvillier tsɔ Giants abo ƒo ha doɖa ŋgɔ kaba kple age eve esime aboƒoƒoaa dzegɔme medidi o.
Mike Sullivan kple Jordan Cownie aƒe nɔlawo nye Dundee abo ƒo ha sɔ kple Giants abo ƒo ha le age dodo me hafi Dwyer do age hetsɔ Giants abo ƒo ha doɖa ŋgɔ.
Francis Bouchard do age na Dundee tɔwo si wɔe be wole dasɔe dam hafi Lukas Lundvald Nielsen ƒe age eve dodo wɔe be Dundee abo ƒo ha la ɖu dzi.
Esia nye zi etɔlia wo ɖu Adam Keefe ƒe amewo dzi esime wo do tso megbe heɖu Dundee dzi kple age eve eye woxe ɖeka ɖe eŋu le Belfast le fiɖagbe za me le hoʋiʋli kɔkɔ wɔna nyawo me.
Esia nye zi enelia akpa eve sia dogo eye Giants abo ƒo ha ɖu dzi zi etɔ sɔŋ vayi.
Dwyer do age gbatɔ le gaƒoƒo etɔlia kple aɖaba ƒoƒo bla etɔ vɔ atɔ me, Beauvillier do age evelia le gaƒoƒo ene megbe esime David Rutherford nɛ kpekpeɖeŋu.
Esi wo dze egɔme gidigidi le gɔme dzedzea me la, Sullivan tsɔ aƒenɔlawo va hoʋiʋlia me le gaƒoƒo wuiatɔ kple aɖaba ƒoƒo ewo me hafi Matt Marquardt zu kpeke ɖeŋu nala na Cownie ƒe age dodo hewɔe be wole dasɔe dam le gaƒoƒo wuiatɔ kple aɖaba ƒoƒo wuiade me.
Dwyer tsɔ Giants ab ƒo ha do ɖa ŋgɔ le akpa gbatɔ me esime wo do age eve le akpa gbatɔ ƒe nuwuwu me le zame ƒe aboƒoƒo wɔna me.
Aƒenɔlawo ma woɖokuiwo ɖe hatsotso ɖe me eye mlɔeba, Bouchard do age kple abo sesea ɖe ƒoƒo si wɔe be wole dasɔe dam le gaƒoƒo bla eve vɔ adre kple aɖaba ƒoƒo bla etɔ vɔ adre me.
Cownie kple Charles Corcoran wɔ ɖeka hekpeɖe Nielsen ŋu eye wo do age gbatɔ na Dundee abo ƒo ha tsɔ dowo ɖa ŋgɔ le akpa evelia ƒe nuwuƒe eye wo wɔe be dziɖuɖu etɔlia su yewo si tso hoʋiʋlia ƒe akpa evelia ƒe afa heyi nuwuƒe.
Giants abo ƒo ha, esi wo ɖu wodzi zi ene sɔŋ le woƒe aboƒoƒo zi atɔ siwo vayi mea, woa nɔ aƒe ado go kple Milton Keynes abo ƒo ha le woƒe abo si gbɔna la ƒe ƒoƒo me le fiɖagbe
Ame si kpɔa egbɔ be yameʋuwo dzona ɖe ɖoɖo nyuitɔ dzi la ku be ne ame alɔfa siwo le yameʋua me la wote ŋu tsi agbe esime anyigba ʋuʋu.
Wole vivi dom ɖe ame si kpɔa egbɔ be yameʋu dzona ɖe ɖoɖo nyuitɔ dzi ŋu le Indonesia be enye ame ŋkuta esime wòku bena ame alɔfa siwo yameʋua tsɔ la, wole dedie esi wòdzo le anyigba la
ame 800 kple edzivɔwo ku eye gbogbo aɖewo hã bu esime anyigba ʋuʋu gãa aɖe dzɔ le ƒukpo du aɖe si woyɔna be Sulawesi la me le Fiɖagbe si ate ŋu ana atsiãƒu gɔme hã na ʋuʋu.
Megbe nudzɔdzɔ sesewo le edzi yim le fu ɖe na nutoa eye ame geɖewo tsi gbeɖuɖɔwo me le Palu dua me.
Togbɔ eƒe dɔwɔhatiwo si dzo be yewoaɖe yewoƒe agbe hã la, Anthonius Gunawan Agung,si xɔ ƒe 21 la gbe be yemadzo le yeƒe dɔwɔƒe mumum sɔɔ sɔɔ la me o le Muntiara Sis Al Jufri yameʋudzeƒea.
Enɔ afi ma kpɔ egbɔ be Batik Air Flight 6321,si le dzodzo mɔa dzi le ɣemaɣi me la, te ŋu dzo dedie.
Ke edzo le xɔ si me wokpɔa yameʋuwo ƒe dzozo nyawo dzi le la, esime wòbue be ele gbagbam.
Eku ɖe dɔyɔƒe emegbe.
Nyanuɖela na Air Navigation Indonesia, Yohanes Sirait, gblɔ be eƒe tiatia ate ŋu ana be ame alɔfawo natsi agbe Australia’s ABC News na nutsotso.
Míedzra ɖo kple helikɔta tso Balikpapan le Kalimanta be míatsɔe ayi dɔyɔƒe gã le du bubu me.
Dzɔgbevɔetɔe la míe bui ŋdi sia hafi helikɔta la ɖo Palu
“Esi míese nya sia, míaƒe dzi gbã” wòtsɔ kpe ɖe eŋu.
Ke azɔ la, dua tɔwo vɔ be ame siwo ku la ade akpewo eye dukɔa ƒe dɔwɔha si kpɔa afɔkunyawo dzi la, le gbɔgblɔm be mɔ mele duwo abe Donggala,Sigi and Boutong ene ŋu o
“Míexɔe se be xexlẽme aganɔ dzi yim esime ametiwo gale nugbagbãwo te ko eye mite ŋu ɖo ame geɖewo gbɔ hã o,” dɔwɔha ƒe nyanuɖala Sutopo Purwo Nugroho gblɔ.
Yaƒoƒo si ɖo mita ade la gblẽ nu Palu ŋu si awɔe be woaɖi ame le agbɔsɔsɔ le Kɔsiɖagbe.
Asrafowo kple asi yameʋu nukpeɖeamenuwo kple nuhiahiãwo gbɔnae.
Risa Kusuma, dzila nyɔnu si xɔ ƒe 35 la gblɔe na Sky News: “ Le aɖabaƒoƒo ɖe sia ɖe megbe la dɔnɔkɔʋu tsɔa ametiwo va nɛ.
Tsi nyui kpɔkpɔ sesẽ.
Wotu asi viwo ɖe teƒe ɖe sia ɖe.”
CNN gblɔ be, Jan Gelfand, tatɔ na International Red Cross le Indonesia: Indonesia Red Cross le du dzi be yeakpe ɖe ame siwo tsi agbe la ŋu gake mίenya nu si woakpɔ le afi ma o.
Nu sia zu afɔkunya xoxo, gake egale gbegblẽ ge ɖe edzi wu esia.
Indonesia tɔwo ƒe Dukɔkplɔla Joko Widodo va ɖo Palu le Kɔsiɖagbe eye wὸgblɔ na dukɔ ƒe asrafowo be: “Mele biabiam tso mia si be miawɔ dɔ ŋkeke kple zã bena miawu dɔ sia dɔ si ku ɖe amewo kuku dzoe ŋu la nu.
Miele klaloa?” CNNna nutsotso.
Anyigbãʋuʋu dzɔ ɖe Indonesia ƒe du Lombok dzi do ŋgɔe si me ame siwo ku la wu 550 le.
Micronesia tɔwo ƒe yameʋu kpɔ afɔku. Air Niugini gblɔ fifia be ame ɖeka bu le yameʋu fɔku si dzɔ le ta me la vɔ megbe
Yameʋu dɔwɔha si ƒe ʋu ge dze Pacific ta si le Micronesia me la gblɔ fifia be ame ɖeka le bubum, esi me wogblɔ va yi be woxɔ na ame 47 siwo le yameʋu la me kple yameʋume dɔwɔlawo kata tso yameʋu si le nyɔnyrɔm me la vɔ megbe.
Air Niugini ɖee gblɔ be va se ɖe Memleɖagbe ŋdɔ la, yewomekpɔ ŋutsu ɖeka si nye yameʋuɖolawo dometɔ o.
Yameʋu dɔwɔha la gblɔ be yewole dɔ wɔm kple yameʋume mɔzɔnyadzikpɔla siwo le nutoa me, dɔyɔƒewo kple nugɔmekulawo hena ŋutsu la kpɔkpɔ.
Yameʋu dɔwɔha la medi be yewoaƒo nu enumake tso ŋutsu la ŋu esime wobia tso wo si be woana nutsotso deto o, nu si anye eƒe ƒe alo dumevinyenye.
Tɔdziʋukula siwo le nutoa me la kpe ɖe wo ŋu hexɔ na yameʋuɖolawo bubuwo kple yameʋume dɔwɔlawo le esi me yameʋu la ge dze tɔ la me vɔ megbe, esime yameʋu la nɔ agbagba dzem be yeadze ɖe yameʋudzeƒe si le Chuuk tɔdomekpo la dzi me.
Dɔmegãwo gblɔ le Fiɖagbe be wokɔ ame adre yi dɔyɔƒe aɖe mee.
Yameʋu dɔwɔha la gblɔ be yameʋuɖola ade kpɔtɔ ɖe dɔyɔƒe la Memleɖagbe, eye wo katã li nyuie.
Nu si he yameʋu la ƒe gege vɛ kple nu siwo dzɔ le emegbe la me mekɔ o.
Yameʋu dɔwɔha la kple U.S. la Tɔdzisrafo eve gblɔ be yameʋu si ge dze ta la me zɔ sesiẽ wu ale si dze le esime wὸnɔ dzedzem.
Nuteƒekpɔla aɖewo bui be yameʋu la tso eme esime wὸle be wὸadze.
Bill Jaynes si nye Amerikavi le yameʋu la me gblɔ be yameʋu la ɖiɖi fuu akpa.
Jaynes gblɔ be, “Kema nye nu si nyo ŋutɔ.”
Jaynes gblɔ be ye kple ame bubuwo dze agbagba zɔ to tsi si se alidzi na yewo la me yi afi si woato ado kpata le nyavɔdzɔgbe le yameʋu si le nyɔnyrɔm la me.
Egblɔ be yameʋu dzikpɔlawo nɔa vɔvɔm henɔ ɣli dom eye yexɔ abi vi aɖe ɖe ta.
U.S la Tɔdzisrafo gblɔ be meli ŋudɔwɔla siwo nɔ dɔ wɔm le melidzeƒe aɖe si wo ŋutɔwo be yewoa tu ɖe tɔ me ŋu la hã kpe ɖe wo ŋu hexɔ na wo to tɔdziʋu aɖe si wodea ya eme la zazã me tsɔ ku amewo yi kpo dzie hafi yameʋu la nyrɔ abe mita 30 ene (afɔ 100) ɖe tsi la me.
Nutsotso tso Aviation Safety Network dzesii be ame 111 ku le yameʋufɔku me to PNG-dzeside ƒe yameʋdɔwɔha dzi le ƒe blaeve siwo va yi la me ke ɖeke medzɔ ɖe Air Niugini dzi o.
Numekula na ɣeyiɣi si wotɔ zã nyɔnu la agbagbe.
Ʋɔnudrɔla wu eƒe nyanu le Memliɖagbe le esime woagbugbɔ adrɔ ʋɔnu ŋutsu si dzi woɖoe be etɔ dzo Mississippi nyɔnu agbagbe le 2014.
America Numekula Paul Rowlett tso U. S. Department of Justice ɖi aɖase gaƒoƒo geɖe abe ame si nyanu tso aɖaseɖiɖi le susume nukuku wɔnawo me ene.
Ena ʋɔdrɔlawo nya ale si wòza kaƒomɔ ƒe nuléɖi tsɔ te ƒoƒu Quinton Tellis si xɔ ƒe 29 le eɖokui ta ʋlim kple dzɔgbevɔetɔ Jessica Chambers si xɔ ƒe 19 ƒe zɔzɔ le zã si me wòku la.
Rowlett gblɔ be yexɔ nutsotso tso teƒewo tso kaƒomɔ vovovowo dzi si fia be Tellis nɔ kple Chambers fiẽ ma me wòku la si mesɔ kple eƒe nuƒo gbãtɔwo o, Clarion Ledger ka eta.
Esi nutsotso ɖee fia be eƒe kaƒomɔ nɔ Chambers gbɔ le ɣeyiɣi si me wògblɔ be yenɔ kple yeƒe velia Michael Sanford la, kpovitɔwo yi ɖaƒo nu kple Sanford.
Sanford nɔ tsitre le Memliɖagbe eye wòɖi aɖase be gbemgbe la yemenɔ dua me o.
Ʋunudrɔla bia be nenye be Tellis nɔ nyateƒe tom esi wògblɔ be yenɔ Sanford ƒe ʋu me le zã ma me, Sanford gblɔ be enɔ “alakpa dam, elabena nye ʋu nɔ Nashville”
Nu bubu si megadze edzi o hãe nye be Tellis gblɔ be anɔ abe kɔsiɖa eve aɖewo ene koe nye esia yenya Chambers esime wòku.
Kaƒomɔ ƒe nuléɖi ɖee fia be kɔsiɖa ɖeka koe nye esi wonya wo nɔewo.
Rowlett gblɔ be le ɣe aɖewo ɣi le Chambers ƒe ku megbe la, Tellis tutu Chambers ƒe nu ŋɔŋlɔwo, yɔyɔwo kple nutsotsowo ɖa le eƒe kaƒomɔ dzi.

The High Breed. Nu kae nye hip hop ƒe nudzɔnɔnɔ?
Hip hop hadzila etɔwo dzi be yewoaɖe ɖeklemi tso nugbegblẽ si wokpɔna tso yewoƒe hadzilɔdze ŋu be yewoatsɔ gbedeasi nyui ato woƒe hadzidzi me.
The High Breed, tso Bristol xɔe se be hip hop te ɖe xaa tso eƒe taɖodzinu si nye dunyahehe gbedeasi gbɔ eye wòle hadomenɔnɔ ƒe nyawo gbɔ kpɔWodi be yewoatrɔ ayi eƒe dzɔtsoƒe eye woaƒlɔ ŋku ɖe hip hop ƒe nudzɔnɔnɔ me.
Wodi be yewoatrɔ ayi eƒe dzɔtsoƒe eye woana be hip hop ƒe nudzɔnɔnɔ nagakaka.
Hadzilawo abe The Fugees kple Common ene kpɔ nyɔnyɔ sẽe le UK to hadzilawo abe Akala kple Lowkey ene la dzi.
Ameyibɔvi bubua!?
NY Vidzikpɔla sama srɔtɔwo ɖe ale si wonyae ɖe “amemetiatia” nuŋɔŋlɔ ta la.
New York Vidzikpɔla le srɔtɔwo samam ɖe ale si wonyae ɖe amemetiatia ta esi woxɔ nuŋɔŋlɔ si medze na wo o la tso dada gbɔ si nɔ liʋĩliʋĩ lim be eya nye “ameyibɔvi bubu.”
Srɔtɔwo gbe be yewomenye amemetiala o, wokpɔ samasia be enye “amebaba”
Lynsey Plasco-Flaxman, dzila nyɔnu dzi vi eve, mekpɔ dzidzɔ o esime wònyae be vidzikpɔla yeyea, Giselle Maurice nye ameyibɔ, esi wòva ɖo dɔ me le ŋkeke gbãtɔ dzi le 2016 me.
“AOOOOOOOOOOOOOO AMEYIBϽVI BUBU” Mrs. Plasco-Flaxman ŋlɔe ɖo ɖe srɔa.
Ke hã la, togbɔ be wòaɖoe ɖe srɔa, eɖoe ɖe Ms. Maurice zi eve.
Esi wonyɔ le eɖokui me be yewɔ nugbegblẽ, Plasco-Flaxman “ame si me vovom le eɖokui me o la” nya Ms. Maurice, enɔ gbɔgblɔm be vidzikpɔla si le dzodzom nye ameyibɔvi wɔ dɔ gbegblẽ eye Filipinotɔ boŋ yenɔ mɔ kpɔm na le New York Post ƒe nyagbɔgblɔ nu.
Woxe gbeɖeka ƒe dɔ si Ms. Maurice wɔ la ƒe fe nɛ eye woɖoe ɖe aƒe to Uber dzi.
Fifia la, Maurice le srɔtɔwo samam be woakpata ye ɖe ale si wonya ye la ta, emɔ kpɔm be woakpata ye kple ga home $350 le gbeɖeka ƒe ɣleti ade na ye si woxɔ ye be yeneva wɔ, si nu ɖoɖo aɖeke mele o.
“Medzi be mafi wo,kpɔ, megawɔ nu nenema o.” Egblɔ na Post le Fiɖagbe, ekpe ɖe eŋu be “menya be amemetiatiae”
Srɔtɔwo xɔe de eme be amemetialawoe wonye, wonɔ gbɔgblɔ be yewoxɔ dɔ le Maurice si nye nu nyui yewowɔ, vɔvɔ li be yewomate ŋu axɔ edzi ase o esi yewowɔ nugbegblẽ ɖe eŋu.
Srɔnye ɖo nane ɖee si meɖo be yagblɔ o.
Menye amemetialae wònye o.
“Menye amemetialae ƒe amewo míenye o” Aƒetɔ Joel Plasco gblɔ na Post la.
“Ke ate ŋu agble viwòwo ɖe ame si ŋu newɔ anyra le la ƒe asi mea, nenye be ɖe meɖoe hã?
Viwò ʋukɔea?
Nu ka.”
Agblɔ be samasia nye “amebaba” Plasco gblɔ be yesrɔ dzi vi dzinu eve koe nye esi.
“Miebe yewoakplɔ ame ma ƒomevi ɖoa?
Menye nu nyuie ma miawɔ o,” gadzikpɔla gblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu.

Paddington agbalẽtala la vɔ be nuxlẽlawo mase bear ƒo nua gɔme o, lɛta yeyea ɖe fia.
Bond ƒe vi nyunuvi Karen Jankel, ame si wodzi kpuie ko esi woda asi ɖe agbalẽa dzi la, gblɔ tso lɛta ŋu. Asesẽ be natsɔ ɖokuiwò ada ɖe ame aɖe teƒe nenye be ele agbalẽa xlẽm zi gbãtɔ hafi wotae.
Enye dzidzɔ ŋutɔ be fifia míe nu nyam tso nu si míenya tso Paddington ƒe nudzedzi gã la ŋu.
Egbɔgblɔm be ye fofo, ame si wɔdɔ na BBC abe fotoɖela ene hafi nyɔnyɔa va eme be woaŋlɔ agbalẽ tso ɖeviwo ŋu abe fefenu vi bear ene ŋu la, dzi aɖe le eƒo be womada asi ɖe yeƒe dɔ dzi o. Egagblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu be ƒe 60lia ƒe azãɖuɖu na agbalẽawo tata nye “vivim vevem” esi wòku ƒe si va yi me
Paddington ame si wòɖɔ abe “ame ŋkuta kekeake le míaƒe ƒomea me” ene la. Egblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu hã be ye fofo dãna ɖe eƒe dzidzedzekpɔkpɔ dzi
“Enye ŋutsu fafa aɖe eye medo eɖokui ɖe dzi o,” wò gblɔ.
Ke elabena Paddington nye ame ŋutɔ nɛ ta la, ɖeko wò abe nadzi vi wòawɔ nu aɖe si nu nakpɔ dzidzɔ ɖo ene togbɔ be menye wò ŋutɔ wò dɔwɔnae o
Meka ɖe edzi be ekpɔ Paddington ƒe dzidzedze nenema tɔgbi.
Togbɔ eya ŋutɔ ƒe nuwɔwɔ kple eƒe nukpɔkpɔ hãe la, eƒona abɔta na Paddington ŋutɔ ɣe sia ɣi.
Vinye nɔ kuku eye megblɔ be emegbe le kaƒomɔa dzi
Esi woɖo la, wotsɔ via nyɔnuvi la kaba yi Nice’s Hospital Louis Pastuer 2, afi si ɖɔkitawo wɔ dɔ vlo tsɔ ɖe eƒe agbe.
Nad nɔ yɔyɔm edzidzi be yeagblɔ be ele gbegblẽm ɖe edzi ŋutɔ, be womemɔ kpɔm nɛ be wòawɔ nua o.
“Enumake mexɔ yɔyɔ tso Nad gbɔ nɔ gbɔgblɔ nam be yele kuku ge le miniti eve siwo gbɔna la me si hiã be mado xede nyuie na ye.
Eye mewɔe.
Megblɔ be, “Tashi, melɔ wὸ ŋutɔ, lɔlɔtɔ.
Maɖo gbɔ wὸ kpuie ŋutɔ.
Manɔ gbɔ wὸ.
Atike siwo ɖɔktawo nɛ be eƒe dzi nanɔ dɔ wɔm la ƒe ŋusẽ nu nɔ ɖiɖim va se ɖe esime atikeawo ƒe ŋusẽ vɔ le lame nɛ.
Eku do ŋgɔ ɣeyiɣi aɖewoe nye esi eye nu sia nu nu nɔ yiyim.
Ehiã nam ko be manɔ anyi alala, si menya be nu siawo katã nɔ dzɔdzɔm.
Nyemete ŋu do lãgbelãgbe alo ɣli alo fa avi o elabena ƒonyemetɔwo kple amewo ƒo xlam le nudzɔdzɔ la me.
Ele nam be male ɖokuinye.”
Le nuwuwu la, Aƒenɔ Ednan-Laperouse, anɔ veve sem le via nyɔnuvi si ɖo yameʋu kple yameʋuɖola bubuwo heku la ta – ame si le manyamanya me ɖe nu si me tom wὸle la ŋuti.
Egblɔ be, “ame aɖeke menya o.”
“Mede mo to, eye aɖatsi nɔ tsyɔtsyɔm mo nam le ɣeyiɣi la katã.
Esesẽ be magblɔ, gake le yameʋu la mee mese vevesese ɖe ame nu sia gbegbe ɖe Nad nu le.
Be ehiã lɔlɔ kple ame gɔmesese tso gbɔnye.
Menya ale si gbegbe wὸlɔe.”
Nyɔnu siwo le veve sem ɖoa nyagbalẽviwo ɖa be woaxe mɔ na ame ɖokui ƒe agbe ɖeɖe ɖa le agbasasa dzi.
Nyɔnu eve siwo bu woƒe lɔlɔtɔwo to ame ɖokui ƒe agbe ɖeɖe ɖa me la le dɔ wɔm be woaxe mɔ na ame bubuwo be woagaɖe wo ŋutɔwo ƒe agbe ɖa o
Sharon Davis kple Kelly Humphreys nɔ nyagbalẽviwo klam ɖe Welsh gbasasa la dzi kple ŋusẽdoame nyawo kpakple kaƒodzesi bena ame siwo hiã kpekpeɖeŋu la nayɔ.
Aƒenɔ Davis ƒe vi ŋutsu Tyler xɔ ƒe 13 esime wὸdze vevesese tso teteɖeanyi aɖe me si wɔe be wὸwu eɖokui esi wὸxɔ ƒe 18.
" Egblɔ be, “Nyemedi be dzila aɖeke nanɔ veve sem abe ale si wὸle name ne gbe sia gbe o.
Aƒenɔ Davis, si xɔ ƒe 45, ame si le Lydney la, gblɔ be yeƒe vi ŋutsuvi nye nuɖala adoduia si si etsɔme le eye eƒe alɔgbɔnukoko hea ame sia ame.
“Ame sia ame nyae ɖe eƒe alɔgbɔnuikoko ta.
Wogblɔna zi geɖe be eƒe alɔgbɔnuikoko klẽna ɖe viviti ɖe sia ɖe.”
Togbɔ be ele alea hã la, eɖe asi le dɔ ŋu hafi ku, ɖe esi wὸnɔ teteɖeanyi gã me ta.”
Le 2014 me la, Tyler nɔvi ŋutsu, si xɔ ƒe 11 le ɣeyiɣi ma me la, nye ame si adi nɔvia esime eya ŋutɔ wu eɖokui vɔ megbe.
Aƒenɔ Davis gblɔ be: “Eɖea fu nam ɖaa be nu sia agadzɔ le etsɔme.”
Aƒenɔ Davis wɔ agbalẽviwo, “si ana amewo nanya be ame siwo ŋuti nate ɖo la kple ame siwo naƒo nu na la li, neganye xɔlɔ aɖee hã.
Megazi kpui ɖe edzi o – ehiã be naƒo nu.”
Aƒenɔ Humphreys, si nye Aƒenɔ Davis xɔlɔ ƒe geɖewoe nye esi la, bu Mark, eƒe kpeɖeŋutɔ ƒe 15, medidi boo le edada ƒe ku megbe o.
Egblɔ be, “Megblɔ be dzi mele ye dzɔm alo yekpɔ teteɖe anyi alo naneke ɖe fu na ye o.”
“Mίede dzesi tɔtrɔ aɖe le eƒe nɔnɔme ŋu le ŋkeke ʋɛe aɖewo hafi Christmas naɖo.
Dzidzɔ aɖeke menɔ eme le Christmas Ŋkeke dzi o – esime ɖeviwo ʋu woƒe nunanawo la, menye kɔ kpɔ wogbɔ alo fia nɔnɔme aɖeke o.”
Egblɔ be eƒe ku he teteɖeanyi gã aɖe vɛ na yewo, gake ele na wo be woadze agbagba ado le eme: “Eɖe ʋe ɖe ƒome la me.
Ede mama mίa dome.
Gake ele na mί katã be mίayi edzi aʋli.”

Brett Kavanaugh ƒe etsɔme ku ati esi FBI dze numekuku gɔme.
“Mebui be nenye be nyateƒe míate ŋu akpɔ nane abe ale si wònɔ biabiam ene la – numekuku le ɖoƒe ɣeyiɣi me, ɖoƒe le kekeme - ɖewohĩ míate ŋu atsɔ ɖekawɔwɔ vi aɖe avɛ” Aƒetɔ Flakes gblɔ le Memliɖagbe, egblɔ kpe ɖe eŋu be yevɔ na habɔbɔ la nɔ “kakam” ɖe dunyaheha ƒe ɖoƒe si wòlé vevie la ta.
Nu ka ta Aƒetɔ Kavanaugh kple eƒe Republican dzidelawo madi be woana FBI naku nu me o?
Woƒe heheɖemegbe katã nye ɣeyiɣi.
Kɔsiɖa atɔ koe le ŋgɔ ko woawɔ ƒe dome ƒe ametiatiawo le Ademakpɔxe ƒe ŋkeke 6lia dzi – nenye be ale si míedie la,ke Republicanwo wɔ dɔ gbegblẽ, woagbɔdzɔ vevie le woƒe agbagba dzedzewo me be woakpɔ ame si woatsi aɖo ɖe ʋɔnudrɔƒe kɔkɔtɔ kekeake le anyigba la dzi.
George W. Bush nɔna kaƒomɔ kɔm henɔ Senetorwo yɔm, enɔ wo nu blem be woade Kavanaugh dzi, ame si wɔ dɔ le White House na Aƒetɔ Bush eye to edzi la edo go srɔa Ashley, ame si nye Aƒetɔ Bush ƒe agbalẽdzigla.
Nu kae dzɔ esi FBI ɖe eƒe nutsotso ɖe go?
Woawɔ akɔdada le Senate afi si Republicans 51 kple Democrats 49 nɔ anyi ɖo fifia.
Eme mekɔ o be Aƒetɔ Kavanaugh ate ŋu akpɔ akɔdada metsonu 50 le Senate xɔme, si ana be Mike Pence, dukplɔla ƒe kpeɖeŋutɔ, ade mama eme be wòadɛ ɖe dzi ahaɖoe ɖe ʋɔnudrɔƒe kɔkɔtɔ.
Ame si gbena nu le North Korea gbɔ la ƒe xexlẽme ɖiɖi le Kim te.
Ame xexlẽme si gbea nu le North Korea gbɔ yia South Korea gbɔ la ɖiɖi esime Kim Jong-Un va zia dzi ƒe adrewoe nye esi, South Korea sewɔtakpekpemenɔla gblɔ.
Park Byeong-Seug, kpɔ nutsotso aɖe tso South Korea ƒe ɖekawɔwɔ ƒe dɔwɔƒea, egblɔ be ame 1127 yegbe nu le woƒe dukɔa gbɔ le ƒe si va yi me – ne míetsɔ sɔ kple ame 2706 le 2011 me.
Aƒetɔ Park gblɔ be edee tutu le North Korea kple China sesẽe eye ga home si woxɔna le ame siwo gbãna dee kple amewo si la woe nye mɔxenuwo.
Pyongyang mewɔ dutoƒo gbeƒãɖeɖe aɖeke o.
Ame gbogbo siwo gbena nu le North Korea gbɔ la xɔna dumevinyenyegbalẽ le South Korea gbɔ.
Seoul gblɔ be North Koreatɔwo30000 alo wu nenemae tso dee ɖe madzemadze dzi esime Koreaʋa wu enu le 1953 me.
Geɖewo si to China, si kple North Korea ƒe dee dome nye diditɔ kekeake eye abɔbɔ nawo be woatsoe tsɔ wu esi nu dzɔm Demilitarised Zone (DMZ) tɔwo le le Korea eveawo dome.
China kpɔna nugbelawo abe dukɔmevi madzewo ene tsɔ wu aʋasilawo eye wotrɔna wo ɖona ɖe aƒe enuenu sesẽtɔe.
Kadodo si North kple South dome – siwo le ayemeʋa wɔm - kpɔ nudzedze blibo le ɣleti ʋee siwo va yi me.
Ʋee le ɣleti sia me la, dukɔ eve sia kplɔlawo do go le Pyongyang eye woƒe nuƒe ƒe Tometi la katã xaxa ɖe ale si woadzudzɔ aʋawɔnu gblẽnuwo wɔwɔ.
Esia va eme esi US dukplɔla Donald Trump kple Kim Jong-un wɔ takpekpe wɔnuku aɖe le Singapore le Anyɔnyɔ me, wolɔ ɖe ɖoɖo edzi gbadza be yewoawɔ dɔ kuɖe Korea Peninsula ŋu be wòavo tso aʋawɔnu gblẽnu sime.
Ke le Memliɖagbe la, dudɔwɔla si kpɔa gbetanyawo dzi Ri Yong-ho bu fɔ US ɖe tohehe si wòna yewo wɔe be yewomekpɔ ŋgɔyiyi tso ɣe ma ɣi ke o.
Aƒetɔ Ri gblɔ le nuƒo si wὸna la me le UN General Assembly le New York be, “Ne ame nɔewo dzi xɔse mele US o la, dzideƒo aɖeke manɔ anyi le dukɔa ƒe dedinɔnɔ dzikpɔlawo me eye le nu siawo me la, mɔ aɖeke meli si nu mίaɖe asi le aʋawɔnuwo ŋu gbã o.”
Nancy Pelosi yɔ Brett Kavanaugh “fewuɖutɔe” gblɔ be medze na dɔwɔwɔ le Supreme Court la o
House Minority Leader Nancy Pelosi yɔ ame si wotia hena dɔwɔwɔ le Supreme Court Brett Kavanaugh “fewuɖutɔe” hegblɔ bena medze na dɔwɔwɔ le Supreme Court o ɖe eƒe dɔmedzui dodo ta.
Pelosi ɖe nya sia gblɔ esi wole nume tem nɛ le Memleɖagbe le Texas Tribune Zã me le Austin, Texas.
“Pelosi gblɔ le eƒe nya si wὸgblɔ tso Kavanaugh ƒe aɖaseɖiɖi ŋu na Senate Judicial Committee le Yawoɖagbe be, ”Nyemete ŋu lé ɖokuinye o gake mebu be ne nyɔnu wɔ dɔ nenema kpɔ la, woagblɔe “fewuɖutɔ.
Kavanaugh gblɔ seselelãmetɔe hegbe nu le nyatsɔɖeameŋuwo gbɔ be yemeɖe gbɔdɔdɔ fɔ madeamedzi aɖeke kple Dr o. Christine Blasey Ford esime wo katã nye ƒewuiviwo
Le Kavanaugh ƒe nyanuɖeɖe me la, edo dziku hede ɣli do ge eye ta dzo ɖo veme nɛ ɣe aɖewo ɣi kloe le esime wὸle nu ƒom tso eƒe ƒome kple eƒe titina sukudede ƒe ƒewo ŋuti.
Ebu fɔ hã gaglã Democrat tɔ siwo le dɔwɔha la me, si wὸyɔ nyatsɔɖeameŋuwo be wonye “nu madzɔmadzɔ kple ame ŋu gbegblẽ ƒe sebla” si Liberty dukplɔhamenɔlawo ɖo esime wokpɔ dziku be Hillary Clinton meɖu dzi le 2016 dukɔkplɔlawo ƒe akɔdada la me o.
Pelosi gblɔ be yexɔe se be ɖaseɖiɖi si le Kavanaugh si la fia be mate ŋu awɔ dɔ le Supreme Court o, elabena efia bena ede ame bubuwo dzi ɖe Democrat tɔwo ŋu.
"Egblɔ be, “Mebu be ege eɖokui le nya mawo gbɔgblɔ me kple nɔnɔme si me wὸti Clinton kple etɔawo kple Democrat tɔwo yome le la.”
Pelosi meɖo mya aɖeke ŋu enumake o esime wobiae be ne ate ŋu adze agbagba be yeaɖe Kavanaugh le zi dzi ne woɖo kpe etiatia dzi, kple ne Democrat tɔwo de ha le House of Representatives la me.
"Pelosi gblɔ be, “Magblɔ esia – ne mele nyateƒe tom na Congress alo FBI o la, ke medze o menye be le Supreme Court ƒe dɔwɔwɔ ɖeɖe ŋuti o ke le ʋɔnudrɔƒe si wὸle fifi hã la ta.”
Kavanaugh nye ʋɔnudrɔla fifia le D.C. Circuit Court of Appealwo.
Pelosi gblɔ yi edzi be abe Democrat tɔ ene la Kavanaugh ƒe afiatsotso si woate ŋu ana si made Affordable Care Act alo Roe v dzi o la ka ye. Wade, abe ale si wobunɛ be enye ʋɔnudrɔla si melɔa tɔtrɔ yeye o la ene.
Le dzeɖoɖo si me woaɖo kpe edzi le la me la, Kavanaugh ƒo asa na biabia sia be ne ava trɔ Supreme Court ƒe tiatia aɖewo.
Pelosi gblɔ be ɣeyiɣi mede o be fewuɖula, ame si dea ame bubu dzi ɖe ame ŋu la nayi ʋɔnu la akpɔ mɔ be mίagblɔ be, ‘mewɔ nuku o ma hã.’”
Eye edze be Nyɔnuwo Nanɔ Enu.

"Le ƒe 45 megbe la, Aƒenɔ Steinem gblɔ be, “Mίefaa avi ne mίekpɔ dziku.”
“Nyemebu be kema mebɔ o, alekee nekpɔe?”
Eyi edzi be, “Nyɔnu aɖe si nye ame ŋkuta le teƒe aɖe la kpe ɖe ŋunye ale gbegbe, ame sia gblɔ be ye hã yefaa avi ne yekpɔ dziku, gake yefɔ atsyia aɖe si nenye be yekpɔ dziku hele avi fam la, yegblɔna na ame si yele nu ƒom kpli la be, “Abu be ɖe mekpɔ dziku elabena mele avi fam.
Mekpɔ dziku.”
Ke hã la ele dzi yim.
Eye mebui be ekema nyo ŋutɔ.”
Mɔɖeɖe li na aɖatsi fafa abe dzi vevi ɖeɖe fia ƒe akpa ɖe ene elabena womese wo gɔme kaba o.
Nu siwo dometɔ ɖeka si dzi meɖoa ŋkue le nye dɔwɔwɔ ƒe gɔmedzedze me, le dɔwɔƒe si ŋutsuwo sɔgbɔ wu nyɔnuwo le, afi si mekpɔ ɖokuinye gbeɖeka menɔ avi fam kple dɔmedzoe le, lae nye nyɔnu tsitsi aɖe lé fu siwo le kɔme nam la sesiẽ - dɔdzikpɔla ɖivɔvɔ si vɔvɔ vi aɖe le menye na ɣe sia ɣi la – si hem de atrakpui la nu.

Le ƒe 1987 me la, Aƒenɔ Schroeder tɔtɔ ale gbegbe, eye wὸɖee gblɔ be yemenya susu si ta ye ŋutɔ yemate ŋu age ɖe dɔkɔkplɔlanyenye ƒe hoʋiʋli la me o, esime Aƒetɔ Hart do go le hoʋiʋli la me ɖe esi wolé le nyɔnu bubu yome titi le gbeta dukɔ aɖe me le tɔdzimɔzɔdɔwɔƒe ʋu aɖe si woyɔna be Monkey Business me la ta.

Ale ke US-China ƒe tsotso ɖe wo nɔewo ŋu le asitsatsa me ahe nyui vɛ na Beijing
Ame siwo nya tso nudzɔdzɔ sia ŋu ɖe eme be, asrafo siwo le US kple China ƒe tsotso ɖe wo nɔewo ŋu le asitsatsa me le gɔmedzedzea me la nɔ toku dom wo,eye esime aʋa le keke ta la, dzre si le dukɔ siawo dome la, ade Beijing dzi le etsɔme.
Donald Trump, ame si nye US Dukɔkplɔla la, do kpɔnyuie gbãtɔ na wo le ƒe sia ƒe gɔme dzedze me kple adzɔga dada ɖe China tɔwo ƒe nu vevi aɖe siwo vana US abe solar panelwo, steel, kple aluminium la dzi.
Nu si ɖe fu wu la dzɔ le kɔsiɖa sia me kple adzɔga yeyewo ɖoɖo wo dzi si gblẽ nu le nu siwo ƒe home nye $200 billion (£150 billion) la ŋu, adzɔga vevi ɖoɖo nu siwo katã tsoa China vana US la ƒe afã dzi.
Beijing wɔa wɔɖenu ɣe sia ɣi, esi wὸwɔ eteƒe medidi o lae nye adzɔga ɖoɖo tso atɔ va se ɖe ewo mama ɖe alafa dzi ɖe agba siwo tso Amerika si ƒe home nye $60 billion la dzi.
China ɖe adzɔgbe be yeanɔ te ɖe US ŋu le woƒe afɔɖeɖe ɖe sia ɖe me, eye mele bɔbɔe be dukɔ sesẽ evelia le xexea me ƒe ganyawo me la nadze anyi kpuie o.
Bena Washington nagawɔ anyra ɖe edzi o la fia be woadze agbagba akpɔ mɔ le woƒe hiãhiãwo gbɔ kpɔkpɔ ŋu, gake nudodo na US le gaglãgbe la atɔtɔ Xi Jinping si nye China Dukɔkplɔla la akpa.
Egbe egbe la, ame siwo nya tso nudzɔdzɔ sia ŋu ɖe eme be ne Beijing ate ŋu awɔ eƒe dɔdeasi nyuie la, mavomavo si ado tso US ƒe tsotso ɖe eŋu le asitsatsa me la ado China ɖe ŋgɔ le etsɔme to ŋuɖoɖo ɖe wo nɔewo ŋu dzi ɖeɖe kpɔtɔ me.
Abigail Grace, nugɔmekula si lé ŋku ɖe Asia ŋu le Center for New American Security si nye aɖaŋuɖoha la gblɔ be, togbɔ be enye nyateƒe be dɔkplɔ ɖoɖo wɔwɔ kpata le Washington alo Beijing ate ŋu ahe nɔnɔme si aɖiɖi asitsanyawo kpata le dukɔ eveawo katã me la nye nu dziŋɔ ŋutɔ wu esi eteƒekpɔlawo kpɔ kpɔ.
Dutanyawo Dzikpɔla gblɔ be, Syria le klalo be ame siwo si aʋa la natrɔ gbɔ.
Syria gblɔ be yele klalo be ame siwo si aʋa la natrɔ gbɔ lɔlɔnu fãa eye wὸle koko ƒom be woakpe ɖe ye ŋu be yeagbugbɔ atu du si gbã la le ɣeyiɣi didi si wu ƒe adrẽ ƒe aʋawɔwɔ me la.
Le dzeɖoɖo kple United Nations General Assembly me la, Dutanyawo dzikpɔla Walid al-Moualem gblɔ be ŋgɔyiyi le dukɔa me vam.
Egblɔ be, egbe la, dukɔa me fa eye dedinɔnɔnyawo hã nyo wu tsã, akpe na ŋgɔyiyi si va le ŋɔdzidodo na amewo nu tsitsi la me
Dziɖuɖu la yi edzi nɔ asi trɔm teƒe siwo ŋɔdzidonamela siawo gbã la ŋu be nuwo natrɔ ɖo wo teƒe.
Nu sia nu le eteƒe azɔ be aʋasilawo natrɔ gbɔ fãa va dukɔ si me wὸle be woadzo le ɖe ŋɔdzidodo na ame kple ga ŋuti ɖoɖo siwo mede ame dzi o ta si wɔe be woƒe gbe sia gbe ƒe agbenɔnɔ sesẽ na wo la.
UN kae be Syriantɔwo milliɔn 5.5 alo wu nenema wosi le woƒe dukɔ me esime aʋa dze egɔme le 2011 me.
Ame Milliɔn ade bubu siwo gakpɔtɔ le dukɔ le dukɔ ma me la hiãna amelɔlɔnufãa tɔwo ƒe kpekpeɖeŋu.
Al-Moualem gblɔ be Syria dukplɔla axɔ kpekpeɖeŋu le dukɔ gbagbã sia tutu ɖo me.
Ke eɖo kpe edzi be maxɔ kpekpeɖeŋu si nu se anɔ la o alo tso dukɔ siwo de ʋunyaʋunya dzi.
Europe ɖu dzi le Ryder Cup me le Paris.
Europe bɔluƒoha la xɔ 2018 Ryder Cup esi wòɖu USA bɔluƒoha dzi to dzesi mamletɔ dzi si nye 16.5 heyi 10.5 me le Le Golf National le Paris godo, France.
US megaɖu dzi kpɔ o enuenu zi ade sɔɔ le Europenyigba dzi eye mexɔ Ryder Cup le Europe kpɔ o tso 1993 me ke.
Europe gaxɔ dziɖuɖua esi Danishtɔwo ƒe ŋgɔgbeda Thomas Bjorn ƒe bɔluƒoha xɔ dzesi14.5 si wohiã be woatsɔa to US ŋutie la.
US ƒe doŋku Phil Mickelson, si wɔ avu le hoʋliʋli zi geɖe la, eƒo eƒe tee-shot de tsi me le pake ƒe do 16lia me,helɔlɔm ɖe edzi, tsɔ eƒe hoʋliʋli na Francesco Molinari.
Italytɔwo ƒe gɔlfƒola Molinari dze agbgbã le eƒe wɔnawo katã va zu bɔluƒola 1-le- 4 me si te ŋu ɖo 5-0-0 esime hoʋliʋlia ƒe ɖoɖowo dze egɔme le 1979 me.
American Jordan Spieth nye bɔluƒola mamlea kekeake le European bɔluƒoha me ƒo 5&4, Thorbjorn Olesen tso Denmark.
Xexea me ƒe bɔluƒola kɔkɔtɔ kekeake,Dustin Johnson ge 2 kple 1 na Ian Poulter tso England si ɖowomahĩ le eƒe Ryder Cup mamlea ƒom la.
Ame xoxo si ƒo Ryder Cup zi enyi sɔɔ, Spaniard Sergio Garcia va zu hoʋliʋlia ƒe dziɖula ɣea wo katã ɣi European kple dzesi 25.5.
"Nyemete ŋu faa avi o gake egbe ya la alée o.
Enye ƒe sesẽ aɖe.
Akpe geɖe na Thomas be wὸtiam hexɔ dzinye se.
Mele dzidzɔ kpɔm ŋutɔ, dzi dzɔm ŋutɔ be mekpɔ nye kplu si bu la.
Garcia gblɔ seselelãmetɔe le Europetɔwo ƒe dziɖuɖu vɔ megbe be, hadɔwɔwɔ ƒe nyae., eye mele dzidzɔ kpɔm ŋutɔ be mete ŋu wɔ kpekpeɖeŋu,”
Etsɔ gɔfuƒoti la na eƒe dumetɔ John Ram ame si ɖu US gɔfuƒola xɔŋkɔ Tiger Woods dzi 2&1 le afɔti ɖeka nu le Kɔsiɖagbe.
Rahm si xɔ ƒe 23 gblɔ be, “Dada si gbegbe yɔ menye, be meɖu Tiger Woods dzi la, elabena menɔ eƒe gɔfuƒoƒo kpɔm esi menɔ tsitsim.”
Woɖu Woods dzi le eƒe gɔfuƒoƒo eneawo katã me le France eye dzesi si le esi fifia lae nye 13-21-3 le Ryder Kplu dɔwɔwɔ dzesi nu.
Dzesi si mede dzi ƒo o la tso gɔfuƒola gãwo dometɔ ɖeka le ɣeyiɣiawo katã me gbɔ, ame si kpɔ dziɖuɖu le fiakuku gã 14 xɔxɔ me si lé ɖoƒe evelia na Jack Nicklaus ɖeka ko.
USA Bɔluƒoha ʋli le kɔsiɖa nuwuwuwo katã be yewoa kpɔ bɔbɔeƒe aɖe ato Patrick Reed, Justin Thomas kple Tony Finau manɔmee hã, ame siwo ƒo gɔf ale gbegbe le hoʋiʋli blibo la katã me.
US gɔfuƒoha nunɔla Jim Furyk ƒo nu le esime woɖu eƒe gɔfuƒoha dzi vɔ megbe be, “Mekpɔ ŋudzedze le gɔfuƒolawo ŋu, wowɔ avu.
Ɣeyiɣi aɖe nɔ anyi ŋdi sia esime mίeɖe fun a Europe.
Mίeʋli.
Dɔnɔ na Thomas.
Nunɔla nyui wὸnye.
Eƒe bɔlƒola 12 katã ƒo bɔl nyuie.
Mίele gbugbɔ ge ama, mele dɔ wɔ ge kple Amerika ƒe PGA kple mίaƒe Ryder Cup Committee bena mίayi ŋgɔ.
Melɔ ame 12 katã eye wὸnye dada nam be masubɔ abe nunɔla ene.
Edze be miawɔ aha na miaƒe nunɔla
Mίeɖu dzi.”
Red Tide Nutsotso Ŋusẽ dzi ɖiɖi le Pinellas, Manatee kple Sarasota
Nutsotso yeyetɔ kekeake si tso Florida Fish kple Wildlife Commission gbɔ fia be Red Tide ŋusẽ ɖiɖi le Tampa Bay ƒe teƒewo.
Le FWC ƒe nya nu la, wona nutsotso tso dzedzeme nyakpɔ si mele alɔ ɖeka dzi o la ƒe nɔnɔmewo ŋu le Pinellas, Manatee, Sarasota, Charlotte kple Collier nutowo me ƒe teƒewo ŋu, si fia be ŋusẽ dzi le ɖiɖim.
Red Tide si nyakpɔ la keke ta abe agbadroƒe 130 ene ƒe ƒukpowo tso Pinellas ƒe anyiehe va se ɖe Lee ƒe dziehe nutowo me.
Woate ŋu akpɔ tiatiaƒewo le abe agbadroƒe 10 ene tso atiaƒu me yi ƒukpo dzi na Hillsborough Nuto la, gake le teƒe ʋɛewo aɖewo ku ɖe kɔsiɖa si va yi me la ŋu.
Wokpɔ Red Tide le Pasco Nutome hã.
Wona nutsotso tso vedomesi ŋusẽ ŋu le alo tso Pinellas atiaƒu me yi ƒukpo dzi Nutome ŋu le kɔsiɖa si va yi la me, ŋusẽ si tso anyi yi dzi la le Hillsborough atiaƒu me yi ƒukpo dzi Nutome, si dzi ŋusẽ si yi dzi la atso ɖo le Manatee Nutome, si dzi ŋusẽ si yi dzi la atso ɖo le alo Sarasota atiaƒu me yi ƒukpo dzi Nutome, si dzi ŋusẽ si le vedomesi la atso ɖo le Charlotte Nutome, si dzi ŋusẽ si yi dzi la atso ɖo le alo Lee atiaƒu me yi ƒukpo dzi Nutome, kple ŋusẽ si ɖiɖi la le Collier Nutome.
Woyi dzi le nutsotso nam tso akɔtaveame ŋu le Pinellas, Manatee, Sarasota, Lee, kple Collier nutowo me.
Womede dzesi akɔtaveame le Florida ƒe Anyieheɣetoɖoƒe lɔƒo le kɔsiɖa si va yi la katã me o.
